+++
title = "०५"
unicode_script = "devanagari"
+++
## Text

**atha pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ**

	**śrutvaitān ṛṣayo dharmān snātakasya yathoditān |**

**	idam ūcur mahātmānam analaprabhavaṃ bhṛgum || 5.1 ||**

brahmacārigṛhasthyor adhyāyatrayeṇa ye dharmā vihitās **tāñ chrutvā ṛṣayo** marīcyādayo **bhṛgum** ācāryam **idaṃ** vakṣyamāṇaṃ vastv **abruvan** pṛṣṭavantaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cātra snātakasyeti śrūyate | tatra brahmacārigrahaṇaṃ kim artham |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | vṛttasaṃkīrtanam etat | brahmacāriṇo dharmā uktā eva |

	**mahātmānam analaprabhavam** iti ca **bhṛgu**viśeṣaṇam | analād agneḥ prabhava utpattis yasya tam[^1] |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> prathame 'dhyāye "ahaṃ prajāḥ sisṛkṣuḥ" (MDh 1.34) ity atra manor apatyaṃ bhṛgur uktaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | arthavādaḥ | amutra agneḥ sakāśād bhṛgor janma śrutaṃ taddarśanenaivam uktam | tathā ca nāma nirvacanam | "bhṛṣṭād retasaḥ prathamam udadīpyata tad asāv ādityo 'bhavat yad dvitīyam āsīt tad bhṛguḥ" iti | upacārato vaitad ucyate | tejasvitāsāmānyād agner iva prasava iti | na cātrābhiniveṣṭavyaṃ kataraḥ pakṣo yukta iti | anidaṃparatvād asya śāstrasya | sarva evāyaṃ praśnaprativacanasaṃdarbho vakṣyamāṇasyānnadoṣasya gauravajñāpanārthaḥ[^2] | parigrahaduṣṭād annasvabhāvaduṣṭaṃ gurutaram iti | saṃbandhidoṣāt svarūpadoṣo balavān antaraṅgatvāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca pūrvaṃ bahutaraṃ prāyaścittaṃ śrūyate "amatyā kṣapaṇaṃ tryaham" (MDh 4.223) iti | idaṃ tu "śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ" (MDh 5.20) iti | tat katham asya gurutaratvam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | laśunādyapakṣam etat | teṣu hi "matyā jagdhvā patet" (MDh 5.19) iti patitaprāyaścittaṃ bhavati || 5.1||

	**evaṃ yathoktaṃ viprāṇāṃ svadharmam anutiṣṭhatām |**

**	kathaṃ mṛtyuḥ prabhavati vedaśāstravidāṃ prabho || 5.2 ||**

yan maharṣibhiḥ pṛṣṭaṃ tad idānīṃ darśayati | **evam** iti śāstravyāpāraparāmarśaḥ | **yathoktam** iti śāstrārthaṃ parāmṛśati | etena śāstrasaṃdarbheṇa yādṛśo dharma uktas tatpunas tam **anutiṣṭhatāṃ** dvijātīnām | **vipra**grahaṇasya darśanārthatvād vakṣyati: "etad uktaṃ dvijātīnām" (MDh 5.26) iti | **kathaṃ mṛtyuḥ prabhavati**, snātakāvasthāyāṃ brahmacaryāvasthāyāṃ vā | yataḥ paripūrṇāyurbhis tair bhavituṃ yuktaṃ puruṣāyuṣajīvibhiḥ | śatavarṣaṃ puruṣāṇām āyus tataḥ purāpamṛtyunā[^3] maraṇam eṣāṃ na yuktam | yata uktam "ācārāl labhate hy āyuḥ" (MDh 4.156), "japatāṃ juhvatām" (MDh 4.146) iti || 5.2 ||

	**na tān uvāca dharmātmā maharṣīn mānavo bhṛguḥ |**

**	śrūyatāṃ yena doṣeṇa mṛtyur viprān jighāṃsati || 5.3 ||**

**	anabhyāsena vedānām ācārasya ca varjanāt |**

**	ālasyād annadoṣāc ca mṛtyur viprān jighāṃsati || 5.4 ||**

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca "svadharmam anutiṣṭhatām" iti praśnena yuktam "yena doṣeṇa" iti uttaraś ca grantho naivopapadyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | **anabhyāsene**tyādidṛṣṭāntatvenocyate | yathā bhavadbhiḥ pratipannā vedānabhyāsādayaḥ purāyuṣo maraṇahetavaḥ, evaṃ vakṣyamāṇo 'nnadoṣaḥ | satsv api vedābhyāsādiṣu na tāvat svadharmo yaḥ pūrvatra kathitaḥ, kiṃ tv ayam annadoṣo garīyastaraḥ | pṛthak prakaraṇāc caitad abhidhīyate[^4] || 5.3–4 ||

	**laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuṃ kavakāni ca |**

**	abhakṣyāṇi dvijātīnām amedhyaprabhavāni ca || 5.5 ||**

**laśunā**dayaḥ padārthā loke prasiddhā eva | **kavaka**śabdo jātiśabdaḥ | kvacit kṛyākur iti prasiddhe 'rthe manyate | chatrākāni kavakāny eva | tathā hi kavakaśabdena pratiṣiddhaṃ chatrākaśabdena prāyaścittaṃ vakṣyati "chatrākaṃ viḍvarāhaṃ ca" iti (MDh 5.19) | na ca chatrākaṃ nāma padārthāntaraṃ prasiddham | na cākṣaravarṇasāmānyena yo yac chatrākāras taṃ taṃ chatrākam iti yuktaṃ pratipattum | tathā sati suvarcalādīnāṃ samācāravirodhī pratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti | tasmād yāny eva kavakāni tāny eva chatrākāṇi | tathā ca niruktakāraḥ: "kṣuṇṇam ahicchatrakaṃ bhavati yat kṣudyate" (Nir 5.16) iti | tena[^5] yāny etāni bhūmāv akṛṣṭāyām anupūrvajāyāṃ ca sitavarṇāni jāyante tāni ca kavakāni | vakṣyati ca "bhaumāni kavakāni" (MDh 6.14) iti | darśitaṃ ca "padā kṣuṇṇam iva" iti | pādaprahāreṇa yāni kṣudyante | yato yāni vṛkṣād gulmāj jāyante teṣāṃ tadākārāṇām pratiṣedhaḥ | kukuṇḍāni kavakāni vaidyake vyākhyātāni | etac ca vyākhyānaṃ na gavādiśabdavat | śāke[^6] kavakaśabdo loke ca prayujyate | ato 'sya samācārād vaidyakādiśāstrārthe niścayaḥ | pradarśitaś cāsau | laśunādīnāṃ tu samānavarṇagandhā api viṣṇunā pratiṣiddhāḥ (ViDh 51.3) | pārāśarikāyāṃ tu śabdenaiva niṣedhaḥ prāyaścittaviśeṣārtha uktaḥ "cāndrāyaṇam" iti (cf. YDh 1.175) | tena lavatakakarṇikārādīnāṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | **amedhyaprabhavāny** amedhyajātāni ca saṃsargajātāni |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tv āhur mūlavāstūkavat kevalāmedhyaprabhavānāṃ yuktaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | tataś ca yāny adhikapuṣṭyarthaṃ dhānyaśākādīny amedhyakṣetrajātāni saṃsṛjyante tāni na duṣyantīti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam,</span> śruteḥ[^7] sarvasyāpy abhakṣyatvād | ihāpi ca yady amedhyasaṃsargam antareṇa na kiṃcid vastūtpadyate tataḥ syād api | yatas tu kiṃcin medhyāj jāyate kiṃcit saṃsṛṣṭāt tato 'yaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ kevale 'medhyaprabhave, na saṃsṛṣṭe, avatiṣṭhate | 

	māṃsasya saty api śukraśoṇitāmedhyaprabhavatve nāyaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ, pṛthakprakaraṇārambhāt tasya || 5.5 ||

	**lohitān vṛkṣaniryāsān vraścanaprabhavāṃs tathā |**

**	śeluṃ gavyaṃ ca pīyūṣaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet || 5.6 ||**

vṛkṣakoṭarasrāveṇa hetvantareṇa vā bahir yan mūlaskandhaphalapalāśaśākhākusumavyatiriktaṃ vṛkṣalagnaṃ jāyate sa **vṛkṣaniryāsaḥ** | **lohita**grahaṇāt karpūrādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ | **vraścanāc** chedanād yeṣāṃ prabhavo janma | evaṃ vṛkṣāder valkapradeśā ye tatraiva[^8] jāyante teṣām alohitānām apratiṣedhaḥ | **śeluḥ** śleṣmātakaḥ prasiddho vaidyakādiśāstrebhyaḥ | na tu sutasya kṣīrasya santānikā, aprasiddhatvāt | yat tu "pīyūṣasāhacaryāt[^9] santānikā yuktā" iti, bhavati sāhacaryaṃ viśeṣahetur ubhayatra prayoge sati, na punaḥ sāhacaryam adṛṣṭaprayogāṇāṃ prayogajñāpakam | **gavyaṃ ca** | gavyagrahaṇān māhiṣāder apratiṣedhaḥ | anādyam[^10] agnimātrasaṃyogāt piṇḍībhūtam anāsaktaṃ ca | sadyaḥprasūtāyā goḥ kṣīraṃ pīyūṣaśabdenocyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca kṣīrasya savikārasya daśāhaṃ cābhakṣyatāṃ vakṣyati | tricaturāṇi vāhāni tādṛśaṃ kṣīraṃ bhavati |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | yadi kathaṃcit kasyāpi daśāhat pareṇa bhavati tad idam arthavat | 

	**prayatnene**tyādi padadvayaṃ ślokapūraṇārtham | abhakṣyāṇīty anuvartate || 5.6 ||

	**vṛthākṛsarasaṃyāvaṃ pāyasāpūpam eva ca |**

**	anupākṛtamāṃsāni devānnāni havīṃṣi ca || 5.7 ||**

atra **kṛsarasaṃyāvam** iti samāhāre dvandvaḥ | tilaiḥ saha siddha odanaḥ **kṛsara**śabdenocyate | **saṃyāvo** bhojyaviśeṣaḥ sarpirguḍatilādikṛtaḥ pureṣu prasiddhaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ye tu</span> yauter miśraṇārthatvād yāni miśrīkṛtyānnāni sādhyante mudgamakuṣṭhakādibhis[^11] tāni **saṃyāva**śabdenocyante iti teṣāṃ kṛsaragrahaṇam anarthakam | so 'pi hy anena prakāreṇa saṃyāva eva | **vṛthā**śabdaḥ sarvatrānuṣajyate | yad ātmārthaṃ kriyate, na devapitratithyartham | tadā kṛsarādīnām upadeśa iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam</span>[^12] | na hi gṛhasthā ekenārthena[^13] pacanti[^14] | haviṣa ivāvāpāt prabhṛti tādarthyenoddeśaḥ |[^15] kiṃ tarhi anuddiṣṭaviśeṣasya sāmānyataḥ kṛtasyānnasya pañcayajñānuṣṭhānaṃ vihitam | tatrākṛtavaiśvadevasya bhojane vihitātikramaḥ, na punaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ samasti | tathā hi dve prāyaścitte bhavataḥ | vihitātikramāt pratiṣiddhasevanāc ca | kṛsarādayas tu devatāviseṣaṃ vāstuyajñādiviṣayam anuddiśya kṛtāś ced[^16] āhnikavidhayo 'pi pratiṣidhyante | 

	yaś cāpi "nātmārthaṃ pacet" iti so 'py avaśyakartavyatvāt kṛtātikramasya[^17] bhojanaprāptyanuvādo na punaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | tathā sati dvimūlakalpanāprāyaścittaṃ syād ity uktam | na cānyārthatvenāpi kṛtasyātmārthatā pākasya niṣeddhuṃ śakyate | pacyamānārtho hi pākas tasya taddvārikā na śakyā ātmārthatā niṣeddhum, tenaiva vṛttividhānāt | na hi bhṛtyādiśiṣṭabhojanaṃ[^18] gṛhasthasya śeṣasaṃskāro na cātra saṃkalpaḥ śruto yena madarthaṃ pacyatām iti pākakāle saṃkalpamātraṃ niṣidhyate | ātmārthaṃ cottarakālam avicāryety ucyate | mithyāsaṃkalpadoṣaś ca syāt | devatārthatayā saṃkalpitasyātmārthatayā yoga iti | tasmād ayam anuvādo yat pacen nātmārtham evopayojyaṃ prāg vidher vaiśvadevikād iti | tathā ca apakvabhojane 'pi vidhim etaṃ smaranti | "yadannaḥ puruṣo rājaṃs tadannās tasya devatāḥ" (Rām 2.95.31) iti | na ca bubhukṣamāṇasyaivādhikāraḥ, gārhasthyapratipattinimittatvāt | tena yad ahar na bhuñjīta tad ahar apy akurvan pratyavaiti | 

	etad uktaṃ bhavati | svārthaṃ vā pacatu parārthaṃ[^19] vā pākṣīd iti sarvathā kṛtavaiśvadevātikramaṇavratā api na pravartante iti nityatām anuvadati | yac cāpi paṭhati | 

	laukike vaidike vāpi hutotsṛṣṭe jale kṣitau |

	vaisvadevas tu kartavyaḥ pañcasūnāpanuttaye || iti |

anenāpi nityataivocyate | na hi vaidike vaiśvadevasaṃbhavaḥ | na ca smārtavacane pramāṇam asti | 

	**pāyasāpūpam** iti | payasā siddha odanaḥ **pāyasḥ**, na dadhyādipayovikāraḥ | **apūpāḥ** puroḍāśāḥ | **devānnāni** samācārapramāṇakāni | **havīṃṣi** śrutivihitāni hotavyāni — prāg grahahomād — yato haviḥśeṣasya bhakṣyatāṃ vakṣyati | **anupākṛtasya** ayajñātasya[^20] paśor **māṃsāni** | upākaraṇaṃ paśoḥ saṃskāraviśeṣaḥ | sa paśuyāgeṣu vihitaḥ | etena ca yajñopayuktaśeṣabhakṣyatā māṃsasya lakṣyate | **vṛthā**śabdādhikāre 'py **anupākṛta**grahaṇam atithyādiśiṣṭasyāpi go'vyajamāṃsasya pratiṣedhārtham | go'vyajamāṃsam eva vānupākṛtaśabdena vivakṣitam | go'vyajasyaiva tatrālambhaś codito yataḥ śiṣṭaṃ prokṣitam ity uktam[^21] || 5.7 ||

	**anirdaśāyā goḥ kṣīram auṣṭram aikaśaphaṃ tathā |**

**	āvikaṃ saṃdhinīkṣīraṃ vivatsāyāś ca goḥ payaḥ || 5.8 ||**

yadīha "anirdaśāhaṃ goḥ kṣīram" iti pāṭhaḥ uṣṭrādīnām api dāśāhādikaḥ pratiṣedha āśaṅkyate | anirdaśāgrahaṇānuvṛttyā tatra samācāra ātyantikapratiṣedhārtha āśrayaṇīyaḥ | anirdaśāyā iti tu strīliṅgapāṭhe āśaṅkaiva nāsti | na hi taddhitāntair anirdaśāyā uṣṭram ityādibhiḥ saṃbandhopattiḥ | uttaratra ca punaḥ kṣīragrahaṇāt samācārāc ca uṣṭraikaśaphāvikānirdaśagavīkṣīrāṇi savikārāṇi pratiṣidhyante | saṃdhinīvivatsayos tu kṣīram eva | 

	**anirdaśā** ca gaur ucyate yasyāḥ prasūtāyā daśāhāny anatikrāntāni | **saṃdhinī** yā ubhayoḥ prāptadohā kathaṃcid anyatarasmin duhyate | prātaradugdhā[^22] sāyaṃ  duhyate | sā tu svalpakṣīratvād ekasminn eva kāle, sāsau **saṃdhinī** | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kaścid</span> āha yā mṛtasvavatsā parakīyaṃ vatsaṃ saṃcārya duhyate sā **saṃdhinī** | **vivatsā** tu yā saty eva vatse vinākṛtavatsā vatsaprasravaṇam anapekṣya kuṣṭhakayavaśālituṣādinā bhojanaviśeṣeṇa duhyāt | 

	**vivatsāyā** iti | tenaiva vatsagrahaṇenāvatsā dhenur ānīyatām itivad gor iti labdhe gograhaṇam ajāmahiṣyor apratiṣedhārtham | na punar anirdaśāyā ity atra | ataś ca gograhaṇaṃ tatrājādyupalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "goś ca kṣīram anirdaśāyāh sūtake | ajāmahiṣyoś ca " (GDh 17.22–23) ity āha | **payo**grahaṇaṃ saṃdhinīkṣīram iti samāsāntavartinaḥ kṣīrapadasya nātisukaraḥ saṃbandho yataḥ || 5.8 ||

	**āraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ māhiṣaṃ vinā |**

**	strīkṣīraṃ caiva varjyāni sarvaśuktāni caiva hi || 5.9 ||**

**āraṇyā** gohastimarkaṭādayaḥ | puṃsāṃ kṣīrābhāvaḥ | **sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇām** iti jātimātravivakṣāyāṃ puṃliṅganirdeśasāmarthyāt strībhiḥ saṃbandhaḥ | mṛgakṣīraṃ kukkuṭāṇḍam itivat | darśitaṃ caitat puṃbhāvavidhau mahābhāṣyakāreṇa (Pat III: 157 on Pāṇ 8.3.42) | **māhiṣaṃ vinā** payo'pekṣayā napuṃsakanirdeśaḥ | **strī** mānuṣī | yady api "strī gauḥ somakrayaṇī" ityādau sāsnādimatyarthe prayogadarśanam, tathāpi jātyantarasyāprakṛtatvāt prasiddhataratvāt tatra prayogaḥ syāt | "striyo madhuram icchanti striyo ratnam anuttamam" iti nāry eva pratīyate | **eva**kāram añjanādipratiṣedhe vyācakṣate | na kevalaṃ strīkṣīraṃ bhakṣaṇe varjyam, kiṃ tarhy anyāsv apy evaṃvidhāsu kriyāsu | eṣa tu smṛtyantarasamācārasāpekṣa eva śabdaḥ sūcako yuktaḥ, na tv asyārthasya vācakaḥ || 5.9 ||

	**dadhi bhakṣyaṃ ca śukteṣu sarvaṃ ca dadhisaṃbhavam |**

**	yāni caivābhiṣūyante puṣpamūlaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ || 5.10 ||**

aviśeṣeṇa sarvaśukteṣu pratiṣiddheṣu keṣucid ayam apavādaḥ[^23] | śuktāny ucyante yāni prāptasārasyāni[^24] kālātyayena dravyāntarasaṃsargeṇa vāmlatām apadyante | yathāmrātakādīni madhurāṇi cirakālam atirasatvāc chuktāni bhavanti | niṣpīḍito madhurarasaḥ kālato 'mlatām etītyādinā evaṃvidhāni |[^25] yāni tu svabhāvato 'mlāni dāḍimāmalakajambīrādīni tāni naiva śuktāni | yāni ca prāptakālotpattyādīni | na hy ayam āmlaparyāyaḥ śuktaśabdaḥ | tatra kevalāni pākataḥ śuktāni pratiṣidhyante | dravyāntaraiś ca puṣpamūlakādibhir yojitāny atra jñāyante | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "śuktaṃ kevalam adadhi" (GDh 17.14 ) |

	**abhiṣūyante** | abhiṣava udakena saṃsṛjya parivāsanam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady evaṃ</span> kāla eva tarhy amlatāhetuḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | etāny api dravyāṇi | tṛtīyā ca karaṇe sahayoge vā | puṣpādibhir udakena saha abhiṣūyante saṃdhīyante |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tv āhuḥ | yatra puṣpamūlāṇy amlatām janayanti | yāni dāḍimāmalakādīni śuktāni tāni bhakṣyāṇi, yāni drākṣādibhir madhurair abhiṣūyante saṃdhīyante tāni na bhakṣyante | abhiṣavo hy ucyate śuktatājananam | yāni puṣpādibhiḥ śuktīkriyante | na ca drākṣādīni śuktatāpādakāni | kiṃ tarhi kevala eva kālaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">etat</span> tu na samyak, aśabdārthatvāt | na hi somam abhiṣuṇotīti śuktaṃ karotīti pratipattiḥ | kiṃ tarhi ya eva prāg vyākhyāto 'rthaḥ | 

	**dadhisaṃbhavam** udaśvinmastukilāṭakūrcikādi || 5.10 ||

	**kravyādaḥ śakunīn sarvān tathā grāmanivāsinaḥ |**

**	anirdiṣṭāṃś caikaśaphaṃṣ ṭiṭṭibhaṃ ca vivarjayet || 5.11 ||**

**kravyāda** āmamāṃsabhakṣakāḥ kaṅkagṛdhrādayaḥ | abhakṣyavat kevalāmamāṃsabhakṣakā gṛhyante | na tūbhayaraktā[^26] mayūrādayaḥ | **grāmanivāsinaḥ** akravyādā api | **ekaśaphā** aśvāśvataragardabhādayaḥ | **anirdiṣṭās** tu na bhakṣyatvenoktās[^27] te na bhakṣyā iti | ye tūktās tatraiva bhakṣyāḥ | ye tūṣṭravaḍavaṛkṣagauragardabhāḥ[^28] prajākāmas teṣāṃ ca māṃsam aśnīyād iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śrutita eva tatra bhakṣyāvāptiḥ | pratyuta nirdiṣṭagrahaṇe sati śrutau coditānām anyatra bhakṣyāśaṅkā, anidiṣṭān varjayen na nirdiṣṭān iti vākyārthapratipatteḥ | na ca smṛtau kecid bhakṣyatvena nirdiṣṭāḥ, yena tadvyatiriktaviṣayam anirdiṣṭagrahaṇaṃ vyākhyāyeta | ataḥ śrutau ye nirdiṣṭās te na bhakṣyā iti prāpnoti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | ācārāvirodhī sa smṛtyarthaḥ | anirdiṣṭagrahaṇam anuvādaḥ | 

	**ṭiṭṭibhaḥ** śakunir eva, ṭiṭīti yo vāśate | prāyeṇa śabdānukaraṇanimittaṃ śakunīnāṃ nāmadheyapratilambhaḥ | taduktaṃ niruktakāreṇa: "kāka iti śabdānukṛtis tad idaṃ śakuniṣu bahulam" (Nir 3.18) iti || 5.11 ||

	**kalaviṅkaṃ plavaṃ haṃsaṃ cakrāhvaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |**

**	sārasaṃ rajjudālaṃ ca dātyūhaṃ śukasārike || 5.12 ||**

**kalaviṅko** grāmacaṭako nigameṣūktaḥ | grāmavāsitvāt tasya siddhe pratiṣedhe punaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ striyāś caṭakāyā abyanujñānārthaḥ | puṃśabdo hy ayaṃ vṛṣabavat | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tv āraṇyasya nivṛttyarthaṃ manyante | te hi varṣāsu vanavāsino bhavanti | bāhulayavyapadeśāc ca grāmacaṭakā ucyante | yathā mahiṣā āraṇyāḥ | 

	**plavahaṃsacakravākānāṃ** vakṣyamāṇajālapādapratiṣedhāt siddhe pratiṣedhe nityārthaṃ grahaṇam | ata āṭyādīnāṃ vikalpena bhakṣaṇaṃ gamyate | **grāmakukkuṭam** | grāmagrahaṇād āraṇyābhyanujñānam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kutaḥ</span> punar āraṇyasyābhakṣyatāśaṅkā |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">smṛtyantare hi</span> "kukkuṭo vikirāṇām" (ĀpDh 1.17.32) iti paṭhyate | ataś cāviśeṣeṇābhakṣyatā prāptā, vacanena tasya sāmānyapratiṣedhasya viśiṣṭaviṣayatā prajñāyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> vikalpaḥ kasmān na bhavaty[^29] anena śāstreṇāsyābhyanujñānāc chāstrāntareṇa cāviśeṣeṇa tasyāpi pratiṣedhāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nāyaṃ</span> vikalpasya viṣayaḥ | virodhe hi tulyabalānāṃ vikalpo na cātra virodho 'sti | na hy anayoḥ smṛtyoḥ śāstrabhedo 'pi, sāmānyasya viśeṣa upasaṃhartuṃ nyāyyatvāt, śākhāntaratas tṛtīyasyāpy ekaśāstrasya darśitatvāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady</span> evaṃ jālapādapratiṣedhasyāpi haṃsādiviśeṣa evopasaṃhāro yukto nāviśeṣeṇa kākajālapādānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratiṣedhaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">bhaved evaṃ</span> yady apauruṣeyo 'yaṃ granthaḥ syāt | bhinnakartṛke tv apauruṣeyatve na sāmānyasya[^30] kiṃcit prayojanaṃ haṃsādiviśeṣamātraparyavasāne | bhinnakartṛkatve tu[^31] pauruṣeyatve sati sāmānyadarśino viśeṣaviṣayam ajñānaṃ saṃbhavati, viśeṣadarśino 'pi sāmānyaviṣayam[^32] | ubhayoś ca mūlakalpanāyām ekasya sāmānyavedanaṃ vacanamūlaṃ kalpyate, anyasya viśeṣavacanam | tayoś ca vaidikayor bhinnaśākhādītayor asati śāstrabhede, ekavākyataiva nyāyyā | na ca vede paryanuyogo 'sti, kiṃ sāmānyena yadi viśeṣaniṣṭhatā, tasya kartur abhāvāt | śrutād dhi tatra pratipattiḥ kevalaśabdaśaktisamāśritā | na prayojanavaśenārthāntarakalpanam | 

	**rajjudālā**dayaḥ śākunikebhya upalabdhavyāḥ || 5.12 ||

**	pratudān jālapādāṃś ca koyaṣṭinakhaviṣkirān |**

**	nimajjataś ca matsyādān saunaṃ vallūram eva ca || 5.13 ||**

pratudya prahṛtya cañcvā ye bhakṣayanti | svabhāva eṣa eṣāṃ pakṣiṇām | **pratudāḥ** śatapatrādayaḥ | **jālapādā** āṭyādayaḥ | teṣāṃ vikalpa uktaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yatra vikalpa anyataratrecchātaḥ[^33] pravṛttiḥ | sā cāpratiṣiddheṣv api sthitaiva | laukikaṃ hi bhakṣaṇam, tat saty evārthitve | na śāstrīyam, yena niyamataḥ syāt | tatra vikalpitasya pratiṣedhasya na kiṃcit prayojanaṃ paśyāmaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | dattottaram etat | 

	yatrābuddhipūrvaprayogāc chabdād evārthāvagatiḥ | pauruṣeyas tv ayaṃ granthaḥ samāhitacetasā prayatnavatā śatasāhasrikaṃ saṃkṣeptum ācāryeṇa praṇītaḥ, yatrāśakyam anarthakaṃ prayoktum | ata ācāryābhidhānam unnīyate | na tu[^34] jālapādapratiṣedhe 'sati tadviśeṣaṃ[^35] haṃsaṃ svaśabdena niṣedhayati | yata etad api smaraṇam eva |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tv anyena jālapādas tv iti pramādapāṭhaḥ syāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">uktaṃ</span> caitad iṅgitena ceṣṭitena mahatā vā sūtrapraṇayanenācāryāṇām abhiprāyā lakṣyante | viśeṣaś cātrānumīyate | "jālapādādi[^36] na bhakṣayet"it vivakṣate sāmānyapratiṣedha ubhayor arthavattvāya | 

	yatra māṃsavikrayārthāḥ paśavo hanyante sā **sūnā** | āpaṇo māṃsasyety <span style="text-decoration:underline;">eke</span> | **vallūraṃ** māṃsaṃ saṃśoṣya cirasthāpitam | nakhair vikīrya bhakṣayanti te **nakhaviṣkirāḥ** | mayūrabalākādayaḥ | "āpatsu" (MDh 11.28) iti vacanāt tu teṣāṃ pākṣikī bhakṣyāpy asti | sa hi paṭhati "kukkuṭo vikirāṇām" (ĀpDh 1.17.32) iti | na cāsya mānavasya vacanasya kukkuṭopasaṃhāraḥ śakyo vaktuṃ kukkuṭanāmagrahaṇasyānarthakaprasaṅgāt || 5.13 ||

	**bakaṃ caiva balākāṃ ca kākolaṃ khañjarīṭakam |**

**	matsyādān viḍvarāhāṃś ca matsyān eva ca sarvaśaḥ || 5.14 ||**

**bakabalākākākolā**dīnāṃ[^37] **matsyāda**graṇāt siddhe pratiṣedhe tadanyeṣāṃ vikalpārthaṃ punarvacanam | **matsyādā** apakṣiṇo 'pi matsyādagrahaṇād abhakṣyā vijñeyāḥ nakrādayaḥ, kriyānimittatvān **matsyāda**śabdasya | **kākolaś** ca śyeno deśāntaraprasiddheḥ, ayaṃ bāhlīkeṣv evam ucyata iti prasiddham | **viḍvarāha**pratiṣedhāc cāraṇyābhyanujñā[^38] grāmavāsipratiṣedhaś ca[^39] pūrvasūtre prakaraṇāc chakuniviśeṣaṇārtho vijñeyaḥ | evaṃ hi ceha viḍvarāhagrahaṇam arthavad bhavati | grāmavāsī śūkaro **viḍvarāhaḥ** |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yadi tatra prakaraṇād grāmavāsinaḥ[^40] pakṣiṇo gṛhyante, ihāpi **matsyādāḥ** pakṣiṇa eva grahītuṃ nyāyyāḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span> | na cātra śakunīnāṃ prakaraṇam asti viḍvarāhamatsyānām apakṣiṇām[^41] api nirdeśārtham | 

	**sarvaśaḥ** sarvadā | utsargo 'yam | asyāpavādaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || 5.14 ||

	**yo yasya māṃsam aśnāti sa tanmāṃsāda ucyate |**

**	matsyādaḥ sarvamāṃsādas tasmān matsyān vivarjayet || 5.15 ||**

pūrvasya matsyapratiṣedhavidher arthavādo 'yam | yatsaṃbandhimāṃsaṃ yo 'śnāti sa tanmāṃsasaṃbandhinyāśanakriyayā vyapadiśyate | yathā sarpādo nakulaḥ, mārjāro mūṣakāda ityādi | yas tu **matsyādaḥ** sa **sarvamāṃsāśī** bhavati | gomāṃsāda[^42] ity api vyapadeṣṭuṃ yuktaḥ | ato nindātiśayān **matsyān vivarjayet** || 5.15 ||

	**pāṭhīnarohitāv ādyau niyuktau havyakavyayoḥ |**

**	rājīvāḥ siṃhatuṇḍāṃś ca saśalkāś**[^43]** caiva sarvaśaḥ || 5.16 ||**

**pāṭhīnarohitau** matsyajātiviśeṣau tayor havyakavyaniyogena śrāddhādau bhakṣyatābhyanujñāyate, nānvāhike bhojane | **rājīvasiṃhatuṇḍasaśalkānāṃ** **sarvaśaḥ** havyakavyābhyām anyatrāpy anivṛttir bhojane | **rājīvāḥ** padmavarṇāḥ kaiścid iṣyante | aparais tu rājayo rekhā[^44] yeṣāṃ santi | **siṃhatuṇḍāh** siṃhakṛtimukhāḥ | **saśalkāḥ** śakalinaḥ || 5.16 ||

	**na bhakṣayed ekacarān ajñātāṃś ca mṛgadvijān |**

**	bhakṣyeṣv api samuddiṣṭān sarvān pañcanakhāṃs tathā || 5.17 ||**

**ekacarāḥ** sarpolūkādaya ekākinaś caranti | **ajñātān** nāmato jātiviśeṣataś ca | **mṛgadvijān** | mṛgāḥ pakṣiṇaś ca na bhakṣyāḥ | **bhakṣyeṣv api samuddiṣṭān** | ye pratiṣiddhās te tādrūpye asati bhakṣyatāṃ prāptāḥ samuddiṣṭā iva bhavanti | na tu bhakṣyāṇāṃ samuddeśo 'sti | parihartavyatayā viśeṣato 'vijñātā bhakṣypakṣapatitā[^45] bhakṣyeṣv api samuddiṣṭā ity evam ucyante | **pañcanakhāś** ca vānaraśṛgālādayaḥ | **sarva**grahaṇaṃ pādapūraṇārtham || 5.17 ||

	**śvāvidhaṃ śalyakaṃ godhāṃ khaḍgakūrmaśaśāṃs tathā |**

**	bhakṣyān pañcanakheṣv āhur anuṣṭrāṃś caikatodataḥ || 5.18 ||**

pañcanakhānāṃ madhyāc chvāvidhādayo[^46] bhakṣyāḥ | smṛtyantare tu khaḍge vikalpaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "khaḍge tu vivadante" iti (VaDh 14.47) | **uṣṭra**varjitā **ekatodato** go'vyajamṛgā bhakṣyāḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śvāvitprabhṛtīnāṃ pañcanakhānāṃ bhakṣyatvavacanād anyeṣām abhakṣyatāsiddheḥ "sarvān pañcanakhān" (MDh 5.17) iti pratiṣedhavacanam anarthakam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naiṣa</span> doṣaḥ | sarvaśabdena pratiṣedhe spaṣṭā pratipattir bhavati | bhakṣyaviśeṣanirdeśena tadanyeṣāṃ yā abhakṣyatāpratipattiḥ sā ānumānikī pratipattiḥ | gauravaṃ hi tathā syāt || 5.18 ||

	**chatrākaṃ viḍvarāhaṃ ca laśunaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |**

**	palāṇḍuṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva matyā jagdhvā pated dvijaḥ || 5.19 ||**

**chatrākaṃ** kavakāni | **viḍvarāhaḥ** grāmaśūkaraḥ svatantraviharaḥ | etāni bhakṣayitvā patito bhavet | patitaprāyaścittaṃ kuryāt | vakṣyati ca "garhitānnādyayor jagdhiḥ surāpānasamāni ṣaṭ" (MDh 11.55) || 5.19 ||

	**amatyaitāni ṣaḍ jagdhvā kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret |**

**	yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ vāpi śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ || 5.20 ||**

**amatyā** abuddhipūrvaṃ **ṣaṭ jagdhvā** ṣaṇṇām anyatamam api | bhakṣaṇasya avidheyatvanimittatayā sāhityasyāvivakṣā | **śeṣeṣu** abhakṣyeṣu bhakṣaṇe lohitavṛkṣaniryāsādiṣu ekam ahorātraṃ na bhuñjīta | **ahaḥ**śabdo rātrāv api dṛṣṭaprayogaḥ | "ahaś ca kṛṣṇam ahar arjunaṃ ca" (RV 6.9.1) iti | yeṣu cātra prakaraṇe pratiṣiddheṣu prāyaścittādhikāre pratipadaṃ prāyaścittam anyad vakṣyate "kravyādasūkara" (MDh 11.155) ityādi tatra tad eva draṣṭavyaṃ pratipadavihitatvāt, asya copavāsasyānyatra caritārthatvāt || 5.20 ||

	**saṃvatsarasyaikam api caret kṛcchraṃ dvijottamaḥ |**

**	ajñātabhuktaśuddhyarthaṃ jñātasya tu viśeṣataḥ || 5.21 ||**

bhojyaśūdragṛhabhojino brāhmaṇasyedam ucyate | yasya śūdrasya gṛhe yāni brāhmaṇānām abhojyāny annāni saṃbhavanti, na dūrataḥ parihriyante, tādṛśasya gṛhe yo brāhmaṇo 'nnaṃ bhuṅkte tasya pratiṣiddhānnabhojanāśaṅkāyāṃ prājāpatyakṛcchracaraṇam upadiśyate | aviśeṣanodanāyāṃ prājāpatyaṃ kṛcchraṃ pratīyata iti vakṣyāmaḥ | 

	**ajñātabhuktaśuddhyartham** ajñātadoṣaśaṅkāyām āha | doṣo yadi bhuṅkte tasya śuddhyartham |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca īdṛśasya śuddhiṃ vakṣyati: "adṛṣṭam adbhir nirṇiktam" iti (MDh 5.125) | tasya viṣayaṃ tatraiva darśayiṣyāmaḥ | 

	**jñātasya tu** doṣasya **viśeṣataḥ** vaiśeṣikaṃ prāyaścittaṃ kartavyam, yasya yad vihitaṃ pratipadam || 5.21 ||

	**yajñārthaṃ brāhmaṇair vadhyāḥ praśastā mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ |**

**	bhṛtyānāṃ caiva vṛttyartham agastyo hy ācarat purā || 5.22 ||**

bhakṣyaprasaṅgena hiṃsābhyanujñāyate | atyarthaṃ kṣutpīṣāyāṃ bhṛtyāder bhojanāntarāsaṃbhave bhakṣya**mṛgapakṣi**vadhaḥ kartavyaḥ | **bhṛtyāḥ** prāg vyākhyātāḥ | **agastyas** tathākṛtavān ity agastyagrahaṇaṃ praśaṃsārtham | **yajñārtham** ityādyo 'rdhaśloko 'rthavāda eva | tatra hi vadhaḥ pratyakṣaśrutivihitatvād eva siddhaḥ | **praśastā** ye bhakṣyatayānujñātāḥ | eṣa evārtha uttaraśloke vistarataḥ karmārthavādatayā kathyate || 5.22 ||

	**babhūvur hi puroḍāśā bhakṣyāṇāṃ mṛgapakṣiṇām **

**	purāṇeṣv ṛṣiyajñeṣu brahmakṣatrasaveṣu ca || 5.23 ||**

ṣaṭviṃśatsaṃvatsaraṃ nāma satram | tatra mṛgapakṣivadha āmnātaḥ | so 'nenānūdyate | idaṃ tatra brāhmaṇam: "saṃsthite 'hani gṛhapatir mṛgayāṃ yāti sa tatra yān yān mṛgān hanti teṣāṃ tarasāḥ puroṣāśā bhavanti" (ĀpŚ 23.11.12–13) | arthavādatvād **babhūvur** iti bhūtapratyaye na vivakṣā | tenādyatve 'pi bhavanti | evaṃ **purāṇeṣv** api | na kevalaṃ kaścid adyatve satrāṇāṃ vyavahāra iti darśanābhiprāyam etat **purāṇeṣv** iti | na punar adyatve yadi kecit sarvāṇy eva hareyuḥ.[^47] teṣām eṣa vidhir na bhavatīti mantavyam | atha vā yaḥ svayaṃ śāstrārthaṃ veditum asamarthaḥ kevalaṃ paraprasiddhyā "mahājano yena gataḥ sa panthāḥ" (MBh 3. App. 32.68) iti nyāyena pravartate, tatra tv etad ucyate: **purāṇeṣv** iti | nāyam idaṃprathamako dharmaḥ | kiṃ tarhi, anādiḥ | purāṇā[^48] ṛṣayo brāhmaṇāḥ kecana tapaḥsiddhāḥ, jātyantaraṃ vā | yathā mahābhāratādau varṇitam | na cātra nirbandhaḥ kartavyaḥ: "ṛṣīṇāṃ jātyantaratve gandharvādivat kathaṃ yāgeṣv adhikāraḥ" iti | yato 'yam arthavādo yena kenacid ālambanena pratīyate | **brahmakṣatrasavāḥ** brahmakṣatriyayajñāḥ || 5.23 ||

	**yat kiṃcit snehasaṃyuktaṃ bhakṣyaṃ bhojyam agarhitam |**

**	tat paryuṣitam apy ādyaṃ haviḥśeṣaṃ ca yad bhavet || 5.24 ||**

**bhakṣyaṃ yat kiṃcit snehasaṃyuktam** | **bhojyam** odanādi | bhuktibhujyor ekārthatve 'pi pṛthagupādānād viṣayabhedo 'yaṃ pratīyate | **agarhitaṃ** śuktatām anāpannam | **tat paryuṣitam apy ādyam** | rātryantare paryuṣitam ucyate | pūrvedyuḥ siddham apy aparedyuḥ paryuṣitaṃ bhavati | **snehasaṃyuktam** iti | evaṃ saṃdihyate | kiṃ yat snehasaṃyuktaṃ sat paryuṣitaṃ rasamiśraśākādi tat paryuṣitam aśitavyam, uta śuṣkasyāpi[^49] paryuṣitasya bhakṣaṇakāle[^50] snehasaṃyogaḥ kartavyaḥ | bhakṣāpūpādy api paryuṣitaṃ bhojanakāle snehena saṃyojya bhakṣayitavyam iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra saṃdihyate</span>:[^51] snehayuktānāṃ bhakṣyatocyate **tat paryuṣitam ādyam** iti | uddiśyamānaṃ snehasaṃyuktam[^52] nipatanaṃ na punar vidheyārthe | na hi tacchabdasaṃbandho 'sya śruto yat paryuṣitaṃ tat[^53] snehasaṃyuktam ādyam iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | haviḥśeṣāṇāṃ paryuṣitānām asnehasaṃyuktānāṃ teṣāṃ vacanam anartham | na ca teṣāṃ snehasaṃyuktānāṃ parivāsaḥ saṃbhavati | evaṃ ca teṣāṃ vacanam arthavad bhavati yadi bhojanakāle teṣāṃ snehasaṃyogo nāpekṣyate | atas teṣāṃ tāvad bhojanakāla eva snehasaṃyoganirapekṣatayā vacanasyārthavattvam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady evaṃ</span> tathāpi na saṃdehaḥ | arthavattvād viśeṣapadasya vidheyarthatā snehasaṃyuktaśabdasya[^54] nyāyyā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | etāvad atra saṃdehe bījam | yathāśrutasaṃbandhasya balīyastvāt kiṃ haviḥśeṣapadam anuvādo 'stu utānarthanakatvaṃ mā prāpad iti yat paryuṣitaṃ tena snehasaṃbandhaḥ kriyatām | tatrānarthakyād vyavahitakalpanā jyāyasī | samācārān nirṇayaḥ | 

	sarpistailavasāmajjāḥ **snehāḥ** || 5.24 ||

	**cirasthitam api tv ādyam asnehāktaṃ dvijātibhiḥ |**

**	yavagodhūmajaṃ sarvaṃ payasaś caiva vikriyā || 5.25 ||**

**cirasthitaṃ** dvirātrādyantaritam | **api**śabdād **āktam** ity atrāpi saṃbandhayitavyam | **snehāktam api** yavagodhūmajaṃ saktvapūpādi | **payaso vikriyā** vikārā dahimathitādayaḥ || 5.25 ||

	**etad uktaṃ dvijātīnāṃ bhakṣyābhakṣyam aśeṣataḥ |**

**	māṃsasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjane || 5.26 ||**

ādyena ślokārdhena pūrvaprakaraṇam avacchinatti | tad etad anantaram anukrāntaṃ prakaraṇam etat[^55] dvijātīnāṃ na śūdrāṇām iti, uttaraṃ tu yad vakṣyate tac chūdrāṇām apīti prakaraṇavyavacchedaprayojanam | 

	ataś ca māṃsabhakṣaṇe prakāro vakṣyate | yac ca tadvarjanena phalaṃ tac chūdrasyāpi bhavatīti | anyathā "abhakṣyāṇi dvijātīnām" (MDh 5.5) ity adhikārāl laśunādiṣv iva[^56] śūdrasya māṃsabhakṣaṇe 'pi kāmacāraḥ syāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady</span> evaṃ devādyarcane śiṣṭasya māṃsasya bhakṣyatā vakṣyate: "devān pitṝṃś cārcayitvā khādan māṃsaṃ na duṣyati" (MDh 5.32) iti | devādyarcanaṃ medhyena māṃsena | ye ca dvijātīnāṃ pratiṣiddhā mṛgaśakuntās te 'medhyāḥ | ataś ca teṣāṃ māṃsena devārcanāsaṃbhavād ataccheṣasyābhakṣyatvād[^57] anye 'pi prakaraṇabhedāḥ, yathā brāhmaṇādīnāṃ mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ pratiṣiddhāḥ, te śūdrasyāpi prakārāntareṇa pratiṣiddhā bhavanti | tatra prakaraṇabhedena na kiṃcid[^58] ucyate | laśunādipratiṣedhaḥ śūdrasya na bhavati |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">asti tāvat</span> prakaraṇabhedena prayojanaṃ laśunādipratiṣedhe śūdrasyādhikāro mā bhūd iti | māṃse 'pi devādyarcane gṛhasthasyādhikārād agṛhasthasya śūdrasya yathākāmyam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca pākayajñe śūdrasyādhikārataḥ sthita eva[^59] | bhojanaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ca vihitam | na ca laśunādibhiḥ pākayajñāḥ kriyante | tataś ca nāpi śūdrasya yathākāmyaṃ laśunādayo bhakṣyāḥ syuḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ko doṣaḥ</span> | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">dvijātigrahaṇam</span> anarthakam | 

	parihṛtam etad agṛhasthasya proṣitasya vā kāmacāraḥ | na ca gṛhasthena yad ahutaṃ tan na bhoktavyam | "śeṣabhug bhavet" (MDh 3.107) ity asyāyam arthaḥ: akṛtavaiśvadevakriyeṇa na bhoktavyam | tatra yasyaiva yāgasādhanatā dravyasya tad eva medhyaṃ hotavyam | anye tu bhojanakāle kutaścid āhṛtya madhyagehe vā bhujyate | tac cāhutaśeṣam[^60] api na pratiṣiddham | māṃse tu punarvacanān niyamaḥ: na kadācid devānupayuktaṃ bhojyam iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yadi</span> cāturvarṇyasyātrādhikāras tadā yad vakṣyati parastāt[^61] śuddhavidhau "caturṇām api varṇānām" (MDh 5.57) iti tad anarthakam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tatraiva</span> tasya prayojanaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha</span> śvamāṃsādy apy śūdrasya bhakṣyaṃ prāpnoti dvijātigrahaṇāt pūrvatra | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kiṃ tv</span> ekādaśe "viḍvarāhakharoṣṭrāṇām" ityādiślokatrayanirdiṣṭāḥ (MDh 11.153–55) śūdrasyāpi na bhakṣyā iti jñāpakaṃ darśayiṣyāmaḥ || 5.26 ||

	**prokṣitaṃ bhakṣayen māṃsaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca kāmyayā |**

**	yathāvidhi niyuktas tu prāṇānām eva cātyaye || 5.27 ||**

agnīṣomīye paśau hutaśiṣṭaṃ māṃsaṃ lakṣaṇayā **prokṣitam** ucyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> **prokṣita**śabdo yaugika ukṣasecana ity asya dhātoḥ prakṣālanakriyānimittakaḥ | tathā ca "prokṣaṇīr āsādaya," "ghṛtaṃ prokṣaṇīyam" iti, "prokṣaṇībhir udvejitāḥ stha" iti sarvatra kriyāyogāt prayujyate | yady āsecanasādhanam, tatra kuto vaidikasaṃskāranimittakānāṃ svasaṃbandhe paśulakṣaṇādvāreṇa māṃse pravartate | mukhyaṃ ca śabdārtham atikramya kim iti lakṣaṇāśrīyate | ataḥ prakṣālitam udakādinā[^62] yuktam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, yady atra vākyāntarāṇy arthavādāś ca śeṣabhūtā[^63] na syuḥ: "anupākṛtamāṃsāni" (YDh 1.170), "asaṃskṛtān paśūn mantraiḥ" (MDh 5.36) iti | atas tatparyālocanayāyam evārtho 'vatiṣṭhate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady evaṃ</span> tata eva siddhatvāt kim anena | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> āhuḥ anuvado 'yam | māṃsecchayā bhakṣaṇasya vidhis tāvad ayaṃ na bhavati kṣutpratighātārthino lipsayā pravṛttyupapatteḥ | sa hi vidhir ucyate yaḥ puruṣasya dṛṣṭena prayojanena pravṛttāv asatyāṃ pravṛttyavabodhakaḥ: "yāvijjīvam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt" iti | śāstram evātra pramāṇam | yatra "asmin kṛte idam abhimatam abhinirvartate[^64], akṛte vāyam anartha āpatati" evam anvayavyatirekābhyām avagamyate tatra śāstram eva mṛgyate | yatra tu nāyam anyato 'vagamaḥ[^65] kevalāgamaikagocaraḥ[^66] sa vidhir iti cocyate | iha tu bhojane kṛte puṣṭir upajāyate, yad duḥkhaṃ tan nivartata iti, bālā api stanapāyino 'nupadiṣṭam avayanti | niyamo 'pi bhavati, tadrūpānavadhāraṇāt | yadi tāvat prokṣitaṃ ca bhakṣayed eveti niyamas tadā kālaviśeṣāvacchedābhāvād āhāravihārakālā apy avasīdeyur anavaratam aśnann evāsīta, aśakyaś cārtha upadiṣṭaḥ syāt | yathoktam "aśrāddhabhojī" iti, "yad ahar eva pratyaveyāt" iti | mahābhāṣyakāreṇa vidhiviśeṣa eva ca niyama uktaḥ | asaṃbhavati ca vidhau kuto niyamaḥ | na cānyena prokṣitam anyena labhyeta | tasmād ayam anarthaḥ | atha prokṣitam eveti aprokṣitaṃ neti parisaṃkhyā | na hi prokṣitāprokṣitobhayabhakṣaṇasya tyāgād aśanāyā nivṛttau yugapat paryāyeṇa vā pravṛttyā parisaṃkhyālakṣaṇasya vidyamānatvāt | tathāpy "anupākṛtamāṃsāni" (YDh 1.170) ity eva siddham |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tv</span> asya pakṣasyaivaṃ doṣam upapādayante | aviśeṣeṇa[^67] sarvāprokṣītapratiṣedhe[^68] śakunīnām api pratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti | na ca yeṣām eva prokṣaṇaṃ vihitaṃ teṣāṃ tu pratividhānādyabhāvād iti na viśeṣaparigrahe pramāṇam asti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktaṃ</span> manyante | evaṃ sati bhedena śakunīnāṃ pratiṣedhānukrameṇa, gamakatvāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tasmāc</span> chrutakarmāṅgatvena[^69] niyamasya prokṣitamāṃsabhakṣaṇasyāyam anuvāda iti yuktaṃ dṛṣṭāntatayā | yathā yajñe 'vaśyaṃ bhakṣaṇam, abhakṣaṇāc chāstrātikramaḥ, evam uttareṣv api nimitteṣu | anuvādaś cet parisaṃkhyāpekṣāpy astu | go'vyajamāṃsam aprokṣitaṃ na[^70] bhakṣayed ity ananaitad anupākṛtānām evāsadrūpam anūdyate, aprokṣitasyāpi brāhmaṇakāmyādinimitteṣv anujñāpanārthaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anyac</span> ca "anarcitaṃ vṛthāmāṃsam api" (MDh 4.213) cāturthikena vṛthāmāṃsaśabdena etad anuparijñānārtham itarathā na[^71] vijñāyeta kiṃ tad vṛthāmāṃsam iti | atha vā ekatra bhoktur upadeśo 'nyatra kalpayitvā yena devādyarcanaṃ na[^72] kṛtaṃ tadīyaṃ māṃsam anyenāpy atithyādinā na bhoktavyam | anadhikṛtenāpi devādyarcanena hy atithyādayaḥ paragṛhe tadīyena māṃsena devārcane 'dhikriyate | atha kalpayitvā yadi kṛtaṃ tadārhaty aśitum | dvitīyas tu praṣedho "devān pitṝn" (MDh 5.32) iti svagṛhe 'dhikṛtānām akṛtavatāṃ bhakṣaṇāya | yas tarhi[^73] "asaṃskṛtān paśūn mantraiḥ" (MDh 5.36) iti sa[^74] uktaḥ prokṣaṇaśabdārthaḥ | evaṃ pañcāpi niṣedhavākyāni pṛthagarthāni darśitāni |

	**brāhmaṇānāṃ ca kāmyayā** | kāmyā[^75] kāmanā icchā | kāmyāśabdaḥ chāndasaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yadā</span> brāhmaṇādīnām aprokṣitānām idam anujñānam, tadā kiṃ punar ayaṃ niyamaḥ | abhakṣaṇe śāstrātikramaḥ | uta pratiprasavamātram | pratiprasave bhoktavyaṃ vivāhe punar bhoktavyam iti vacanād api pratiṣedhāpravṛttir[^76] vivāhe gamyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">na bhojanārtham</span> āvaśyakaṃ kiṃ tu brāhmaṇā yadi garīyāṃsas tadā tadvacanātikramo na yuktaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> "krītvādi"śloke (MDh 5.32) brāhmaṇānām ity anuvartya śaśādimāṃsasyāpi vidhim icchanti | yajñavivāhayor anyatra ca goṣṭhībhojanādau yadi brāhmaṇā arthayante tadā teṣāṃ māṃsaṃ svarūpeṇa devauddeśikayā na pratiṣiddham, avasthāviśeṣeṇa prokṣaṇam devārcanādīni kartavyāni | viśeṣaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ | tasya brāhmaṇakāmanānimittata abhyanujñātā[^77], na tu[^78] "kravyādān śakunān" ityādeḥ pratiṣedhasya[^79] "nivṛttis tu mahāphalā" (MDh 5.11) iti kṛtasaṃkalpas tasyāpy anujñānam iṣyate, prokṣite 'prokṣite ca kṛtārcane 'kṛtārcane vā |

	**yathāvidhiniyukta tu prāṇānām eva cātyaye** | madhuparke ca śrāddhe ca niyukto 'prokṣaṇenāpi bhakṣayet | eṣa hi yathāśāstraṃ niyogas tatra śrāddhe niyamā uktā eva | "ketitas tu yathānyāyam", "kathaṃcid apy atikrāman" (MDh 3.180) iti | śrāddhaṃ bhokṣya ity abhyupatyedam ahaṃ nāśnāmīti na labhyate vaktum, abhakṣyam aśucikaraṃ vyādhijananaṃ ca varjayitvā, haviṣyavidhānān na bhakṣyaṃ yad yad rocate tat tan nāprītikaraṃ dīyate | ata idaṃ vacanaṃ madhuparka eva |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> madhuparke nāsti niyogaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">aśitavyaṃ</span> madhuparkārheṇeti[^80] niyamaḥ, nāsau madhuparkasya vidhiḥ | sa hi tatrādhikṛto na dhanyo rājādiḥ | yathaiva "nāsyānaśnan gṛhe vaset" (MDh 3.95) iti gṛhasthasya niyamo dṛśyate | etenāvagamyate amatike na dātavyam iti | yais tu kāmacāra evaṃ pūjitasamādānena pūjyasyāśanena, na hi tat tadarthaṃ karma |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cātithyam evānityam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | dṛṣṭaṃ prītyutpādanena[^81] dharmārtham anuṣṭhānam | tasya niyamoktadharmārtham eva dātus tasya hi gor utsargapakṣe vihito "nāmāṃso madhuparkaḥ syāt" iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanv</span> ārtvijye[^82] vacanasyāpi viṣaya iti cet | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">astv</span> ayam api pūrvavad anuvādaḥ śrāddhe ārtvijye ca |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cārtvijye uktam eva iḍādibhakṣaṇaṃ yajamānasya tatra śāstranibandhano niyamaḥ, nartvijām |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | kiṃ tu ṛtvijo yadi na bhakṣayanti te pravādyante | aviditena adṛṣṭenāpi doṣeṇa yujyante |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> teṣāṃ bhakṣaṇam adhikṛtānām āstām[^83] | na hi te karmaphalena yujyante | bhṛtyādir hi parikrīto vihitān[^84] padārthān anutiṣṭhati | vihitaś ca "yajamānapañcamā iḍāṃ[^85] bhakṣayanti" iti | teṣāṃ bhakaṣaṇato 'syābhyupagatārtvijyānāṃ niyataṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ tadā tenānūdyata iti yuktam | na hi śrāddhabhujām ṛtvijāṃ ca bhakṣaṇe śāstrīyayogaḥ | yajamānasyaivānuvādaḥ kimartha iti cen, nānuvādaḥ prayojanam apekṣate | kiṃ tarhi prāptam asti cātrocyate | atrāpi yadā gopena govadhapūjābhyupagatā tadāvaśyam aśitavyam | tadanugrahārtham asau madhuparkapūjāṃ pratīkṣati[^86] | ataḥ pūrvā tena kriyā saṃpādanīyā | anyathā prākramikasyābhāvād aparpūrṇena[^87] madhupareṇa tadanugrahāsampattes tasmin pratiṣiddhamāṃsāśane madhuparkapūjārtvijyaṃ ca prathamam evābhyupagantavyam | brāhmaṇabhojane ca | brahmacāriṇas tu vratavad ity anujñānād anaśanam eva[^88] grāhyaṃ māṃsasya |

	**prāṇānām eva cātyaye** | prakṛtatvād devādyarcanam antareṇa abhakṣyamāṇe vyādhinā kṣudhā bhojanāntarāsaṃbhave jīvanāśaśaṅkāyāṃ go'jāvi bhakṣayitavyam | "sarvata evātmānaṃ gopāyet" (GDh 9.34) ity etacchrutimūlo 'yaṃ niyamaḥ | ataś cedṛśe nimitte māṃsam anaśnann[^89] ātmahā saṃpadyate | ātmavadhaś ca "sarvata evātmānaṃ gopāyet" (GDh 9.34). "tasmād u ha na purāyuṣaḥ svaḥkāmī preyād alokyaṃ hy etad bhavati" (ŚB 10.2.6.7) ityādiśrutibhir mantrārthavādaiś ca tair doṣavān neti jñāpitaḥ | tathāhi mantraḥ:

	asuryā nāma te lokā andhena tamasāvṛtāḥ |

	tāṃs te pretyābhigacchanti ye ke cātmahano janāḥ || iti | (ĪśU 3)

	brahmacāriṇo 'pi prāṇātyaye bhakṣaṇam iṣyate | tasyaiva bālyādyavasthānimittaṃ vācanikaṃ prāyaścittaṃ bhaviṣyatīti: "brahmacārī tu yo 'śnīyān madhu māṃsaṃ kadācana" (MDh 11.157) iti | kṣudhā tu prāṇātyayāśaṅkāyāṃ pratiṣiddhamāṃsāśanam apīti vyāsaḥ (VeSū 3.4.28) | jāghanīnidarśanenaikāhikaṃ ceṣyate | etāvatā[^90] atītavyādhau tu na śakyam etat jñātum avaśyam aśitenānena jīvatīti | tatra na pratiṣiddhagrāmyakukkuṭādimāṃsabhakṣaṇam iṣyate | prokṣaṇadevābhyarcanarahitasya[^91] tu prakṛtatvād asty anujñānam | vyādheś ca na kevalam utpannasya nivṛttyarthaṃ yāvat kṛśakṣayyāturadurbālādīnāṃ sarvakālaṃ māṃsāśanaṃ niyamata iṣyate | 

	strīmadyanityāḥ kṣayiṇaḥ śramavyādhyā ca karśitāḥ | 

	nityamāṃsarasāhārā āturāś cāpi durbalāḥ ||

aprokṣitasyāpi chāgamāṃsasya devatādyarcanaṃ tu tair avaśyaṃ kartavyam | asaṃbhave tu kasmiṃścid ahani na doṣaḥ || 5.27 ||

	**prāṇasyānnam idaṃ sarvaṃ prajāpatir akalpayat |**

**	sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ caiva sarvaṃ prāṇasya bhojanam || 5.28 ||**

**prāṇaḥ** kauṣṭhyo vāyuḥ jīvabījabhūtaḥ | pañcavṛttasyodānādikasya śarīrasthityartham idaṃ **sarvaṃ** jagat **prajāpatir** annatvenākalpayat[^92] | **idam** iti sāmānyato nirdiśya viśeṣaṇaṃ nirdiśati **sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamam** iti | ato hetoḥ **sarvaṃ prāṇasya bhojanam** | tiryakprakṣimanuṣyasarīsṛpāvasthahetumadbhedanirdeśāt dvitīyaṃ **sarva**grahaṇam apunaruktam | yataḥ prajāpatinā sarvam āpadi prāṇasya kalpitam | ataḥ sarvam etasya bhojanam | tathā ca prāṇasaṃvadopaniṣadi śrūyate "sa hovāca kiṃ me 'nnaṃ bhaviṣyatīti | yad idaṃ kiṃcit āśvabhya ā kīṭapataṅgabhyaḥ" (ChU 5.2.1) iti || 5.28 ||

	**carāṇām annam acarā daṃṣṭriṇām apy adaṃṣṭriṇaḥ |**

**	ahastāś ca sahastānāṃ śūrāṇāṃ caiva bhīravaḥ || 5.29 ||**

**carāś** caraṇpatanaraṇotsāhayoginaḥ śyenanakulādayaḥ | teṣām **acarāḥ** sarpakapotādayaḥ **annam** | evaṃ **daṃṣṭriṇāṃ** siṃhavyāghrādīnāṃ **adaṃṣṭriṇaḥ** rurupṛṣatādayo mṛgāḥ | **ahastāḥ** sarpamatsyādayaḥ **sahastānāṃ** nakulaniṣādādīnām | **śūrāṇāṃ** mahotsāhayuktānāṃ jīvitanirapekṣāṇāṃ **bhīravaḥ** priyajīvitāḥ | alpasattvā annatvena hanyante || 5.29 ||

	**nāttā duṣyaty adann ādyān prāṇino 'hany ahany api |**

**	dhātraiva sṛṣṭā hy ādyāś ca prāṇino 'ttāra eva ca || 5.30 ||**

**attā** bhakṣayitā | **ādyān prāṇinaḥ** attuṃ śakyān | pratidivasaṃ bhakṣayan **na duṣyati** | **dhātraiva** prajāpatinā **attāra ādyā** ubhaye 'pi **sṛṣṭāḥ **| tasmāt prāṇātyaye māṃsam avaśyaṃ bhakṣaṇīyam iti triślokī vidher asyārthavādaḥ || 5.30 ||

	**yajñāya jagdhir māṃsasyety eṣa daivo vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |**

**	ato 'nyathā pravṛttis tu rākṣaso vidhir ucyate || 5.31 ||**

yajñārthaṃ **māṃsasya** piṇḍaprāśitrādi**jagdhir** aśanam | **eṣa daivo vidhiḥ,** devair etad vihitam | **anyathā** tu māṃsāśinaḥ[^93] sarīrapuṣṭyarthakamāṃsāśane **pravṛttiḥ sa rākṣaso vidhiḥ** | piśācānāṃ māṃsabhakṣaṇe sthitir iti nindā || 5.31 ||

	**krītvā svayaṃ vāpy utpādya paropakṛtam eva vā |**

**	devān pitṝṃś cārcayitvā khādan māṃsaṃ na duṣyati || 5.32 ||**

mṛgapakṣimāṃsaviṣayam idaṃ śāstram | rurupṛṣatādīnāṃ śaśakapiñjalādīnāṃ māṃsaṃ devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ cārcanaṃ kṛtvā khādato na doṣaḥ | yathā gṛhe vaiśvadevādyarthe kṛte[^94] saṃvidhānaṃ vināpi vaiśvadevenodanādibhojanam asti, na tathā māṃsasya | evamartham etat punarvacanaṃ **devān pitṝṃś cārcayitveti** | anyathā gṛhasthasya pūrvam eva bhojanam evaṃ rūpam | devebhya iti tena śabdenoddiśya śucau deśe māṃsasya prakṣepaḥ | yadi vā agnaye vāyave sūryāya jātavedasa iti devārcanaṃ kartavyam | agnau evaṃrūpā āhutayaḥ kṛtā[^95] agnimato 'nyatra na bhavanti | na cāgau homena vinā baliharaṇaṃ[^96] kartavyam, karmāntarasya prayogāntarasya ca pratipāditatvāt | āstāṃ tāvad etat | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> śrāddhaṃ pitṝṇām arcanam āhuḥ | dṛṣṭaś ca śrāddhe 'rcanaprayogaḥ | pitṝṃś caiva devān[^97] vadanti | tataś ca sarvasmṛtikāraiḥ śrāddham eva vihitam, na punar anyā kācid eva kriyā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar māṃsasya krayasaṃbhavaḥ, yāvatā āpaṇabhūmer māṃsaṃ krīyamāṇaṃ saunam āpadyate |[^98] saunikair ahatasya svayaṃ mṛtasya paśor māmsam abhakṣyam anārogyakaratvāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | vyādhaśākunikādibhir āhṛtaṃ kreṣyate | na ca te saunikā iti prasiddhās taiś ca vikrayārthaṃ bhrāmyadbhir gṛha ānītaṃ bhavati | tadā saṃbhavati krayaḥ | na hi tat saunam ucyate | 

	**svayaṃ vāpy utpādya** | brāhmaṇo yācñayā, kṣatriyo mṛgayākarmaṇā || 5.32 || 

	**nādyād avidhinā māṃsaṃ vidhijño 'nāpadi dvijaḥ |**

**	jagdhvā hy avidhinā māṃsaṃ pretas tair adyate 'vaśaḥ || 5.33 ||**

pūrvoktād devādyarcanaśiṣṭāt brāhmaṇakāmanādinimittāt antaraṃ[^99] yad bhakṣaṇaṃ so 'vidhis[^100] tena nāśnīyāt māṃsam | uktānuvādo 'yam | **āpadi** prāṇātyaye devādyarcanam api nāpekṣyam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> caitad api nimittatayoktam eva | tataś ca vidhir evāyaṃ nāvidhiḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | prokṣitasaṃbandhād go'vyajasyaiva tatra saṃnidhānāśaṅkāyāṃ[^101] śaśādiviṣaye 'bhyanujñānārtham **anāpadīty** ucyate | 

	[^102]vidhyarthānuṣṭhānaparo **vidhijña** ucyate | tathā laukikānuṣṭhāne 'pi jānātir upacārāt prayujyate | eṣa sa tajjānātīti anuṣṭhānapare prayuñjate | 

	atra phalakathāyām — **jagdhvā** aśāstrīyeṇa nimittena | **preto** mṛtas **taiḥ** prāṇibhir **avaśo 'dyate** | yena viṣayeṇa yo yeṣāṃ māṃsam aśnāti tasya vividhā pīḍā bhavati, etāvanmātraparam etat | anyathā prāyeṇa chāgādimāṃsam aśnāti lokāḥ, na ca chāgādayo māṃsāśinaḥ | atha vā tatkṣtena pāpena kravyādbhir apy adyamānas tair adyata ity ucyate || 5.33 ||

	**na tādṛśaṃ bhavaty eno mṛgahantur dhanārthinaḥ |**

**	yādṛśaṃ bhavati pretya vṛthāmāṃsāni khādataḥ || 5.34 ||**

prasiddhārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 5.34 ||

	**niyuktas tu yathānyāyaṃ yo māṃsaṃ nātti mānavaḥ |**

**	sa pretya paśutāṃ yāti saṃbhavān ekaviṃśatim || 5.35 ||**

saṃbhavān[^103] janmāni | avaśyaṃ prāṇātyayasaṃbhave devārcanaṃ yo na karoti atha ca māṃsam aśnāti sa duṣyaty eva || 5.35 ||

	**asaṃskṛtān paśūn mantrair nādyād vipraḥ kadācana |**

**	mantrais tu saṃskṛtān adyāc chāśvataṃ vidhim āsthitaḥ || 5.36 ||**

prokṣaṇādayaḥ paśubandhe mantravantaḥ saṃskārā vihitās te yeṣāṃ kriyante paśūnāṃ vaidikayāgaśeṣāṇāṃ māṃsam **adyāt** | **śāśvatam** | śāśvato nityo vaidika ity arthaḥ | **āśthita** āśritaḥ || 5.36 ||

**	kuryād ghṛtapaśuṃ saṅge kuryāt piṣṭapaśuṃ tathā | **

**	na tv eva tu vṛthā hantuṃ paśum icchet kadācana || 5.37 ||**

yady eṣāṃ buddhiḥ syāt: "sītāyajñakhaṇḍiyajñacaṇḍikāyāgādiṣu[^104] samācārapramāṇeṣu paśuvadhaḥ phalakāmasya nyāyyaḥ,[^105] dṛṣṭā hi paśuvadhopayācitakenātiśayavatī sasyasaṃpattiḥ" iti, tanniṣedhārtham āha:[^106] **saṅge** prastāvāt paśuvadhaprasaṅge **ghṛtapaśuṃ kuryāt,**[^107] ghṛtapaśum eva kuryāt | paśunā yaṣṭavye tatsthāne ghṛtena yajeta devatāḥ | tad dhi sāmānyena yāgadravyam | atha vā **piṣṭapaśuṃ** piṣṭamayapaśupratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā devatābhya upaharet, piṣṭena vā puroḍāśādi kṛtvā |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">katham</span> ayaṃ vṛthā paśubandhaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | śiṣṭānāṃ[^108] samācāraḥ pramāṇam, na tu[^109] strīśūdrajanānām, avaidyatvāt | nātra vedamūlatā śakyā kalpayitum | devatārādhanārthaṃ tadā hy etad[^110] ācaranti | na ca devatārādhanārthāni vaidikāni karmāṇi, guṇatvena devatāśruteḥ | anvayavyatirekamūlatāṃ cātrecchanti, "dṛśyate paśuvadhopayācitakena phalasaṃpatti" iti manyamānāḥ | ato na vedamūlatā | anvayavyatirekāv api bhrāntimātram, asakṛdvyabhicārāt | 

	ato 'yaṃ śloko nyāyaprāptārthānuvāda eva sauhārdād ācāryeṇa paṭhitaḥ || 5.37 ||

	**yāvanti paśuromāṇi tāvatkṛtvo ha māraṇam |**

**	vṛthāpaśughnaḥ prāpnoti pretya janmani janmani || 5.38 ||**

tāvatīr janmanām āvṛttīr **māraṇaṃ prāpnoti** | **vṛthāpaśughnaḥ** śrutismṛtyor acoditaṃ paśuvadhaṃ yaḥ karoti | tac ca prakaraṇān mahānavamyādiṣu laukikair yat kriyate | paśughna iti kapratyaye chāndasaṃ rūpam || 5.38 ||

	**yajñārthaṃ paśavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ svayam eva svayaṃbhuvā |**

**	yajño 'sya bhūtyai sarvasya tasmād yajñe vadho 'vadhaḥ || 5.39 ||**

nāyam anantarokto doṣaḥ śrutismṛticodite vadhe | yo vadho yajñāṅgabhūtas[^111] tannirvṛttyartham eva **svayaṃbhuvā** prajāpatinā **paśavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ** utpāditāḥ | **svayam evety** arthavādaḥ | **asya** jagato viśvasya | **yajñaḥ** jyotiṣṭomādiḥ | **bhūtyai,** bhūtir vibhavaḥ puṣṭiḥ sphītiḥ | tasmāt tatra yo **vadhaḥ** so **'vadho** vijñeyaḥ | hiṃsājanyasya pāpasya nivṛtter evam ucyate || 5.39 ||

	**oṣadhyaḥ paśavo vṛkṣās tiryañcaḥ pakṣiṇas tathā |**

**	yajñārthaṃ nidhanaṃ prāptāḥ prāpnuvanty ucchritīḥ punaḥ || 5.40 ||**

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar yajñe hiṃsādoṣo nāsti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | hiṃsā hiṃsyamānasya mahān apakāraḥ, prāṇaviyogena putradāradhanavibhavādiviyogena sarvānarthotpatter duṣkṛtasya ca samanantaraṃ narakādiphalavipākasya pratyāsatteḥ | yajñe tu hatānām upakāraḥ, nāpakāraḥ, narakādiphalānutpatteḥ | yato yajñe **nidhanaṃ** vināśaṃ gatā **ucchritīr** utkarṣaṃ jātito devagandharvayonitvaṃ dvīpāntareṣūttarakuruprabhṛtiṣu varṣāntare vā janma **prāpnuvanti** |

	arthavādaś cāyam | na hy atra vidhiḥ śrūyate, **prāpnuvanti** iti vartamānopadeśāt[^112] | na cārthavādāt "pratitiṣṭhanti" itivad vidhipratipattir yuktā, vidhyantarasyābhāvād asaṃbhavāc ca | 

	sarvo 'yam avidhimāṃsabhakṣaṇapratiṣedhaśeṣaḥ | aihalokasaṃpādyatayāpy ayaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ: "na tv eva tu vṛthā hantuṃ paśum icchet" (MDh 5.37) iti | yac cābhyanujñānam "yajñārthaṃ pasavaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ" (MDh 5.39) iti, tat sarvaṃ bhaṣaṇapratiṣedhatayā pratīyate | tathā ca vakṣyati "nākṛtvā prāṇināṃ hiṃsām" (MDh 5.48) ityādi |

	na cātra vidher asti saṃbhavaḥ | na tiraścām adhikāraḥ saṃbhavati, viśeṣavijñānābhāvāt | na cānadhikṛtasya kartṛtvam | nāpy akartṛtve śāstrīyāt karmaṇaḥ phalotpattiḥ | na hy atra dṛṣṭā vastusvābhāvyena[^113] phalotpattiḥ | yathā viṣam aviduṣo 'pi pītavato janayaty eva svaphalam | naivaṃ vaidikārthāḥ | 

	acaitanyāc cauṣadhyādīnām[^114] ṛtviṅnyāyo 'pi nāsti | dṛṣṭaṃ kila kutaścana karmaṇaḥ paraprayuktād apy ṛtvijāṃ phalam: "yaḥ kāmayeta[^115] pāpīyān syāt" (cf. GoB 2.3.3) ityādi | tatra vidhyantaraśeṣatvābhāvāt spaṣṭatvāc[^116] ca vidhipratipatter manuṣyādhikāratvāc ca śāstrasya yukto 'ṅgavyāpārasamāśrito[^117] vācanikas tāvanmātro 'dhikāraḥ | yathā parakīyāśvamedhāvabhṛthe brāhmaṇasya prāyaścittam uktam | iha tv adhikāra eva nāstīty uktam |

	**oṣadhyo** darbhādayaḥ | **paśavaś** chāgādayaḥ | **vṛkṣāḥ** pūjyāḥ | **tiryañcaḥ** apaśavo 'pi paśavo yeṣāṃ haviṣṭvena[^118] codanā "kapiñjalān ālabhate" (VS 24.20) iti | bhārapravahaṇād[^119] anaḍvāhas tiryañco vājapeyādau tiryañca iti vyapadiśyante | yady api teṣāṃ tatra nidhanaṃ nāsti tathāpi yāvatī ca pīḍā vidyata iti sā nidhanaśabdena lakṣyate | **pakṣiṇaḥ** kapiñjalādayaḥ | yady api te paśutvena cocyante,[^120] aprasiddhataraprayogās tu "sapta grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ saptāraṇyāḥ" (ŚB 9.5.2.8) iti | gavādayo 'pakṣiṇaḥ | catuṣpājjātivacanaḥ paśuśabdaḥ | gobalīvardavad vā bhedo draṣṭavyaḥ || 5.40 ||

_yāvatyaḥ kāścic chāstracoditahiṃsās tāḥ saṃkṣpya darśayati |_

	**madhuparke ca yajñe ca pitṛdaivatakarmaṇi |**

**	atraiva paśavo hiṃsyā nānyatrety abravīn manuḥ || 5.41 ||**

	**eṣv artheṣu paśūn hiṃsan vedatattvārthavid dvijaḥ |**

**	ātmānaṃ ca paśuṃ caiva gamayaty uttamāṃ gatim || 5.42 ||**

**madhuparko** vyākhyātaḥ | tatra govadho vihitaḥ | **yajñaḥ** jyotiṣṭomādiḥ | tatra saṃsthaikādaśinyādipaśuvadho nirūḍhapaśuvadhādiḥ svatantra eva ca[^121] | **pitṛdaivataṃ** pitaro devatā yasmin karmaṇy aṣṭakādau, na tu śrāddham | tad dhi siddhena māṃsena vihitam, na ca paśuvadhaś coditaḥ | na cedam eva vidhāyakaṃ yuktam, utpattau śrāddhasya hiṃsāyā acoditatvāt, asya ca vispaṣṭavidhānād aṣṭakāpaśuvadhenāpi netuṃ śakyatvāt, vidhitve cāsya mūlakalpanāprasaṅgāt, vidhyantaraśeṣatāyāś ca vakṣyamāṇatvāt | yeṣāṃ[^122] tu mataṃ pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca karma mahāyañjādi | "brāhmaṇair vadhyāḥ . . . bhṛtyānāṃ caiva vṛttyartham"[^123] (MDh 5.22) āpadi paśuhiṃsanam aprāptaṃ prāṇātyaye 'bhyanujñāyate || 5.41–42 ||

	**gṛhe gurāv araṇye vā nivasann ātmavān dvijaḥ |**

**	nāvedavihitāṃ hiṃsām āpady api samācaret || 5.43 ||**

avedavihitahiṃsāpratiṣedho 'yam | na ca vedavihitābhyanujñāyate | na ca gurau vasato brahmacāriṇo 'raṇye ca tapasyato 'nyā kācid dhiṃsāsti | avakīrṇino brahmacāriṇaḥ syād api | vānaprasthasya tu naivāsti | brahmacāriṇo 'py ātmopekṣaṇaṃ naiveṣyate | ato 'yaṃ vidhir eva śrāddhe | **gṛha** ity anuvāda eva | 

	yadi cāyaṃ vidhiḥ syād — "araṇye" "āpady api" iti kim ālambanam etat syāt | na ca vānaprasthasya sāgnikasyāpi paśuyāgo 'sti | "puroḍāśāś carūṃś caiva" (MDh 6.11) ity atra darśayiṣyāma <span style="text-decoration:underline;">iti kecit</span> | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">upādhyāyas</span> tv āha | yuktaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ | vānaprasthasya tu "aparājitāṃ vāsthāya" (MDh 6.31) ityādinātmatyāgāgo 'pi vihitas tasya nāsti jīvitārthā hiṃseti sphuṭataraṃ tatraiva nirūpayiṣyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> cāpady ayaṃ pratiṣedha ucyate | tat kutas[^124] tatraivānujñānaṃ vyākhyāyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | anyathā na kiṃcid anena kṛtaṃ syāt | arthavādārtham iti ced arthavādasyāpy ālambanam anveṣaṇīyam | ato nāpady ayaṃ pratiṣedho vidhiś cāpdy aviruddhaḥ | bahubhedād āpadām, alpīyasyām āpadi māsikam ardhamāsikaṃ vā bhojanaṃ bhaviṣyatīti buddhyā pravṛttir niṣidhyate | yadā tv eṣā buddhir adhunaivānaśnan na jīvāmi yadā vābhimukhāgata udyataśastra ātatāyī tadāpady anujñā | evaṃ "sarvata evātmānaṃ gopāyet" (GDh 9.34) iti śrutir anugṛhītā bhavati || 5.42–43 ||

	**yā vedavihitā hiṃsā niyatāsmiṃś carācare |**

**	ahiṃsām eva tāṃ vidyād vedād dharmo hi nirbabhau || 5.44 ||**

**vedavihito yaḥ** prāṇivadhaḥ so **'smiñ** jagati **carācare** sthāvarajaṅgame nityo 'nādiḥ | yas tu tantrādiḥ so 'nvayavyatirekabhrāntyā idānīṃtanaḥ | ato vaidikīm hiṃsām[^125] ahiṃsām eva vidyāt, amutra pratyavāyābhāvāt | **ahiṃseti** kāryata ucyate na svarūpataḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca saiva hiṃsārūpā | abhedāt kathaṃ kāryo bhedaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | **vedād dharmo hi nirbabhau** | dharmasyādharmasya ca yat kathanaṃ[^126] tad vedād eva, pauruṣeyāṇām aprāmāṇyāt | vedaś ca tasyā evābhyudayahetutvaṃ kvacit jñāpayati | svarūpābhedo 'pi nāsti, kratvarthapuruṣārthatvena bhedād āśayabedena pravṛtteḥ | laukikyāṃ māṃsīyato dviṣāṇasya vā pravṛttiḥ, vaidikyāṃ tu śāstreṇa coditam idaṃ kratuvartham iti | 

	**nirbabhau** niḥśeṣeṇa bhātaḥ, prakāśatāṃ gata iti yāvat || 5.44 ||

	**yo 'hiṃsakāni bhūtāni hinasty ātmasukhecchayā |**

**	sa jīvaṃś ca mṛtaś caiva na kvacit sukham edhate || 5.45 ||**

akāro 'tra pratiṣedhārthīyaḥ praśliṣṭo draṣṭavyaḥ | ahiṃsakānāṃ ca pratiṣedhāt sarpavyāghrādīnām apratiṣedhaḥ || 5.45 ||

	**yo bandhanavadhakleśān prāṇināṃ na cikīrṣati |**

**	sa sarvasya hitaprepsuḥ sukham atyantam aśnute || 5.46 ||**

**bandhanavadhā** eva **kleśāḥ** | atha vā viśasanādayaḥ[^127] | tān yo na kartum icchati, viśasanam[^128] eva yena na kṛtam, tadviṣayecchaiva yasya nivṛttā | na kevalaṃ pīḍāṃ na karoti, yāvad **dhitaṃ** prepsitum icchati **sarvasya** **sa sukham atyantam aśnute** || 5.46 ||

	**yad dhyāyati yat kurute ratiṃ badhnāti yatra ca |**

**	tad avāpnoty ayatnena yo hinasti na kiṃcana || 5.47 ||**

yac cintayati śulkam arhaṇādi | yatra ca **ratim** abhilāṣaṃ **badhnāty** abhipretya vastuni | **tad ayatnena** svalpenaiva kālen**āvāpnoti** | **yat** tu **kurute** karmaṇā tat karmaniṣpattisamantaram evāvighnena prāpnoti || 5.47 ||

	**nākṛtvā prāṇināṃ hiṃsāṃ māṃsam utpadyate kvacit |**

**	na ca prāṇivadhaḥ svargyas tasmān māṃsaṃ vivarjayet || 5.48 ||**

sarvasya hiṃsāpratiṣedhaślokasaṃghātasya māṃsabhakṣaṇaseṣatāṃ darśayati | yāvat prāṇino na hatās tāvan **māṃsaṃ notpadyate** | hiṃsā cātiśayena duḥkhāvahā | **tasmān māṃsaṃ vivarjayet** |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca svayaṃ mṛtānāṃ bhavaty eva māṃsam, kim idam ucyate "nākṛtvā" iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">arthavādo</span> 'yam | svayaṃ mṛtānāṃ ca māṃsaṃ rogahetutvād aprāptam eva | na hy adatvā māṃsaṃ bhakṣyate | na ca rogahetor dānam asti | 

	**utpadyata** iti māṃsasya hiṃsānimittatvāt kartṛvyapadeśe[^129] samānakartṛkatvaṃ bhavaty evāviruddham | atha vā **utpadyata** iti **na ca svargya** iti | na svargānutpattihetumātram abhipretam api tu narakādiduḥkhahetutvam[^130] || 5.48 ||

	**samutpattiṃ ca māṃsasya vadhabandhau ca dehinām |**

**	prasamīkṣya nivarteta sarvamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇāt || 5.49 ||**

aśucisthāne kukṣau garbhavṛddhiḥ, śukraśoṇitābhyāṃ vāśucibhyāṃ prabhāvaḥ | tathā **vadhabandhau** śarīravatāṃ tatkṛtau | etat sarvaṃ **prasamīkṣya** nipuṇabuddhyā tatvato nirūpya | **nivarteta sarvamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇāt** sarvasyāpratiṣiddhasyāpi, kiṃ punaḥ pratiṣiddhasya | 

	arthavādo 'yam | na punas tatvataḥ aśucy eva māṃsaṃ jñeyam | na hi tadaśucitvavidhiparaṃ vākyam || 5.49 ||

	**na bhakṣayati yo māṃsaṃ vidhiṃ hitvā piśācavat |**

**	sa loke priyatāṃ yāti vyādhibhiś ca na pīḍyate || 5.50 ||**

**vidhir** devārcanaṃ tad **dhitvā** **yo na bhakṣayati,** kiṃ tarhi vidhinā bhakṣayati | **sa** lokasya **priyatāṃ** prāpnoti | priyaḥ sarvasya bhavati | **vyādhibhiś ca** | kṛśadurbalāder māṃsam aśnato vyādhir upajāyate | tenāpi vidhinaivāśitavyam | tathā bhakṣayan **vyādhibhiś ca na pīḍyate** | anyathā aśnann api māṃsaṃ pīḍyata eva vyādhibhiḥ | **piśācavad** iti | piśācās tiryagjātiviśeṣās te vidhim anapekṣya māṃsam aśnanti | tato 'nyo 'pi tathā bhakṣayan piśācasadṛśo bhavatīti nindyate || 5.50 ||

	**anumantā viśasitā nihantā kravikrayī |**

**	saṃskartā copahartā ca khādakaś ceti ghātakāḥ || 5.51 ||**

anyena hanyamānaṃ svaprayojanato yady anyo 'numodate sādhv ayaṃ hantā karotīty **anumantā** | **viśasitā** hatasyāṅgavibhāgakāraḥ | **upahartā** pariveṣakaḥ | **khādaka** ity ete sarve **ghātakāḥ** |

	aghātakeṣu khādanasaṃskāravikrayādikartṛṣu ghātakatve 'dhyāropite nindā, na punas tatvata ete ghātakā eva | laukikī hi vadhakriyā prāṇatyāgaphalā | tasya kartā ghātakaḥ smṛtito gamyate | svatantraḥ karteti viśeṣaśāstrādinā yaḥ prāṇaviyojanaṃ prāṇināṃ kroti sa hantocyate | krayavikrayādyāś ca kiryās tato 'nyā eva |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ceyam api smṛtir eva, ete anumantṛprabhṛtayo ghātakā iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nedaṃ</span> śabdārthasaṃbandhe pramāṇam, kiṃ tarhi dharmādharmayoḥ | abhiyuktataro hi tatra bhavān pāṇiniḥ | manvādayaś ca lokaprasiddhaiḥ padārthair vyavaharanti, na śabdārthasaṃbandhavidhiṃ smaranti | prayoktāro hy ete na smartāraḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca "tam ācāryaṃ prakṣate" (MDh 2.140) ityādeḥ smaranty ete |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | na tatra śāstrasmṛtivirodhaḥ | na ca teṣāṃ vākyānām anyat prayojanam asti | iha tu gauṇenāpi prayojanenārthavādatayāpy upapatter na ghātakatvaṃ śakyam avasātum | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ye 'py āhur</span> "bhakṣakaś cen na vidyate vadhako 'pi na vidyata iti bhakṣaṇaprayukta eva vadhaḥ, prayojakaś ca kartā smaryate | tato mukhyam eva ghātakatvam | ato ghātakaprāyaścittam eva khādakasya yuktam" iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam</span> iti[^131] brūmaḥ | pṛthakprāyaścittaṃ hatānāṃ rasāsvādakasya "jagdhvā māṃsam abhakṣyaṃ ca" iti (MDh 11.151 ) | 

	yad api[^132] prayojakatvena kartṛtvam uktaṃ tad api naivāsti | idaṃ hi tasya lakṣaṇam: 

	preṣaṇādhyeṣaṇābhyāṃ tu yaḥ svatantrasya codakaḥ |

	sa kartā caiva[^133] hetuś ca mukhyo nopacaran paraḥ || iti | 

vadhako hi jīvanaprayuktyā pravartate māṃsavikrayeṇa jīviṣyāmīti, na tu khādakena viniyujyate | 

	atha tatsamarthācaraṇaṃ prayojakatvam | yo 'yaṃ kriyāṃ kartum adhyavasitas tatrānukūlyena yaḥ saṃvidhitsuḥ sa prayojaka iti | etad apy atra naivāsti | sādhanopanidhānaṃ trasataḥ paśor asvatantrīkaraṇaṃ[^134] khaḍgopanayanam ity evaṃ saṃvidhānaśabdavācyaṃ yuktam | tena vinā kriyā na niṣpadyate | 

	atha yadarthaḥ kriyārambhaḥ sa prayojakaś ceti cet, māṇavakam adhyāpayatīty adhyāpanahetukartṛsaṃjñāpratilambhaḥ,[^135]  na hy adhyayanam adhyāpayatyarthaḥ[^136] | 

	na cāsau kaṃcid[^137] uddiśya hanane pravartate | yenāsya tadarthanirūpaṇāya bhakṣaṇe 'narthā pravṛttiḥ syāt | sarva ime svabhūtyai yatante | na kena kaśct paro 'nugrahītavya iti muhūrtam apy avatiṣṭhate ity api pūrṇakāmaḥ | 

	atha svārthaṃ pravṛttasya bhakṣayitāram antareṇa pravṛttir anarthikā | tasmiṃs tu sati phalavatī | phalaṃ ca prayojakam | tac ca khādakādhīnam iti pāraṃparyeṇa khādakaḥ prayojaka iti | 

	evaṃ tarhi yo dveṣād vadhyate sa hantuḥ prayojakaḥ syāt | tataś ca hanyamāna eva hantā saṃpadyate | na hi dveṣeṇa vinā hantṛtvopapattir iti | tathā brahmahatyāyām api sarvasvadānaṃ[^138] pātakasaṃprayojakam | na hi pratigrāhayitāram antareṇa pratigrahopapattis tataś ca pratigrāhī na kevalaṃ pratyaveyād api tu dātāpi | rūpavatī ca strī smaraśaradahyamānahṛdayena rāgiṇā darśitaspṛhātiśayena śīlaṃ rakṣantī pratyaveyāt |

	tasmān nedaṃ prayojakalakṣaṇam | 

	tau hi vadhakakhādakau svārthapravṛttau naṣṭāśvadagdharathavad itaretaropakāram anubhavantau, na punar anyataraprayojakau[^139] | "śūdraviṭkṣatraviprāṇām" (MDh 8.104) ity atra śloke nipuṇam etan nirṇītam[^140] || 5.51 ||

	**svamāṃsaṃ paramāṃsena yo vardhayitum icchati |**

**	anabhyarcya pitṝn devāṃs tato 'nyo nāsty apuṇyakṛt || 5.52 ||**

adhikapuṣṭyarthaṃ yo māṃsam aśnāti tasyeyaṃ nindā | na tu rogotpattibhayāśaṅkayā | yata āha | **yo vardhayitum icchantīti** | tasyāpy **anabhyarcya pitṝn devān** | na tu rogahetots tv arcanam akurvato 'pi kathaṃcid asaṃbhavān na doṣaḥ || 5.52 ||

	**varṣe varṣe 'śvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ |**

**	māṃsāni ca na khāded yas tayoḥ puṇyaphalaṃ samam || 5.53 ||**

devādyarcanaśiṣṭasya śaśādimāṃsasya bhakṣaṇam anujñātam | tato nivartamāno 'śvamedhaphalam aśnute | aśvamedhasya phalam "sarvān kāmān avaśyaṃ sarvāvijitīḥ" ityādi |

	na cātra codanīyam: kathaṃ mahāprayāsena bahudhanavyayena ca tulyaphalatā māṃsanivṛtteḥ syāt | yata eṣo 'pi saṃyamo 'tiduṣkaraḥ | kiṃ ca lokavat parimāṇataḥ phalaviśeṣaḥ syād ity ayaṃ nyāyo jṛmbhata eva | ataḥ phalavidhau na doṣaḥ | 

	vayaṃ tu brūmaḥ | arthavāda evāyam | yato **varṣe śataṃ samā** iti cārthavādapakṣe[^141] sughaṭam | na hi prativarṣam aśvamedhasya vidheyatvasaṃbhavaḥ | nāpi **varṣe śatam**, tāvataḥ kālasyādhikāriṇo jīvanādyasaṃbhavāt | 

	puṇyaṃ ca phalaṃ ca **puṇyaphalam** | samāhāradvandvaḥ | ṣaṣṭhīsamāse hy asāmarthyam || 5.53||

	**phalamūlāśanair medhyair munyannānāṃ ca bhojanaiḥ |**

**	na tatphalam avāpnoti yan māṃsaparivarjanāt || 5.54 ||**

**medhyair** devārhaiḥ | **munyannāni** nīvārādyannāny akṛṣṭapacyajanitāni | ayam arthavāda eva || 5.54 ||

	**māṃ sa bhakṣayitāmutra yasya māṃsam ihādmy aham |**

**	etan māṃsasya māṃsatvaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ || 5.55 ||**

nāmadheyanirvacanam arthavādaḥ | **māṃ sa bhakṣayitā** | sa iti sarvanāma sāmānyāpekṣaṃ yogyenārthena nirākāṅkṣīkaroti[^142] yasya māṃsam aśnāti || 5.55 ||

	**na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣo na madye na ca maithune |**

**	pravṛttir eṣā bhūtānāṃ nivṛttis tu mahāphalā || 5.56 ||**

"prāṇasyānnam" (MDh 5.28) ity ata ārabhya yāvad ayaṃ śloko 'rthavādasaṃghāta eva | dvitrāḥ ślokā vidheyārthāḥ[^143] | 

	**na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣo** yathā "krītvā svayaṃ vāpy utpādya" (MDh 5.32) iti tathāyam api ślokaḥ | **nivṛttis tu mahāphalety** etad atra śrūyate | bahubhir nindārthākarair īdṛśaḥ saṃskāro jāto yan na kiṃcin māṃsam aśitavyam | bhūtānāṃ vṛttyartham āha: **na māṃsabhakṣaṇe doṣa** iti | devārcanaśiṣṭe brāhmaṇakāmyādiṣu nimitteṣu prāgukteṣu na doṣaḥ | kiṃ tu yady aśitum[^144] icchanti | nivṛttir na bhakṣayāmīti saṃkapapūrvikā mahāphalā | phalaviśeṣāśruteḥ svargaḥ phalam iti mīmāṃsakāḥ | 

	evaṃ madye kṣatriyādīnām, maithune tu sarvavarṇānām, divodakyāparvakālād anyatra | alpasv alpā pravṛttir eṣā śāstrīyā | bhūtānāṃ śarīrasthitihetvarthā pravṛttiḥ | tathā cāyurvedakṛt | 

	āhāro brahmacaryaṃ ca nidrā ceti trayaṃ matam |

	mādakaṃ ca striyaś caiva hy upastambhanam āyuṣaḥ || iti |

	yas tu tena vināpi śaknoti jīvituṃ tasya **nivṛttir mahāphalā** | pradarśanārthaṃ caitat | aśiṣṭāpratiṣiddhaviṣayāṇām anyāsām api nivṛttīnām evam eva | yatra vidhānaṃ puruṣasya pravartamānasya prītyatiśayotpattiprayojanam anindyam, garheta vā yato nivṛttiḥ phalāya, yathā madhvaśanaṃ saṃpannabhojanaṃ rāṅkavaṃ paridhānam ity evamādi | tathā ca śiṣṭasamācāraḥ | vyāsaś ca bhagavān evam āha | ye tu saṃsaktito 'śiṣṭāpratiṣiddhā api yathā hasitakaṇḍūyanādayas tato nivṛttir dharmāya || 5.56 ||

	**pretaśuddhiṃ pravakṣyāmi dravyaśuddhiṃ tathaiva ca |**

**	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ || 5.57 ||**

**caturṇām apī**tivacanaṃ sāmānyavihitā dharmāḥ śūdrasya nedṛśaṃ yatnam antareṇa bhavantīti jñāpanārtham | preteṣu jīvatāṃ śuddhiḥ | supsupeti samāsaḥ | prāpaṇaṃ cāpretavan nimittā śuddhir iyaṃ viśeṣasya | ataś ca yady api śuddhivacanaṃ pratijñāyate, tathāpy aśuddhisāpekṣatvāc chuddheḥ śāstrapratyayakārakatvād ubhayoḥ, apratijñātāpi prathamam aśuddhir ucyate || 5.57 ||

	**dantajāte 'nujāte ca kṛtacūḍe ca saṃsthite |**

**	aśuddhā bāndhavāḥ sarve sūtake ca tathocyate || 5.58 ||**

**anujāto** dantajātād bālatara iti smaranti | tathāvibhāgenoddeśamātram idaṃ yatas tadapekṣa āśaucakālabhedo bhaviṣyati | tad yathā smṛtyantare "ā dantajanmanaḥ",[^145] tathā "bāle deśāntarasthe ca" (MDh 5.77) ityādinā sadyaḥśaucaṃ śrutam | bāla ajātadanto vijñeyaḥ | evaṃ ca "nṛṇām akṛtacūḍānām" (MDh 5.66) ity etad ekarātrikam āśaucaṃ dantajāte 'py avasthāpyate | evam ete smṛtī[^146] viṣayavyavasthayā avirodhinyau bālaviṣaye bhavataḥ | naiśikī ca śuddhir ā cūḍākaraṇāt | yato nivṛttamuṇḍakānāṃ trirātraṃ vakṣyati | tac ca trirātraṃ prāg upanayanāt parataḥ "śuddhyed vipraḥ" (MDh 5.82) ityādi | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ye tu</span> "daśāhaṃ śāvam āśaucam" (MDh 5.59) ity etān pakṣān vayovibhāgena varṇayanti, smṛtyantarāt samācārāc ca vyutkrameṇa saṃbandhayanti, daśāham upanītasya anupanītasya caturahaṃ kṛtamuṇḍasya tryahaṃ jātadantasyaikāham anujātasya sadyaḥśaucikādayas tu vikalpāḥ | evaṃ tryahacaturahayoḥ kṛtacūḍasya | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">teṣāṃ</span> mate smṛtyantaraprasiddho vṛttasvādhyāyāpekṣo na vikalpaḥ pratipāditaḥ syāt | taccottaratra darśayiṣyāmaḥ | 

	sarvavyāpāranivṛttyā mṛta ucyate, saṃpūrvasya tiṣṭhater vyāpāroparamadarśanāt | **bāndhavāḥ** sapiṇḍāḥ samānodakāś ca | **sūtake ca** putrajanmādau | **tathocyate aśuddhā bāndhavāḥ sarva** ity etenāsya saṃbandhaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar atra vayobhedapratipattir yāvatā kṛtamuṇḍa iti saṃskārasaṃbandho gamyate | kṛtopanayane cety atra śrutam eva | ata eva kṛtacauḍaḥ kiyantaṃ kālam ucyata iti naiva śrūyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | dantajātānujātasāhacaryāt[^147] kṛtamuṇḍaḥ kālalakṣaṇārtho vijñāyate | sa ca kālo 'tra prathamatṛtīyavarṣaḥ[^148] | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady</span> api prathame varṣe vaikalpikaṃ muṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tasmint samāśrīyamāṇe "ā dantajanmanaḥ sadyaḥ"[^149] ity etad bādhitaṃ bhavati |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad apy</span> ayuktam | kiyān avadhiḥ **kṛtamuṇḍa** iti | **ca**śabdāt **kṛtamuṇḍe ce**ti kṛtopanayane ceti labyate, saṃskārāntaraprāptau vyapadeśāntarapravṛtteḥ | evaṃ caitayā smṛtyā ekavākyatā bhaviṣyati "ā dantajanmanaḥ sadyaḥ"[^150] ity atrāpi | "trirātram ā vratādeśāt"[^151] iti vratādeśagrahaṇaṃ kālopalakṣaṇārtham eva | na ca brāhmaṇasyānityo 'ṣṭamavarṣe evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayor yaś ca kālaḥ, tadā śūdrasya na kaścit kāla uktaḥ syāt | tatrāpy atītaśaiśavasya "paripūrṇaṃ sarveṣām" itivacanāt | ataś ca ā aṣṭamād varṣād ūrdhvaṃ caturṇām api varṇānāṃ sarvāśaucam, śūdrasyāpi tasya kālasya sadbhāvāt | yasmiṃs tu pakṣe ekādaśe varṣe kṣatriyavaiśyayor upanayanaṃ lakṣyate tadā śūdrasya na kaścit kāla uktaḥ syāt | tatrāpy atītaśaiśavasya paripūrṇam, arvāk trirātram | śaiśavasya nivṛttiś ca smṛtyantare "prāg aṣṭamāc śiśuḥ proktaḥ", anyais tu " ā ṣōḍaśād bhaved bālaḥ" iti | ye 'pi ṣoḍaśād bālyanivṛttim āhus teṣām apy aṣṭamād ūrdhvaṃ māsiky eva śuddhiḥ | evaṃ paṭhyate "ūrdhvaṃ tu ṣaḍbhyo varṣebhyaḥ śuddhiḥ śūdrasya māsikī" | anyatra paṭhitam aṣṭavarṣasya māsa iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> vakṣyamāṇebhya eva vākyebhya eṣā vayobhedavyavasthā labhyate | kim anena dantajāta ity uddeśena |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | sukhāvabodhārtham || 5.58 ||

	**daśāhaṃ śāvam āśaucaṃ sapiṇḍeṣu vidhīyate |**

**	arvāk saṃcayanād asthnāṃ tryaham ekāham eva vā || 5.59 ||**

sāpiṇḍyalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyate | **arvāk saṃcayanād** iti caturahopalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyati | "āhitāgneḥ saṃcayanaṃ caturthyām" iti vacanam asti | ayaṃ ca vikalpo vṛttasvādhyāyāpekṣo vṛttāpekṣo vā | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	ekāhād brāhmaṇaḥ śuddho yas tu brahmāgnisaṃyutaḥ |

	tryahāt kevalavedas tu nirguṇo daśabhir dinaiḥ ||

tatra trivedasyāgnimata ekāhaḥ | dvivedasya tu tryaham | nirguṇasya daśāham | gautamena (GDh 14.44) paṭhitaṃ sadyaḥ śaucam | tac ca viśeṣa eva brāhmaṇasya svādhyāyānivṛttyartham | tatra kriyāntarāṇi: 

	ubhayatra daśāhāni kulasyānnaṃ na bhujyate |

	dānaṃ pratigraho homaḥ svādhyāyaś ca nivartate || 

ityādyāḥ kriyā nivartante | kevalaṃ bahuvedasyāguṇyamānaṃ praṇaśyatīti svādhyāyo na nivartate | 

	tathā vṛttyapekṣo yukto vikalpaḥ | ṣaṭkarmajīvino daśāhaḥ, tribir anya ity asya caturahaḥ, dvābhyām eka ity asya tryahaḥ | dāśāhika āśauce pratigrahādāv anadhikārāt prāṇayātraiva durlabhā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ye tu</span> "vayāṃsi catvāri, catvāraś cāśaucakālāḥ, ato yathāvayo yathāsaṃkhyena saṃbandhaḥ," teṣāṃ dantajāte daśāhaḥ prāpnoti, upanīte tu mṛte ekāha eva | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tatra</span> smṛtyantarasamācāravirodhaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha</span> virodhaparihārārthaṃ prātilomyena saṃbandhaḥ kriyate | "upanīte daśāhaḥ kṛtamuṇḍe caturahaḥ tryaho dantajāte ekāho 'nujāta" iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrāpi</span> "nivṛttacauḍakānāṃ trirātrāt" iti virodhena vikalpo yuktaḥ, svaśabdena trirātrasyānuvidhānāt, caturahasya vṛttibhedena saṃcayabhedena viṣayatvasiddheḥ | smṛtyantreṇaivam ekavākyatā bhavati ekāhād ityanena | anyathā vayobhedena vikalpe vyākhyāyamāne vṛttasvādhyāyāpekṣo mānave śāstre kena vikalpo labhyate |

	 ato gautamavacanād yasya prātyahikena pratigraheṇa vināpi vṛttir asti kusūladhānyādes tasya bahusvādhyāyasya svādhyāyādhyayanamātre sadyaḥśuddhiḥ | ye 'pi tryahadayaḥ kalpās tatrāpi tryahaihikādīnāṃ tāvanmātra eva viśuddhir vṛttyarthe pratigrahe 'nenaiva gautamadarśanena | anyathā brāhmaṇasya svādhyāyina ity evāvakṣyat na svādhyāyānivṛttyartham iti | 

	ato yady apy aviśeṣeṇaikāhāc chuddhir ityādi śrutam, tathāpi niyatakriyāviṣayaṃ vijñēyam | yena nityavad brāhmaṇasya daśāham āha "śuddhyed vipro daśāhena" iti (MDh 5.82) | na hy anyat punarvacane prayojanam asti | tasmād vikalpo 'yaṃ yuktena mārgeṇa vyākhyeyaḥ | yatra punar bālādau sadyaḥśaucam, nivṛttamuṇḍakādau trirātram, tatra vikalpābhāvāt sarvakriyāsu śucitvam || 5.59 ||

	**sapiṇḍatā tu puruṣe saptame vinivartate |**

**	samānodakabhāvas tu janmanāmnor avedane || 5.60 ||**

anvayasaṃjñāvijñānād bāndhavagrahaṇānuvṛtteś cānvayajāḥ **saptamapuruṣā**vadhayaḥ **sapiṇḍā** ucyante | "yebhyaḥ svasya[^152] pitā dadyāt tebhyaḥ putraḥ" iti jīvatpūrvapitrāder vidhānāt ṣaṭ tāvad yogyatayā sapiṇḍā bhavanti | yady api pitṛbhyo dīyate ātmanā saptama ataḥ pitāmahaprapitāmahādyāḥ pūrvānvayajātās[^153] te sapiṇḍā iti vyapadiśyante | pūrve ṣaṭ sapiṇḍāḥ | apare putrādayaḥ ṣaḍ eva | yata ekasyāḥ piṇḍadānakriyāyāḥ sahabhāvāt sapiṇḍādyupadeśo labhyate, putrāder api sahabhāvaḥ pautrādinā kriyamāṇo 'yam, tena yebhyo dīyate yaiś ca saha saṃpradānavān bhaviṣyati sarve te sapiṇḍā vyapadiśyante | yato na tatra piṇḍadānam avadhyupalakṣaṇatvāc[^154] chaṅkha[^155] iva śaṅkhavelāyām[^156] āgantavyam iti | tena yāvad uktaṃ syāt "prapitāmahasya yaḥ prapitāmahas tadanvayajā ye yāvat saptamās te sapiṇḍā," evaṃ[^157] svasaṃtatau pitrādisaṃtatau draṣṭavyam | yata eva bhedas tam upādāya gaṇanā kartavyā yāvat saptamāvadhi | yathā pitāmaho yeṣām ekas te tata ārabhya saptamāvadhayaḥ sapiṇḍā ity eva sarvatra |

	tadanvayajatve copalakṣaṇe jāter anāśrayaṇād vijātīyā api kṣatriyādayo brāhmaṇādīnāṃ sapiṇḍā bhavanti | ata eva tajjananādyāśauce brāhmaṇasya daśāha eva, teṣāṃ tu svakāla eva dvādaśāhādiḥ | ataḥ sarvasya vijātīyanimitte vijātīyasapiṇḍanimitte vā janmādau svakāla eva śuddhiḥ | 

	kṣatriyādīnāṃ brāhmaṇāpekṣayā tripuruṣaṃ sāpiṇḍyam | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ:

	yady ekajātā bahavaḥ pṛthakkṣetrāḥ pṛthagjanāḥ | 

	ekapiṇḍāh pṛthakśaucāḥ piṇḍas tv āvartate triṣu ||

"pṛthakkṣetrāḥ" bhinnajātīyāsu strīṣv ity arthaḥ | "pṛthagjanāḥ" pṛthakkṣetrasamānajātīyā apy anekamātṛkā bhavanti, tadartham ubhayor upādānam | "ekapiṇḍāḥ" sapiṇḍā bhavanti | kiṃ tu "pṛthakśaucāḥ" svajātinimitta eva teṣāṃ śuddhikālaḥ | brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyādeḥ sūtakādau daśāhaḥ, brāhmaṇasya sūtake teṣāṃ dvādaśāhaś ca | tathā cānyo 'pi viśeṣaḥ: "piṇḍas triṣv āvartate" | triṣv eva bhavati puruṣeṣu | 

	samānajātīyāpekṣayā kṣatriyādīnāṃ brāhmaṇavat ṣaṭ puruṣasya sāpiṇḍyam "ekajātāḥ pṛthakkṣetrāḥ" ityādiviśeṣaṇopādānāt | asamānajātīyāpekṣaṃ tripuruṣatvam anena vākyena śakyate pratipādayitum | eṣa evārtho 'nayā smṛtyā spaṣṭīkriyate:

	kṣatraviṭśūdradāyādā ye suyur viprasya bāṇdhavāḥ |

	teṣām āśauce viprasya daśāhāc chuddhir iṣyate ||

"ṣaḍbhis tribhir athaikena" ityādi ca | 

	strīṇāṃ tu vijātīyānāṃ bhartṛkālena jīvati bhartari śuddhiḥ | āha ca:

	sūtau mṛte tu dāsānāṃ[^158] patnīnāṃ cānulomataḥ |

	svāmitulyaṃ bhavec chaucaṃ mṛte svāmini paitrakam ||

anye paṭhanti "asavarṇāsutānām" iti prathamaṃ pādam | yady ayam asti pāṭhas tadā putrāṇām api śūdrāṇāṃ pitṛgṛhe vyavasthitānāṃ tatparatantrāṇāṃ pitṛjātyapekṣayā daśāhādir eva śuddhikālaḥ | 

	dāsāś cātra vaitanikā gṛhyante | ye tu garbhadāsās teṣāṃ vidhyantaraṃ śrūyate:

	kāravaḥ śilpino vaidyā dāsīdāsaṃ tathaiva ca |

	rājāno[^159] rājabhṛtyāś ca sadyaḥśaucāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || iti |

sparśane caivam eteṣāṃ śucitvaṃ vijñeyam, na punar dānabhojanādikriyāsu | yataḥ karmanimittā ete śabdāḥ, ataḥ kiṃ viparyaye śuddhiḥ kiṃ sarvāḥ kriyāḥ pratiprasavā uta kāścid evābhyanujñāyante | yato "rājñaś ca kāryāvidhātārtham" ity ākāṅkṣāyāṃ yāny eva karmāṇi tāny eva hṛdayam āgacchanti | tathaiva ca samācāraḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca nātra sparśapratiṣedhaḥ śrutaḥ | 

	yāvatā smṛtyantare paṭhyate: 

	asthisaṃcayanād ūrdhvam aṅgasparśo vidhīyate |

tathānyac ca:

	tribhiś caturbhir vāhobhir brāhmaṇaḥ spṛśyatām iyāt |

	ekādaśena śuddhiḥ syān mṛtake sūtake tathā ||

"rājñaḥ ṣaṣṭhe saptame vā sparśaḥ, dvādaśāhenānnaśūddhiḥ | vaiśyasya sparśanam aṣṭame navame vā, pakṣeṇānnaśuddhiḥ | śūdrasya sparśanam ekādaśe dvādaśe vā, māsenānnaśuddhiḥ " iti[^160] hāritaḥ | tathā vākyantaram api:

	sparśe krameṇa varṇānāṃ tricatuḥpañcaṣair dinaiḥ |

	bhojyānno daśabhir vipraḥ śeṣā[^161] dvitriṣaḍuttaraiḥ ||

	ete ca vikalpāḥ prayojanāpekṣayā guṇavad aguṇāpekṣayā vyavasthāpanīyāḥ | sarveṣāṃ tāvad brāhmaṇasya bhaktadāsās tricaturair ahobhiḥ sparśanena dūṣayanti | garbhadāsās tu sadyaḥ | evam itareṣām api varṇānā | 

	yatredaṃ sadyaḥśaucaṃ tatra sarvatra snānaṃ vāsasā ca | dravyasya śuddhir yā yasya vihitā iti jñāpayiṣyate (MDh 5.109) |

	kanyānām api tripauruṣeyi sapiṇḍatā | "saputrāṇāṃ tu strīṇāṃ tripuruṣaṃ vijñāyate" (VaDh 4.18) iti vasiṣṭhaḥ | āśauca evaitat | vivāhe tu vidhir darśitaḥ | 

	sthitam etat: saptamapuruṣo maryādā, ṣaṭpuruṣāḥ sapiṇḍā iti | **saptame** prāpte **vinivartate** | **samānodakabhāvaḥ** samānodakavyapadeśaḥ | **janmanāmnor avedane** | janma ca "ayam asmatkule jātaḥ", nāma amuṣmād idaṃ nāmakāt pitṛpitāmahādeḥ | ubhayor avedane nivṛttir | ataś cānyatare jñāte[^162] 'py aniṣṭodakaṃ jñeyam | "avatīrya nadīm anyad vā jalāśayaṃ nābhidaghnabhugno[^163] dakṣiṇābhimukhaḥ savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyām udakaṃ kṛtvānavekṣamāṇāḥ pratyāvrajeyuḥ" iti || 5.60 ||

	**janane 'py evam eva syān mātāpitros tu sūtakam |**

**	sūtakaṃ mātur eva syād upaspṛśya pitā śuciḥ || 5.61 ||**

**evam** etat sapiṇḍānāṃ **janane** | yathaiva daśāhādayaḥ kalpāḥ ṣaṭkarmādivṛttyapekṣayā svādhyāyālpamahatvāpekṣayā ca vyavasthitā maraṇe, tathaiva **janane 'py** āśaucamātram atidiśyate kālānavacchinnam | sāmarthyāc cāgṛhyamāṇaviśeṣatayā tatsaṃbandhasakalalābhaḥ | kālāvacchinnātideśe tu ekenaiva mukhyatvād daśāhena saṃbandhaḥ svādhyāyādiṣv syāt | yadi vā pāṭhapratyāsattyā[^164] daśāhādyapekṣayā ekāhena ekenaiva[^165] ca nirākāṃkṣīkṛtatvād anyais tryahādibhir na saṃbandhaḥ syāt | tatreyaṃ smṛtir aviśeṣeṇa vṛttasvādhyāyāpekṣāyāṃ vyavasthāyāṃ mṛtasūtakayor vidadhatī, janane guṇādyanapekṣayā jātimātre sthāpyamānā, virudhyeta[^166] | samācāraś ca bādhitaḥ syāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> evaṃ strīṇām api tryahaikāhādayaḥ kalpāḥ sūtikānāṃ prāpnuvanti samācāravirodhinaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | yady ayaṃ vikalpaḥ syāt tad evam[^167] | vyavasthita evāsīt kalpaḥ | tathā hi **tu**śabda upapannataro bhavati | 

	**sūtaka**śabdaś ca nāśauce vartate | lakṣaṇayā sūtakasaṃbandhy aśaucaṃ lakṣayet | lakṣaṇāyāḥ sāhacaryād aspṛśyataiva lakṣayituṃ yuktā | yadi ca sarvam āśaucam abhipretaṃ syād āśaucagrahaṇam evākariṣyat "aśaucaṃ mātur eva" iti | ataś ca smṛtyantare trirātram aspṛśyatoktyā iha tadabhāvas tayor vikalpaḥ **sūtakaṃ mātur eva** | mātāpitror mātur eveti pitur vikalpaḥ | **upaspṛśya** snātvā **śucir bhavatīti** | upakramamātram idaṃ vakṣyamāṇena ślokena pitur api tryaham eva || 5.61 ||

	**nirasya tu pumāñ chukram upaspṛśyaiva śudhyati |**

**	baijikād abhisaṃbandhād anurundhyād aghaṃ tryaham || 5.62 ||**

sahetukaṃ tryaham upadiśann apasparśanaśuddhiṃ pūrvoktām anumanyate | kim artham ucyata iti cet, sarūpavidhitayārthavādārtham, na vidheyatayā "jartilayavāgvā vā juhuyāt" (TS 5.4.3.2) itivat[^168] |

	**nirasya tu śukraṃ** maithunadharmeṇa saṃprayujya śukrotsargād anantaraṃ **upaspṛśya** snātvā śucir bhavati | ato **baijikād abhisaṃbandhāt** | bījanimitto **baihikaḥ** | **abhisaṃbandhaḥ** apatyotpattiḥ | atas tatra kathaṃ **nānurundhyān** nānuvarteta | **agham** āśaucaṃ **tryaham** | yādṛśaṃ ca śukranirasanena akṛtasnānasyāśucitvam, na tādṛśam eva prasave, api tu tryaham | pūrvaślokārdhatryahaśeṣatayānūdyate | ata evopaspṛśyeti snānam ucyate, "snānaṃ maithuninaḥ smṛtam" iti vacanān nācamanam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">putre tu</span> jāte tadahaḥ spṛśyataiveti kecit | tathā ca śaṃkha āha: "kumāraprasave nāḍyām acchinnayāṃ guḍatilahiraṇyavastraprāvaraṇagodhānyapratigraheṣv adoṣas tadahar ity eke" | 

	tasmāt sa divasaḥ puṇyaḥ pitṝṇāṃ prītivardhanaḥ | 

	smaraṇāc caiva pūrveṣāṃ tadahar na praduṣyati || iti |

tathā śrāddham apy eke kurvantīti ca | anena pituḥ sarvathāśaucābhāva eva | 

	tatraite smṛtī pūrvavad vṛttisadasadbhāvāpekṣayā vikalpyete[^169] || 5.62 ||

	**ahnā caikena rātryā ca trirātrair eva ca tribhiḥ |**

**	śavaspṛśo viśudhyanti tryahād udakadāyinaḥ || 5.63 ||**

trayas trirātrā navāhāni | **ekena ca ahnā** ekayā ca **rātryā** ahorātraḥ | evaṃ daśāho vṛttānurodhād evam upadiṣṭaḥ | **śavaspṛśaḥ** śavasya snānālaṃkārādikāriṇaḥ | anyeṣāṃ snānamātraṃ vakṣyati tanniryāpakānāṃ ca | tathā ca prakaṭīkariṣyati "pretāhāraiḥ samam" (MDh 5.64) ity atra | etac ca samānodakānām, mūlyena vā nirharatām | anāthanirharaṇe tu smṛtyantare |

	na teṣām aśubhaṃ kiṃcin nāśaucaṃ śubhakarmaṇām |

	jalāvagāhanāt teṣāṃ sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate ||

yat tu "asapiṇḍaṃ dvijam" (MDh 5.100) iti tatra vai vakṣyāmaḥ | **udakadāyinaḥ** samānodakāḥ | teṣāṃ ca "pṛthakpiṇḍe ca saṃsthite" (MDh 5.77) iti sadyaḥśaucam api vakṣyate | tatra vikalpaḥ | sapiṇḍeṣv etad asvādhyāyādyapekṣam || 5.63 ||

	**guroḥ pretasya śiṣyas tu pitṛmedhaṃ samācaran |**

**	pretāhāraiḥ samaṃ tatra daśarātreṇa śudhyati || 5.64 ||**

**pitṛmedhaḥ** carameṣṭiḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu sarvaṃ karmaiva lakṣyata iti prāhuḥ | tat kurvan **śiṣyo** **daśarātreṇa śudhyati** | brahmacāriṇo 'py ayaṃ vidhir asty eva | **pretāhāraiḥ samaḥ** | pretaṃ haranti niryāpayanti tathā teṣāṃ daśāhaḥ | evaṃ śiṣyasyāpīty arthaḥ || 5.46 ||

	**rātribhir māsatulyābhir garbhasrāve viśudhyati |**

**	rajasy uparate sādhvī snānena strī rajasvalā || 5.65 ||**

**garbhasrāve** garbhamāsasamā rātrīḥ striyā eva śuddhir yuktā, iha vākye tasyāḥ śrutatvāt | sapiṇḍānāṃ tu smṛtyantarasamācārāv anveṣaṇīyau | vasiṣṭhena tu sapiṇḍānāṃ tryahaḥ samāmnātaḥ: "ūnadivarṣe prete garbhapatane sapiṇḍānāṃ trirātram aśaucam" (VaDh 4.34) | srāvas tu garbhasya māsatrayād ūrdhvaṃ prāg daśamān māsāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu prāṅ navamād ity āhuḥ | aprāptakālasya pātaḥ srāva ucyate | na punar dravarūpasyaiva | tathā gautamena garbhasraṃsane "garbhamāsasamā rātrīḥ" iti paṭhitam (GDh 14.17) | saptamāsyāś ca jīvanti | ataḥ saptame māse pūrṇam āśaucam | etat tu jīvato jātasya yuktam anyathā tu garbhamāsasamā ity eva |
