	iha rajasvalāyā rajasy uparate snānena śuddhir āmnātā | smṛtyantare tryahād ūrdhvam | tatraivaṃ vyavasthā | prāk tryahād rajonivṛttāv api nāsti śuddhir ūrdhvam anuparate 'pi bhavati | kiṃ tu **viśuddhyatīti** | prakṛte punaḥ **sādhvīti** vacanād anivṛtte rajasi vaidikakarmādhikārānupraveśo nāsti, na punaḥ sparśādiniṣedhaḥ | utktam "ādyāś catasro ninditāḥ" (MDh 3.47) iti | **rajasvalā strī rajasy uparate snānena sādhvī** bhavati śuddhā karmayogyety evaṃ padayojanā | strīgrahaṇaṃ varṇamātrastryartham | pūrve tu ślokā brāhmaṇaviṣayā vyākhyātās tadāśaṅkānivṛttyarthaṃ strīgrahaṇam | uttaratrāpi yatra viśeṣapramāṇaṃ nāsti tatrāpi varṇamātraviṣayatayaiva, yathā "nṛṇām akṛtamuṇḍānām" (MDh 5.66) iti || 5.65 ||

	**nṛṇām akṛtamuṇḍānāṃ viśuddhir naiśikī smṛtā |**

**	nirvṛttamuṇḍakānāṃ tu trirātrāc chuddhir iṣyate || 5.66 ||**

imāḥ ṣaṣṭhīḥ "kartṛkarmaṇoḥ kṛti" (Pāṇ 2.3.65) iti kartṛlakṣaṇāḥ <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> vyācakṣate | akṛtacūḍa ekāhena śuddhyati | tathā vayo'vasthāpekṣo 'pi vikalpa ity ekīyamatam uktam | tasyaiva ślokasya vyavasthāvākye ime |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tv adhyāhāreṇa saṃbandhalakṣaṇā āhuḥ: akṛtamuṇḍānāṃ mṛtānāṃ ye sapiṇḍāḥ | 

	tatrottarapakṣaḥ samācārābhipretaḥ |

	smṛtyantare sadyaḥśaucam apy āmnātam | viṣayas tatraiva darśitaḥ: "ā dantajanmanaḥ sadyaḥ ā cūḍān naiśikī nirvṛttacūḍakānāṃ trirātram" iti || 5.66 ||

	**ūnadvivārṣikaṃ pretaṃ nidadhyur bāndhavā bahiḥ |**

**	alaṃkṛtya śucau bhūmāv asthisaṃcayanād ṛte || 5.67 ||**

ūne asaṃskṛtasya dve varṣe yasya jātasya gate, sa ucyate **ūnadvivārṣikaḥ** | taṃ **pretaṃ bāndhavā** **bahir** grāmaṃ **nidadhyur** bhūmau nikhātāyāṃ sthāpayeyuḥ | smṛtyantare "nikhanet" (YDh 3.1) iti paṭhyate | **alaṃkṛtya** pretālaṃkāraiḥ | ūnadvivarṣe 'pi śrūyamāṇo 'laṃkāraḥ samācārāt kṛtopanayanādāv api vijñeyaḥ | **śucau** yatrāsthīni bhūpradeśe na santi | asthisaṃcayarahitatvena yā śuddhā tatra nikhāya sthāpyaḥ | smaśāne kilāsthīni saṃcitāni bhavanti | ata etena[^170] vacanena tato 'nyatra nidhānam ucyate | na punas tādṛśasyāsthisaṃcayo na kartavya ity eva vākyārthaḥ | agnisaṃskārābhāvād eva tadaprāpteḥ || 5.67||

	**nāsya kāryo 'gnisaṃskāro na ca kāryodakakriyā |**

**	araṇya kāṣṭhavat tyaktvā kṣapeta tryaham eva tu || 5.68 ||**

**kāṣṭhavad** iti nirapekṣatām āha | śrāddham api na kartavyaṃ na codakam | **udakakriyā**niṣedhena śrāddhaniṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ aṅgāṅgibhāvāt | ataḥ samācāraprasiddhaḥ śrāddhaniṣedho liṅgena sādhayitavyaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> smṛtyantaradṛṣṭanikhananapratiṣedhārthaṃ varṇayanti | tataś ca vikalpaḥ | **kṣapeta** udāsyeta | śāstracoditaṃ vyāpāraṃ na kuryāt || 5.68 ||

	**nātrivarṣasya kartavyā bāndhavair udakakriyā |**

**	jātadantasya vā kuryur nāmni vāpi kṛte sati || 5.69 ||**

**ā trivarṣasyeti **ā tṛtīyād varṣāt pratiṣedhaḥ | na punaś caturvarṣādau | evamartham **evā**diśabdaṃ <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> paṭhanti: **nātrivarṣasya kartavyā** trivarṣāder iti | samācāraś caivam eva | **jātadantasya vā kuryuḥ** | udakakriyāsāhacaryād agnisaṃskāro 'bhyanujñāyate |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca vikalpe kāmacāraḥ | tatra kaḥ prayāsasādhyaṃ vittakṣayakaram anuṣṭhānapakṣam āśrayeta | vyarthas taddupadeśaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | sarvavilakṣaṇo 'yaṃ pitror adhikāraḥ | pretopakārārtham etat kriyate | naimittikatvād avaśyakartavyam ity etat prāg evoktam | tatrāvaśyakartavyatāpratiṣedho 'stītīha niścīyate | pretopakārārthatvam astīty abhyanujñānena jñāpyate | tatrākaraṇe nāsti vidhyatikramaḥ | pretopakāras tv anuṣṭhānād bhavatīti vidhipratiṣedhayor nāsāmañjasyam || 5.69 ||

	**sabrahmacāriṇy ekāham atīte kṣapaṇaṃ smṛtam |**

**	janmany ekodakānāṃ tu trirātrāc chuddhir iṣyate || 5.70 ||**

**sabrahmacārī** samānacarṇo 'ta **ekodakā** rūḍhyā āsapiṇḍebhyaḥ[^171] parigṛhyante | teṣām itaretaraṃ janmani sūtake trirātram | sadyaḥśaucam api smṛtyantarād udakadāyināṃ vikalpitaṃ draṣṭavyam || 5.70 ||

	**strīṇām asaṃskṛtānāṃ tu tryahāc chuddhyanti bāndhavāḥ |**

**	yathoktenaiva kalpena śuddhyanti tu sanābhayaḥ || 5.71 ||**

**asaṃskṛtā** yā vāṅmātreṇa pratigṛhītā na ca vivāhitās tāsāṃ maraṇe **bāndhavāḥ** patipakṣās trirātreṇa | **sanābhayas tu** sapiṇḍāḥ svapitṛpakṣā yathoktena kalpena "nirvṛttacauḍakānām"[^172] (cf. MDh 5.66) iti jāter adhikārāt trirātreṇa | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anyais tūkam</span> "sodaryā daśarātreṇa" iti | teṣāṃ cābhiprāyaḥ | aṣṭavarṣāyāḥ kanyāyā dānaṃ vihitam | adattāyāś ca nirvṛttacauḍakavyapadeśābhāvāt[^173] puṃsa ivopanītasya, tadānīṃ kalpāntarasyānāmnānād daśāha eva yuktaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anyais</span> tu paṭhitam "ahas tv adattakanyāsu bāleṣu ca viśodhanam" iti | tatra vyākhyātāraḥ pañcadaśābdadeśīyāpi yā hy adattā kanyā tiṣṭhet tadahar evāśaucam |[^174] mukhyam āmnānam atikramya kālakṣapaṇe pramāṇābhāvāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tatrocyate</span> | "bāleṣu ca" iti ko 'syārthaḥ | yāvatā uktam eva yogavibhāge "ā dantajanmanaḥ sadyaḥ" iti | na caitena tad bādhituṃ yuktam, sāmānyarūpatvād asya, tasya ca viśeṣavyavasthāpanarūpatvāt | ato 'yam ekāhaḥ pṛthag ukto 'pi ā cūḍād eva vyavatiṣṭhate, sāmānyasya viśeṣāpekṣatvāt | tasmād anārṣa evāyam ardhaślokaḥ pratipadyate: sparśaviṣayatayā neyaḥ | sparśapratiṣedho hi mṛtakasūtakayor bālasyāpi puṃvat prāptaḥ | tadartham etad uktaṃ syāt "ahas tv adattakanyāsu bāleṣu ca viśodhanam" iti | evaṃ ca viṣayasaptamyāśritā bhavati | sā ca yuktā kārakavibhaktitvāt | itarathā adhyāhṛtya bhāvalakṣaṇā saptamī vyākhyāyeta, "bāleṣu mṛteṣu jīvatāṃ śuddhiḥ" iti | na ca tadupasparśanād āśaucam etenaitat siddhyatīti | viṣayāntare tasya ca caritārthatvāt, bhūmau parivṛtatvāt, bhūmau parivṛtasya ca sparśanasaṃbhavāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">aviśeṣoktau</span> kuto viśeṣapratipattir iti cet | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tasyācamanakalpo</span> vidyata ity etat saṃnidhau tādṛśasyaiva[^175] sparśasya pratīyamānatvāt | tathā ca rajasvalāspṛṣṭino bālasya sparśanaṃ necchanti | athāsya viśeṣaṇaṃ syāt | tathā gautamena tad uktaṃ svasyāṃ smṛtau (cf. GDh 14.44) | yuktam evādhātum etasya | tasmād yuktaivādhānakālalakṣaṇā || 5.71 ||

	**akṣāralavaṇānnāḥ syur nimajjeyuś ca te tryaham |**

**	māṃsāśanaṃ ca nāśnīyuḥ śayīraṃś ca pṛthak kṣitau || 5.72 ||**

**kṣāralavaṇam**[^176] | yavakṣārādi kṣāram | lavaṇaṃ saindhavādi | tan na bhuñjīran | lavanaviseṣaṇaṃ vā kṣāragrahaṇaṃ tena saindhavasya pratiṣedhaḥ | nimajjanaṃ ca nadītaḍāgādāv atīrthasnānam[^177] aṅgaparigharṣaṇādivarjanam | **māṃsāśanaṃ** **ca** yāvad āśaucaṃ smṛtyantarāt pratiṣidhyate | evaṃ paṭhyate "na striyam upeyur na mārjayeyur na māṃsam aśnīyuḥ" | gṛhyakāras tu "tryaham anaśnanta āsīran krītotpannena vā varteran" (cf. ĀśG 4.4.15) ity āha | **śayīraṃś ca** sthaṇḍile parasaṅgavarjam | sūtake 'pi brahmacaryaṃ smṛtyantare pradarśitam || 5.72 ||

	**saṃnidhāv eṣa vai kalpaḥ śāvāśaucasya kīrtitaḥ |**

**	asaṃnidhāv ayaṃ jñeyo vidhiḥ saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ || 5.73 ||**

**saṃnidhau** yatrāsau mṛtas tatra tat saṃnidhīyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu prayāṇakāle ye saṃnihitās teṣām evāyaṃ vidhir ity āhuḥ | **saṃbandhinaḥ** samānodakāḥ | **bāndhavāḥ** sapiṇḍāḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu grāmāntare nagarāntare 'vasthānam asaṃnidhānaṃ manyante, || 5.73 ||

_teṣāṃ ca,_

	**vigataṃ tu videśasthaṃ śṛṇuyād yo hy anirdaśam |**

**	yac cheṣaṃ daśarātrasya tāvad evāśucir bhavet || 5.74 ||**

**videśo**[^178] grāmāntarādiḥ pūrvavat | **vigataṃ** mṛtam | **anirdaśam** | upalakṣaṇam etat | yasya ya āśaucakālas taccheṣaṃ tasyāśaucam | punar **daśarātra**grahaṇaṃ ślokapūraṇārtham | utpattyapekṣayā janmamaraṇayor āśaucakālavikalpenāvaśyam apekṣyam[^179] | yadā sūtakādyutpannaṃ tadā prabhṛti daśāhādi kalpaḥ, na yadā[^180] sapiṇḍair jñātam iti | ataś ca yadātithinā jñātaṃ sūtakādi na tu gṛhasthena tadāpy abhojyam annam | tathaivotpattinimittamātram idam ubhayatreti | daśāham āśaucināṃ tata ūrdhvam, trirātraikāhāśaucinā tu sacailasnānajā sadyaḥ śuciḥ || 5.74 ||

	**atikrānte daśāhe ca trirātram aśucir bhavet |**

**	saṃvatsare vyatīte tu spṛṣṭvaivāpo viśuddhyati || 5.75 ||**

yasya yaḥ kṛta āśaucakālo daśāhādis tasya tadūrdhvaṃ trirātram | yasya tu tryahaikāhādis tasya tata ūrdhvaṃ savāsasaḥ snānamātram eva | tathā cottaratra vakṣyati "savāsāḥ" (MDh 5.76) ityādi | **saṃvatsare atīte** atikrānte **spṛṣṭvaivāpaḥ** snātvā śudhyed ity arthaḥ | "hastena ca sapādena" ityādivacanāt, sarvāṅgasparśanaṃ pratīyate, tac ca snānam eva || 5.75 ||

	**nirdaśaṃ jñātimaraṇaṃ śrutvā putrasya janma ca |**

**	savāsā jalam āplutya śuddho bhavati mānavaḥ || 5.76 ||**

samānodakānām ayaṃ vidhiḥ | tryahaikāhapakṣe ca sapiṇḍānām api | **savāsā** vāsasā sahitaḥ | **jalam āplutya** snātvety arthaḥ || 5.76 ||

	**bāle deśāntarasthe ca pṛthakpiṇḍe ca saṃsthite |**

**	savāsā jalam āplutya sadya eva viśudhyati || 5.77 ||**

**bāle** 'dantajāte sūnau | **deśāntarasthe** **pṛthakpiṇḍe ca saṃsthite**, ity ekārthāni padāni | **pṛthakpiṇḍaḥ** samānodaka iti yāvat | tasmin **deśāntarasthe saṃsthite** sadyaḥ śuddhiḥ | saṃnidhau "tryahāt tūdakadāyinaḥ" (MDh 5.63) ity uktam || 5.77 ||

	**antardaśāhe cet syātāṃ punar maraṇajanmanī |**

**	tāvat syād aśucir vipro yāvat tat syād anirdaśam || 6.78 ||**

atrāpi **daśāha**graṇam āśaucakālopalakṣaṇārtham | yasya ya āśaucakālas tasminn anivṛtte yadi punar anyad āśaucanimittam utpadyate tadā pūrvaśeṣeṇaiva śuddhir na tv antarā nipatitaṃ yat tadīyād ahnaḥ prabhṛti daśāhādigaṇanā kartavyā | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "tac ced antaḥ punar āpatet taccheṣeṇa śuddhyeyuḥ" iti (GDh 14.6) | **maraṇajanmanī** iti samāse yatnam antareṇa kramāpratipatter vyantareṇāpy upanipātaprāptau[^181] samācārāt samānajātīya eveti draṣṭavyam | **punaḥ**śabdaś ca samānajātīyāpekṣayā samarthataro bhavati | **vipra**grahaṇam apy āśaucinām upalakṣaṇārtham | smṛtyantare tu vihitam: "rātriśeṣe dvābhyām, prabhāte tisṛbhiḥ" (GDh 14.7–8) iti | "etasya brāhmaṇasya pretasparśe daśarātram āśaucam" iti prakṛtya "na ced antarā mriyeta jāyeta vā śiṣṭair eva divasaiḥ śuddhyeta" itīyaṃ smṛtiḥ samānajātīyāsamānajātīyabhedaṃ nānumanyate || 5.78 ||

	**trirātram āhur āśaucam ācārye saṃsthite sati |**

**	tasya putre ca patnyāṃ ca divārātram iti sthitiḥ || 5.79 ||**

**ācārya** upanetā | tasmin **saṃsthite** **trirātraṃ** śiṣyasya | **tasya** ācāryasya **putre patnyāṃ ca** saṃsthitāyām **ahorātram** || 5.79 ||

	**śrotriye tūpasaṃpanne trirātram aśucir bhavet |**

**	mātule pakṣiṇīṃ rātriṃ śiṣartvigbāndhaveṣu ca || 5.80 ||**

vedaśākhādhyāyī **śrotriyaḥ** | **upasaṃpannaḥ** maitryā prayojanena vā kenacit saṃgataḥ śīlena yukto vā | pūrvaṃ tu sabrahmacāriṇy ekāham agṛhītavede dṛṣṭam (MDh 5.70) | abhidhānakośe tu upasaṃpanno mṛtaparyāyaḥ | bahukālatvād āśaucasya pūrvaiva vyākhyā jyāyasī | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> "**śrotriye mātule trirātram**" ity eva saṃbandhanti, **pakṣiṇīṃ rātrim** iti śiṣyādibhiḥ | 

	**bāndhavāḥ** śyālakamātṛṣvasreyādayaḥ[^182] | yadā tu "**mātule pakṣiṇīm**" iti saṃbandhas, tadā mātule[^183] bāndhavatvād eva siddhā pakṣiṇī | punarvacanaṃ nityārtham | tenānyeṣu bāndhaveṣu yathākāmam || 5.80 ||

	**prete rājani sajyotir yasya syād viṣaye sthitaḥ |**

**	aśrotriye tv ahaḥ kṛtsnam anūcāne tathā gurau || 5.81 ||**

**rāja**śabdo 'yam abhiṣekādiguṇayogini varṇamātre lakṣaṇayā vartate | yata āha **yasya syād viṣaye sthitaḥ** | jātiviśeṣāvacchinnaviṣayeśvaravacanatve lakṣaṇā, na ca śabdārthaḥ | **sajyotiḥ** | saha jyotiṣā vartate | divā prete divaiva, rātrau tu tan nāsti | evaṃ rātrau rātrir eva nāhaḥ | idam eva jñāpakam anyatra rātrigrahaṇe 'hargrahaṇe 'py ahorātrapratipatteḥ[^184] | yathā "rātribhir māsatulyābhiḥ" (MDh 5.65), "tryaham ekāham" (MDh 5.59) iti | "ahnā caikena" (MDh 5.63) ity atra tu rātrigrahaṇaṃ pādapūraṇārtham | rātrāv agnir **jyotiḥ** | evaṃ hy agnihotrabrāhmaṇe "agninā vai tejasā tejasviny ādityena tejasā na[^185] bhavati" (cf. AitB 25.4) |

	**aśrotriye** avedādhyāyini, **anūcāne** kṛtsnam ahaḥ | rātrau na bhavaty eva, utpanne 'pi rātrau nimitte | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar aśrotriye 'nūcāne | evaṃ hi smaryate "pravacane sāṅge 'dhītīti" |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyaṃ</span> pravaktāpy anūcāna ucyate | tenaivaṃ kathaṃcid aṅgādigranthārthānyaḥ pravakti tasminn ayam ahar vidhiḥ | upasaṃpanne ca[^186] gurau pūjyatvena mukhye, ācārye vā vidhyantarabhāvāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit tu</span> **aśrotriye tv** ity atra nañaṃ saṃbadhnanti | iha nañaḥ praśleṣeṇa yo 'nyeṣām upādhyāyas tasya ca na kaścit tatremaṃ vidhim ācakṣate || 5.81 ||

	**śuddhyed vipro daśāhena dvādaśāhena bhūmipaḥ |**

**	vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati || 5.82 ||**

kṣatriyādīnāṃ prāguktavṛttādyapekṣas tryahacaturahādikalpavyāvṛttyartham idam | brāhmaṇe daśāhas tv anūdyata eva | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra tv</span> idaṃ vācyam:[^187] kena kṣatriyādīnāṃ dvādaśāhena niyatakālāprāptir yena kalpāntaravyāvṛttyarthatāvagamyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">iyam</span> eva hy eṣām iyatkālasya prāpakam | saty asmiṃs tatra daśāho 'yam āśaucakālas tadupalakṣaṇārtho vijñāyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>[^188]<span style="text-decoration:underline;"> ca</span> saty apy asmiṃs tasyopalakṣaṇārthatā | saty api cāturvarṇyādhikāre yasyaiva daśāha uktas tasyaivetare kalpā iti | smṛtyantare ca brāhmaṇavivakṣayaivoktam: "ekāhād brāhmaṇasya syāt svādhyāyaḥ" ityādi | teṣāṃ tu smṛtyantare yāni kalpāntarāṇy āmnātāni tāni[^189] vikalpyante[^190] | ekādaśe āśaucakālaḥ kaścid vivaraṇakāra āha:  "śuddhyed vipro daśāhena" iti | atrāhargrahaṇaṃ vivakṣitam, tena daśamyāṃ rātrau nāsty āśaucam | tataḥ pūrvedyur nimantraṇādi yuktam | agniṃ cādhāsyataḥ paurvāhṇikajāgaraṇādināśauca upakrānto[^191] bhaviṣyati | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam</span> | aharvivakṣāyām ādyāsv api rātriṣu na syād āśaucam | atha "daśāhaṃ śāvam" (MDh 5.59) iti etasmāt tatra bhaviṣyati | atrāvivakṣāyāṃ kiṃ pramāṇam | tasmād ahaḥśabdo 'yam ahorātravacana iti pradarśitam | tathā ca pūrvaśloke "ahaḥ kṛtsnam" (MDh 5.81) iti rātrinivṛttyarthaṃ kṛtsnagrahaṇam || 5.82 ||

	**na vardhayed aghāhāni paratyūhen nāgniṣu kriyāḥ |**

**	na ca tat karma kurvāṇaḥ sanābhyo 'py aśucir bhavet || 5.83 ||**

yasyaiṣā buddhiḥ: "ya uktās tryahādayaḥ kalpās tulyaṃ daśāhena vikalpyante, na vṛttādivyavasthayeti, tataś ciratarakālam anyasya saṃbhave kim ity ekāhapakṣaṃ nityasvādhyāyākleśakaraṃ[^192] pratipatsye, daśāham apāśrayāmi niṣkarmasukham āsiṣye" iti — taṃ prati sauhārddena sā vyavasthā spaṣṭīkriyate | naite tulyā api tu vyavasthitā eva | vyavasthā ca prāg darśitā | anyathā yasyāśaucakālo vihitas tasya tataḥ kālāvadhikasya kuto vṛddhiprāptiḥ, yenaivam arthvat syāt | vispaṣṭārthatve ko doṣaḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tv</span> āhur atīteṣv apy ahaḥsu yāvat snānādikriyā na kṛtā tāvan naiva śuddhiḥ | "vipraḥ śudhyaty apaḥ" (MDh 5.98) ityādi vakṣyati | tatrāśucitvād ananuṣṭhānena na duṣyāmīti[^193] snānādiṣu śuddhaye na pravartate | tatraivam ucyate "**na vardhayet**" nātīteṣv ahaḥsu bāhyāśauce vilambitavyam | 

	ye tv ahaḥśabdo daśamasyāhno yā rātris tasyām āśaucaṃ na bhavatīti, te na samyaṅ manyata ity uktam | tathā ca gautamaḥ āśaucamadhya āśaucāntara utpanne taccheṣeṇa śuddhiḥ ity uktvā (GDh 14.6), ekasyāṃ rātrau śeṣāyāṃ tayaiva śuddhiṃ manyamāna āha "rātriśeṣe dvābhyām" (GDh 14.7) iti |

	**pratyūhen nāgniṣū kriyāḥ** | aśucitvāt sarvaśrautasmārtakriyānivṛttau prāptāyām idam ucyate | agniṣu yāḥ kriyāḥ sāyaṃhomādyās tā na pratyūhen na pratyasyet | pratyūho nirhāsa ananuṣṭhānam | na ca svayaṃ kuryād yata āha **na ca tatkarma kurvāṇaḥ sanābhyo 'pīti** | sanābhyo 'pi nāśuciḥ syāt kiṃ punar anyaḥ | tathā gṛhyam: "nityāni nivarteran vaitānavarjaṃ śālāgnau caike" ity uktvā āha "anya etāni kuryuḥ" (PārG 3.1032–34) iti | na ca yad agnyādhānaṃ homamātram eva kriyate, kiṃ tarhi sāṅgaprayogaḥ, tatraiva kartur narasya saṃbhavāt pradhānahomasya tu dravyatyāgarūpatvāt svayaṃkartṛtaiva | ato homavaiśvadevadarśapūrṇamāsādyā nivartante | anyeṣāṃ tu japasaṃdhyopāsanādīnāṃ nivṛttir na darśitā | tāni ca nityāni | ato anyeṣām evābhyanujñānaṃ yataḥ smṛtyantare pratiṣiddham: "homaḥ svādhyāyaś ca nivartate" (ViPu 3.13.18) iti | ato nityakāṃyabhedena vyavasthā | kāmyaṃ tu naiva kartavyam aśucitvād adhikārāpagamāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca nityeṣv api naivāśucer adhikāraḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">na ca</span> śaucam aṅgam | yadi viguṇaṃ nityam anuṣṭhīyate, na kāmyam ity ucyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">athāsmād</span> vacanād bhavati |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | iha yad api mānaṃ tad asyānya etāni kuryur iti parakartṛtvam abhyanujñāyate | tac ca viguṇatvān nityeṣūpapadyate na kāmyeṣu | 

	vaiśvadeve tu vivadante | smṛtyantaraṃ codāharanti |

	homaṃ tatra na kurvīta śuṣkadhānyaphalair api |

	evaṃ yajñavidhānaṃ tu na kuryān mṛtyujanmanoḥ ||

ataḥ saṃdhyāhomau darśapūrṇamāsau sāṃvatsarikaṃ cāśvayujyādi kartavyam | upākaraṇaṃ tu nakṣatrāśrayam eva, na paurṇamāsyāśrayam || 5.83 ||

	**divākīrtim udakyāṃ ca patitaṃ sūtikāṃ tathā |**

**	śavaṃ tatspṛṣṭinaṃ caiva spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati || 5.84 ||**

**divākīrtiś** cāṇḍālaḥ, atyantāśucisāhacaryād bhārate ca prayogadarśanān mārjāramūṣikasaṃvāde |

	tasminn api ca kāle 'bhūd divākīrtir bhayārditaḥ | iti | (MBh 12.136.106)

na nāpitaḥ, tasya spṛśyatvāt bhojyānnatvāc ca | yat tu śmaśrukarmaṇi tasyedaṃ snānam ity āhus tad api siddhatvād avācyam | avaśyaṃ[^194] śmaśrukarmāṇi kārayato romāṇi gātrāṇi spṛśanti, tāni śarīrāc cyutāny aśuddhānīti siddhaṃ snānam | **tatspṛṣṭinaṃ** tasya spṛṣṭaṃ tatspṛtam, tad asyāstīti **tatspṛṣṭī** | yenaite spṛṣṭās tad api snānam eva | 

	iha sarvasyāpratyāsatteḥ **tatspṛṣṭinam** ity anena saṃbandhaḥ śavasyaiva <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> āhur na divākirtyādīnām | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> ekavākyopanipātād ante śrutatvāt sarveṣāṃ buddhau saṃnidhānāt tacchabdena[^195] sarvanāmnā parāmarśa iti | atra hi śavaparyantānāṃ dvandvaṃ kṛtvā spṛṣṭīty anena saṃbandhaḥ | tatra tatspṛṣṭīti samāsārthasya buddhau saṃnihitatvāt tacchabdenāvamarśaḥ | na hi kevalasya śavasya spṛṣṭipadena[^196] saṃbandho lakṣyate, patitādibhir itaretarayuktatvāt[^197] | kiṃ tu kevalasya padāntasaṃbandhaḥ | dvandve hy ekaikaḥ śabdaḥ sarvārthābhidhāyī | tataḥ sarve pratyāsannaḥ | athāpi śavaspṛṣṭiśabdasya tatspṛṣṭipadena saṃbandhaṃ kṛtvā tato 'nyair abhisaṃbandhaḥ | tathā sati patitādīnāṃ spṛṣṭipadena saṃbandho na syāt | tasmāt samācārata eva nirṇayaḥ || 5.84 ||

	**ācamya prayato nityaṃ japed aśucidarśane |**

**	saurān mantrān yathotsāhaṃ pāvamānīś ca śaktataḥ || 5.85 ||**

aśucayaḥ saṃnidhānāt pūrvoktā eva | sūryadaivatyā mantrāḥ **saurāḥ** "ud u tyaṃ jātavedasam" (RV 1.50.1) ityādayaḥ | **pāvamāṇyaḥ** dāśatayīṣu navame maṇḍale 'dhītāḥ "svādiṣṭayā" ityādyāḥ (RV 9.1.1) | **yathotsāhaṃ śaktita** iti ca eka evārthaḥ | vṛttavaśāc chabdadvayaṃ paṭhitam | bahuvacananirdeśāt tritvasaṃkhyāvaśyaṃ kartavyā | paratas tu yadi gurutarakāryātyayo na bhavati tadā kartavya eva japaḥ | mantragrahaṇāt pāvamānīr iti ca ṛcām upādānād asamāpte 'pi sūkte tribhya ūrdhvaṃ bhavaty eva śuddhiḥ | śvāpy atra prakṣeptavyaḥ | so 'py aśucir eva | paṭhitaṃ ca gautamīye 'sminn eva varge: "śunaś ca | yad upahanyād ity eke" iti (GDh 14.32–33) | **prayataḥ** ananyamanā mantradevatādidhyānaparaḥ | atha vā **prayato** devatādipūjāpravṛtto yadā paśyet tadaiva kuryān nānyadeti || 5.85 ||

	**nāraṃ spṛṣṭvāsti sasnehaṃ snātvā vipro viśudhyati |**

**	ācamyaiva tu niḥsnehaṃ gām ālabhyārkam īkṣya vā || 5.86 ||**

naro manuṣyas tasyedam **nāram** | **sasnehaṃ** māṃsamajjādigdham | gor ālaṃbhanaṃ sparśaḥ | arkadarśanagavālambau vikalpyete[^198] || 5.86 ||

	**ādiṣṭī nodakaṃ kuryād ā vratasya samāpanāt |**

**	samāpte tūdakaṃ kṛtvā trirātreṇaiva śudhyati || 5.87 ||**

ādeśa ādiṣṭam | vratādeśanasaṃbandhād rūḍhirūpeṇa brahmacāry ucyate | tasya brahmacaryāśramasthasya sato ye sapiṇḍāḥ pramīyante teṣām ayam aniṣṭodakadānapratiṣedhaḥ[^199] | prākpramītānāṃ tu vihitam anvāhikaṃ kuryād devapitṛtarpaṇam iti | **ā vratasyeti** ā samāvartanād ity arthaḥ | na punar āntarālikasāhasikād ity arthaḥ | vratacaraṇasamāpteḥ samāvṛttaḥ sa sarveṣām ekaikasyodakaṃ kṛtvaikasminn ahani, trirātram āśaucaṃ kuryāt | mātus tūdakadānaṃ vratino 'pīṣyate | na ca vratalopaḥ | smṛtyantaram udāharanti: aparādhya ādiṣṭī nodaka iti || 5.87 ||

	**vṛthāsaṃkarajānāṃ pravrajyāsu ca niṣṭhatām |**

**	ātmanas tyāgināṃ caiva nivartetodakakriyā || 5.88 ||**

**jāta**śabdaḥ pratyakem abhisaṃbadhyate | **vṛthajāto** yo na devān arcayati na pitṝn na manuṣyān iti | saty adhikāre 'nāśramī, hutāhutaparityaktaḥ, "saṃvatsaram anāśramī bhūtvā" ityādi cirakālāvasthāne mahādoṣaśravaṇāt | brahmacāriparivrājakābhyām anyasya parapākaratitvam | ātmārthas tu pāko niṣiddhaḥ | **saṃkarajātā** itaretarajātivyatikareṇa pratilomā āyogavādayaḥ | ninditatvād vṛthājātasāhacaryeṇa | anulomās tu saty api saṃkīrṇayonitve mātṛjātīyatvād adhikāritvāc ca neha gṛhyante | na cānulomeṣu saṃkīrṇayonivyavahāraḥ | "saṃkīrṇayonayas tv etāḥ pratilomānulomajāḥ" (MDh 10.25) iti | aniyuktā sutādayayaś cānekapuruṣasaṃsargajāḥ, veśyājātāś ca | pārastraiṇeyās tu asatyanekapuruṣasaṃsargeṇa saṃkarajātāḥ |

	ayaṃ ca sapiṇḍānāṃ niṣedhaḥ, na tatputrāṇām iti <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> | ātmatyāgināṃ tu putrāṇām api | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad</span> ayuktam[^200] aviśeṣaśravaṇāt |

	**pravrajyāsu** bāhyāsu bhagālavaraktapaṭādyāsv anadhikārād bahuvacananirdeśāt,[^201] vratādidarśanabhedena bāhyāḥ | **ātmanas tyāgināṃ** puruṣāṇām āyuṣo 'kṣaye svecchayā śarīraṃ tyajanti | vṛddhānām acikitsyamahāvyādhīnāṃ ca bhiṣakpratyakhātānām iṣyata eva | yathoktam |

	vṛddhaḥ śaucasmṛter luptasya pratyākhyātabhiṣakkriyaḥ |

	ātmānaṃ ghātayed yas tu bhṛgvagnyanaśanāmbubhiḥ ||

	tasya trirātram āśaucaṃ dvitīye tv astisaṃcayaḥ |

	tṛtīye tūdakaṃ kṛtvā caturthe śrāddham ācaret || iti |

kuṣṭyādes tu vyādhigṛhītasya iṣyata eva | yathoktaṃ "luptaceṣṭasya" | gṛhasthāvasthāyām api,

	mahāprasthānagamanā vṛthā necchanti jīvitum |

luptaceṣṭaś cocyate yaḥ śaucādiṣv asamarthaḥ saṃdhyopāsanādiṣu ca | "aparikṣīṇaśarīro vā sādayed yas tv ātmānam aluptaceṣṭo vā" | atas tadviparītasyānujñānaṃ bhavati | smṛtyantareṣv anyeṣām apy udakakriyāniṣedho vihitaḥ | yathoktam |

	rājabhir nihatānāṃ ca śṛṅgidaṃṣṭrisarīsṛpaiḥ |

	ātmanas tyāgināṃ caiva śrāddham eṣāṃ na kalpayet ||

	udakaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ ca pretebhyo yac ca dīyate |

	nopatiṣṭhanti tat sarvam antarikṣe vinaśyati ||

	nārāyaṇabaliḥ kāryo lokagarhābhayān naraiḥ |

	tasmād ebhyo 'pi dātavyam annam eva sadakṣiṇam ||

tathānyatra |

	caṇḍālād udakāt sarpād brāhmaṇād vaidyutād api |

	daṃṣṭribhyaś ca paśubhyaś ca maraṇam pākakarmaṇām ||

tathā coktam |

	nṛṇāṃ caivāgnidānāṃ ca snānālaṃkārakāriṇām |

	taptakṛcchradvaye śuddhir aśrupāte 'nuyāyinām ||

	tenoddiṣṭaṃ na caivanyaiḥ kāryam asyaurdhvadehikam |

	na ca nāmāpi kartavyaṃ tadvaṃśasya tadīyakam ||

	atyantanarakasthasya tasya pāpīyaso 'dhikam |

	kāraṇaṃ kīrtanaṃ nāma sarvaṃ caiva bhayāvaham ||

	saṃvartena āsv eva kriyāsu sāntapanam āmnātam, parāśareṇa taptakṛcchram, vasiṣṭhena taptakṛccharasahitaṃ cāndrāyaṇam | tatrāpūrvādiviśeṣā upekṣyāḥ | 

	yad uktam "caṇḍālad udakāt" ityādy upakramya "maraṇaṃ pāpakarmaṇām" iti, tatredaṃ saṃdihyate | kiṃ yaś cāṇḍāladir buddhipūrvam ātmānaṃ ghātayati tasyāyaṃ vidhir aurdhvadehikākaraṇam, tatkaraṇe ca prāyaścittam, uta pramādahastasyānicchata iti | kutaḥ saṃdehaḥ | iha gautamena "prāyānāśakaśastrāgniviṣodakodbandhanaprapatanaiś cecchatām[^202]" ity uktam (GDh 14.12) | iha cāviśeṣeṇa śrutam "caṇḍālād udakāt" iti | tatra smṛtyantareṇaikaśāstratvād "udakād" ity atra tāvad avaśyam "icchatām" iti saṃbadhyate | sāhacaryād anyatrāpi tathaivety āśaṅkā jāyate | kiṃ ca "pāpakarmaṇām" iti śrūyate | pāpaṃ ca karma pratiṣiddham | atra pratiṣiddhaṃ yo 'nutiṣṭhati sa pāpakarmety upapadyate | anuṣṭhātṛtvaṃ ca svavyāpāreṇa paraprayoktṛtayā ca | tatra na vaidyutadaṃṣṭriśṛṅgyādayaḥ | te ca na prayujyante | nāpi te śvabhrodakakhaḍgādisthānīyāḥ | yena tadupādānenātmānaṃ ghnan svatantraḥ kartā syāt | kiṃ tarhi yasyedṛśaṃ maraṇam upanataṃ sa pūrvajanmani kṛtapāpaka iti śāstreṇa jñāpyate | yathā śyāvadantaprabhṛtayaḥ | tatrāpi kim etena jñāpitena | aṅgahīnādīnāṃ pūrvapāpasaṃbandhitvaṃ jñāpyate | prāyaścittam anuṣṭheyaṃ yathā vasiṣṭhenoktam | kasyacit kṛcchradvayacaraṇaṃ kasyacid abhyadhikam api | iha mṛtyunā saṃbandhikārasyāpahṛtatvān nārtho 'nena | yadi vāsau kṛtapātaka ity avasīyate | tena saha yena kenacit[^203] yaunamaukhasrauvāḥ saṃbandhāḥ kṛtāḥ so 'pi pāpakārī syāt | na caivaṃ śiṣṭānām ācāraḥ | na hi tādṛśena saṃbandhaṃ kṛtavantaḥ kenacid vicikitsyante | prāyaścittaṃ nācaranti | ata icchatām anumīyate |

	ye tu "gobrāhmaṇahatānām" iti smṛtyantare paṭhitvā "ātmanas tyāginām" iti pṛthak paṭhanti tena viśeṣapakṣaḥ pratibhāti | 

	ataḥ saṃśayaḥ kiṃ punar atra yuktam | 

	icchatām iti | kutaḥ | pāpakarmavacanāt | svecchayā yaś cātmavyāpattihetau vyāpāre pravartate tena "tasmād u ha na purāyuṣaḥ svaḥ kāmī preyāt" (ŚB 10.2.6.7) iti śāstram atikrāntaṃ bhavati | sa ca yuktaḥ pāpakarmeti vyapadeṣṭum |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> coktaṃ na hi te khaḍgādisthānīyāḥ, yenecchayā vadhopapattiḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | yaḥ pramādaṃ na rakṣati tena tat kṛtam eveti | tena yaś cāṇḍāladasyubhūyiṣṭhe 'raṇya ekākī gacchati, tasya yady api caṇḍālā māṃ ghnantv itīcchā na bhavati, tathāpi tatsamarthācareṇena pramādasyāparihṛtatvād bhavaty eva śāstrātikramaḥ | evaṃ yo bāhubhyāṃ nadīṃ tarati saṃdigdhāṃ vā nāvam adhirohaty akuśalakarṇadhārādhiṣṭhitām, evaṃ tasya vyāpadyamānasya vegakṣayeṇa nauparivartanādinā vā yuktaiva pāpakāritā | tathā cāgādhatāṃ daṇḍādinā grāhamakarasaṃgaṃ cājñātvā[^204] snātāro yady apahriyeran na duṣyeyuḥ | evaṃ yas tu dṛḍhabandhanāṃ tanvaritrāṃ tariṃ tīvrāmbhasi kuśalāvahitasamarthaprerakapreryamāṇām adhirūḍhaḥ sahasotpatite javini pavane cakravātena picchalam avāptavān plavavyāptyā mriyeta na[^205] śāstram atikramet | evaṃ sarpopahataṃ deśaṃ ca apariharan daṣṭo vyāpadyeta pratyaveyād eva, nānyathā | evaṃ tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāṃ gāṃ hastinaṃ vā dṛṣṭvā dūram anapakrāmato hanyamānasya yukto 'trikramaḥ | evam araṇye varṣāsūccarantīṣu vidyutsu grāmanagaryor apraveśe duṣṭataiva | grāmasthasyopari kathaṃcid vidyutpātaḥ syāt tadā na kiṃcid aparādhyati | ato yuktam idṛśaṃ yathāvihitakriyākaraṇam | 

	tatra codakakriyāniṣedhaḥ sarvaurdhvadehikapradarśanārthaḥ, smṛtyantare 'syodāhṛtatvāt || 5.88 ||

	**pāṣaṇḍam āśritānāṃ ca carantīnāṃ ca kāmataḥ |**

**	garbhabhartṛdruhāṃ caiva surāpīnāṃ ca yoṣitām || 5.89 ||**

śāstraparityāgena bāhyadarśanāśrayaṃ naraśiraḥkapālaraktāmbarādidhāraṇaṃ **pāṣaṇḍam**, **tadāśritāḥ** kṛtatalliṅgparigrahāḥ taddarśanavaśavartinyaḥ | **carantīnāṃ ca kāmataḥ** | tadācārakulasthitityāgenecchāmātrānuvṛttyaikānekaparapuruṣasaṃprayogaḥ[^206] kāmacāraḥ | **bhartur** viṣagarādidānena **garbhasya** ca pātanaṃ **drohaḥ** | **surāpyaḥ** yathāpratiṣedhaṃ pratiṣiddhāyāḥ pātena |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra kaścid</span> āha: "brāhmaṇo na pibet surām" iti saty api jātyarthāviśeṣe liṅgāt puṃsa eva brāhmaṇasya pratiṣedho na striyā iti | yady api strīpuṃsayor ekā jātis tathāpi strītvapuṃstvaliṅge bhidyete | iha ca brāhmaṇa iti puṃlliṅgasya śabdasya śravaṇād aśrutāyāḥ kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ | yathā "brāhmaṇī pāyayet putrārtham" iti na puṃsaḥ pāyayed iti, tadvat puṃlligaśrutau na striya upādīyante | yatra[^207] kvacil liṅgaṃ na vivakṣyate, yatha "brāhmaṇo na hantavyaḥ" iti striyā api pratiṣedho vijñāyate, tatra dvitīyayā śrutyā brāhmaṇasyepsitatamatvāt prādhānyam | na ca pradhāne prātipadikārthavyatirekeṇānyaliṅgasaṃkhyādi vivakṣyate | yathā "grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭi" iti naikasya saṃmārgaḥ | iha punar "brāhmaṇena surā na peyā" iti kartṛtayā sādhanabhāvena kriyāṃ prati nirdeśāt "brāhmaṇo na pibet surām" ity ākhyātābhihite 'pi tadarthānām[^208] api vṛtteḥ prātipadikārthopapattyā prathamāpi tṛtīyānuguṇyeti guṇībhāvaḥ,[^209] guṇe ca sarvaṃ śrutaṃ vivakṣyate | yathā "paśunā yajeta" iti pumān paśur ālabhyate ekaś ca | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atrocyate</span> | nātra dvitīyātṛtīye guṇapradhānabhāvenāvivakṣāvivakṣayoḥ kāraṇam, kiṃ tarhi prāptyaprāptī | yad aprāptaṃ vidhiviṣayatayopapadyate[^210] tad vivakṣyate, ananyaparaśabdāvagamyatvāt | yat tv anyato 'vagatam arthāntaraṃ vidhyartham upādīyate, tad yādṛśam eva pramāṇāntarāvagataṃ tādṛśam eva vidheyakāryāntarasaṃbandhitayā śabdena pratipādyate | "brāhmaṇo na hantavyaḥ" ity atra vākye vidhiḥ pratiṣedha eva paryavasyati, yad anyat tad anyato 'vagatam | prātipadikārthavivakṣā tu śrutyānarthakyaprasaṅgāt | liṅgasaṃkhyādes tu pratyayārthasya nāntarīyakatvenāpy upādānasaṃbhavād vivakṣāvivakṣe ucyete | tatreha na brāhmaṇādibhiḥ puruṣo vidhinā pravartyaḥ, taddveṣāt[^211] svataḥ pravṛtteḥ, tat sarvasya cātra svayaṃ prasaṅgāt | na hy avidhīyamānaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kathaṃcid anvetum alam | anyataḥ prāptyabhāvāt, akārakatvād akārakaviśeṣaṇatvāt svabhāvānupraveśenāpi saṃbandhaṃ na[^212] labhyate | tasmād asyānvayasiddhyarthaṃ viṣayabhāva eṣitavyaḥ | tasmiṃś ca vidhinā viṣayīkṛtena bhāvārtho viṣayatayāpekṣyate | bhāvārthaś ca pratiṣedhena viṣayāṃśasya gṛhītatvāt tataḥ pracyuto laukikyā[^213] ca pravṛttyā siddhānuṣṭhāna ātmavidhisiddhyartham anupreveśam apy akāṃkṣann adhikāramātrasāpekṣavidhau pramāṇāntarataḥ pratipannahananakartṛbhāvasya puṃso 'dhikāratāṃ pratipādayaṃs tadviśeṣaṇadvāreṇānvayaṃ pratipadyata ity upapannam anvitābhidhānam | tena bhāvārthasya saviśeṣaṇasyāvidheyatvāl laukikī pravṛttir abhyupetavyā | asti ca rāgalakṣaṇā pravṛttir na tasyā liṅgasaṃkhyāniyamo 'sti, dveṣād vā | tasmād avidheyārthaśabdo 'vagatārthaparatvād abhidhānaśaktim[^214] utsṛjya pramāṇāntarato yathāvadhṛtasvarūpam arthaṃ lakṣayati | tatra liṅgasaṃkhyayos tātparyataḥ śabdenānabhidhānāt kuto vivakṣā | kevalaṃ prātipadikanirdeśārthaṃ yena kenacid vacanena nirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ, na kevalā prakṛtiḥ prayoktavyeti tadarthaṃ liṅgasaṃkhyayor upādānam |

	ata iyam atrāvagatiḥ | hanane 'dhyavasitakartṛbhāvaḥ sa nañarthe niyujyate | ataḥ pratiṣedhavākye dvitīyāśrutir avivakṣāyām atantram[^215] | yatrāpi[^216] hi tṛtīyā śrūyate prathamā vā, "brāhmaṇena na pātavyā," "brāhmaṇo na pibet" iti tatrāpi tadarthaś cānyataḥ prāpter avidheyatvād anūdyate | yādhikāraviśeṣaṇatvenaiva saṃbaddhā tatra te[^217] dvitīyāviśiṣṭe prathamātṛtīye | satyām api ca dvitīyāśrutau yad aprāptaṃ tadvidheyatvād vivakṣyate yathā "bhāryām upagacchet" "apatyam utpādayet" iti | na hi laukiko bhāryārthaḥ, upayamanenaiva tatsiddheḥ | 

	nāpi vākyāntare vidhinā kvacid upātto yena yathāvagamam uddiśyeta yathā "āśvinaṃ gṛhṇāti" (TB 2.6.1.5), "maitrāvaruṇaṃ gṛhṇāti" (TS 6.4.8), "daśaitān adhvaryur gṛhṇāti" (ŚāṅB 14.2) iti saṃkhyāviśiṣṭā eva grahā upādīyante | ato nirjñātasaṃkhyatvāt saṃmārgavidhau yathāsaṃkhyāvagamaṃ nirdiśyate | atra punar vākyāntarābhāvād asyaivotpattivākyatvāc chrutasaṃkhyāparityāge pramāṇābhāvān nirapekṣābhidhānaśaktisamarpitasyaikasya parityāgaḥ puruṣabuddhiprabhava eva syāt | evaṃ "paśunā yajeta" (KS 8.1) iti yāgaviṣayatvād vidhes tasya ca sādhyasvabhāvatvāt sādhanākāṃkṣāyāṃ samarpitasaviśeṣaṇakāritasahitasya vidheyatve yady arthamātre vidhivyāpārāparisamāpteḥ svārthaparaśabdābhihitāpekṣitasvārthāḥ kim iti nayanti | 

	pramaṇāśāstravidas tu svayaṃ vidhiṃ vadanti[^218] anyoktam avagāhante | yat tv asmābhir uktaṃ tat sukhopāyagrāhyam | nātimahatī vyutpattir atropayujyate | iyad eva ca tatsāram | iyatī sā vidyānuṣṭhānopayoginī yadadhikam āhopuruṣikāmātraṃ tadarthavāda eva | tatra hy arthavādād viśeṣāvagatir bhavati yatrākāṃkṣā vidher anivṛtteti[^219] | yathokam upadadhātīti bahuṣu bhojanasādhaneṣu sarpistailalavaṇādiṣu satsu kenety anavasāye ghṛteneti gamyate | yathā tu rātriṣv anuṣṭhānāśravaṇād ākāṃkṣāyāṃ pratitiṣṭhantīty arthavādaḥ | ataḥ pratiṣṭhākāmasyeti gamyate | iha punar brāhmaṇā iti parisamāptatvāt padārthasya nivṛttākākṣeti[^220] stutimātrāpekṣayārthavādaḥ | atha liṅgadarśanamātratayopanyasyate "devānām aśnatā haviḥ" (MDh 11.94) iti | tasmāc chreyaḥ saṃpannaṃ pāpīyān anvetītivat tad api puṃsaḥ pratiṣiddhatvāt pākṣikenānuvādena sālambanam iti na kiṃcit | strīṇām api devānnaśeṣam ājyādiprāśanam asty eva | vedodāharaś ca darśapūrṇamāsādiṣu "videyakarmāsi" (ĀśŚ 1.11.1) iti | na ca śrāddasya kartuḥ surāṃ pāyayed iti codanayā tāsāṃ pānam anumīyate | brahmahatyādānenaiva grahaḥ | 

	tasmāj jātimātrasya pratiṣedha ity eṣa etasyāṃ vipratipattau nirṇayaḥ || 5.89 ||

	**ācāryaṃ svam upādhyāyaṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ gurum |**

**	nirhṛtya tu vratī pretān na vratena viyujyate || 5.90 ||**

**sva**grahaṇam **ācārya**viśeṣaṇaṃ manyate, "guror gurau saṃnihite" (MDh 2.205) ity atideśāt tadācārye 'pi prāpte pratiṣedhaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> **sva**śabdaṃ bāndhavavacanaṃ vyācakṣate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra tu</span> **pitaraṃ mātaram** iti na vaktavyam | nityārthaṃ tv abhidhānam iti |

	**guruḥ** "alpaṃ vā bahu vāpi" (MDh 2.149) ity anena ya uktaḥ | 

	etān **nirharato** vrataviyogo nāstīti śrutasāmarthyād darśayati | anyān nirhṛtyānena viyujyata iti padārthasiddhiḥ || 5.90 ||

	**dakṣiṇena mṛtaṃ śūdraṃ puradvāreṇa nirharet |**

**	paścimottarapūrvais tu yathāyogaṃ dvijanmanaḥ || 5.91 ||**

**puradvāreṇeti** puragrahaṇaṃ grāmādīnām apy upalakṣaṇārtham | yatrānekadvārasaṃbhavas tatrāyaṃ niyamaḥ | yo yatreṣṭe tasyāyam upadeśaḥ | amaṅgalyatvāc ca śūdrād ārabhya karmeṇopadiṣṭam | ataś ca **yathāyogam** iti vaiśyakṣatriyabrāhmaṇāḥ paścimādibhir yathāsaṃkhyaṃ saṃbandhanīyāḥ || 5.91 ||

	**na rājñām aghadoṣo 'sti vratināṃ na ca satriṇām |**

**	aindraṃ sthānam upāsīnā brahmabhūtā hi te sadā || 5.92 ||**

**rāja**śabdo yady api kṣatriyajātau vartate, tathāpīha **aindraṃ sthānam upāsīnāḥ** iti kāraṇasyopādānāj janapadeśvaravacano lakṣaṇayā vijñāyate | uttaraśloke nipuṇaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | **vratinḥ** vratacāriṇaḥ cāndrāyaṇādisthāś ca | **satriṇaḥ** gavāmayanikā anyasmin vā yajñe dīkṣitāḥ | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "anṛtvigdīkṣitabrahmacāriṇām"[^221] (GDh 14.1) iti | atrārthavādaḥ: **aindraṃ sthānam** ādhipatyaṃ padaṃ prajaiśvaryam **upāsīnāḥ** kurvāṇā rājānaḥ brahmatvaṃ prāptā vratinaḥ satriṇaś ca | **aghadoṣam** āśaucam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu satatadānapravṛttān **satriṇo** manyante | 

	mukhyayānuvṛttyā[^222] kratuviśeṣe vartate || 5.92 ||

	**rājño māhātmike sthāne sadyaḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate |**

**	prajānāṃ parirakṣārtham āsanaṃ cātra kāraṇam || 5.93 ||**

mahān ātmā yasya sthānasya tan **māhātmakam** | yasmiṃ sthāne sthitasya puṃsaḥ prajānāṃ parirakṣā | **māhātmyaṃ** tad evocyate | tac ca prajaiśvaryam | yad āha: **āsanaṃ cātra kāraṇam** iti | tad uktam: nātra jātimātram, kiṃ tu prajāpālanādhikāraḥ | **āsana**śabdo 'pīha nāsanaśayyādivacanaḥ, api tu tatpadaṃ prāptavato yat kartavyaṃ tad āha | ataḥ akṣatriyo 'pi yadi prajāpālane samarthaḥ tasyāpy āśaucābhāva eva pūrvair vyākhyātaḥ | **prajānāṃ parirakṣārtham** iti | na sarveṇa sarvāśaucanivṛttiḥ, kiṃ tarhi, prajāpālanavirodhi yadāśaucadhāraṇaṃ tan nivartate | yathā durbhikṣādau svakośād annadānena prajābharaṇam, tathā divyāntarikṣabhaumeṣūtpāteṣu[^223] śāntiḥ | akasmāt sabhyaiḥ kartavyena rājñā, atha vā āśrameṣu[^224] dvijātīnāṃ dharmasaṃśayasattvena, prathamejyādāv apy asti pravaktṛtvam, tad api prayojanam || 5.93 ||

	**ḍimbāhavahatānāṃ ca vidyutā pārthivena ca |**

**	gobrāhmaṇasya caivārthe yasya cecchati pārthivaḥ || 5.94 ||**

**ḍimbo** bahujanasaṃkulaḥ aśastrakalaho vā | **āhavaḥ** saṃgrāmo yuddham | tatra **hatānāṃ** sadyaḥ śaucam | **vidyud** aśaniḥ etad vyākhyātam | **pārthivaḥ** pṛthivyā īśvaraś cāturvarṇyasya yaḥ kaścit | **brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe ca** yuddhād anyatrāpi jalāgnidaṃṣṭrihatasya | **yasya cecchati pārthivaḥ** svakāryārthaparipālanādhikṛtasya || 5.94 ||

_kuta etat | yato rājñāṃ paripālana evāśaucanivṛttis tatra kuto 'nyasyāviśeṣeṇa tadicchayā vinivṛttiḥ syāt |_

	**somāgnyarkānilendrāṇāṃ vittāppatyor yamasya ca |**

**	aṣṭānāṃ lokapālānāṃ vapur dhārayate nṛpaḥ || 5.95 ||**

**vapus** tejo'ṃśaḥ | **vittapatir** vaiśravaṇaḥ | **apāṃpatir** varuṇaḥ || 5.95 ||

_atraiva dvitīyo 'rthavādaḥ |_

	**lokeśādhiṣṭhito rājā nāsyāśaucaṃ vidhīyate |**

**	śaucāśaucaṃ hi martyānāṃ lokebhyaḥ prabhavāpyayau**[^225]** || 5.96 ||**

etair **lokeśair** **adhiṣṭhito** **rājā** | nāsya **śaucāśaucam**, yato **martyānāṃ** manuṣyāṇām ābhyām adhikāraḥ | tayoś ca **prabhavāpyayau** pravṛttinivṛttī **lokebhyaḥ** sakāśān **martyānāṃ**, na tu lokeśānām eva || 5.96 ||

	**udyatair āhave śastraiḥ kṣatradharmahastasya ca |**

**	sadyaḥ saṃtiṣṭhate yajñas tathāśaucam iti sthitiḥ || 5.97 ||**

yena śasyate hanyate tac **chastram** | ataḥ pāṣāṇalaguḍādināpi hatasya yajñasaṃsthā niṣpadyate, nāyudhair eva khaḍgādibhiḥ | āhūyante yatretaretaraṃ spardhamānā yuddhāya sa **āvahaḥ** saṃgrāmaḥ | **kṣatradharmaḥ** aparāṅmukhatvaṃ prajārthaṃ prabhuprayuktaṃ ca | **sadyaḥ** **saṃtiṣṭhate** samāptim eti | **yajñaḥ** jyotiṣṭomādiḥ | tatpuṇyena yujyata iti yāvat | **āśaucam** api sadya eva |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">atra kecit</span> "**kṣatradharmahatasya**" ity anena "**sadyaḥ**" ity abhisaṃbadhnanti | tataś ca yaḥ saṃgrāmabhūmau mṛtaḥ tasyaivāyaṃ vidhiḥ, na tu yo 'nyedyus tato 'nyatra gataḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad</span> etad vicāryam || 5.97 ||

	**vipraḥ śudhyaty apaḥ spṛṣṭvā kṣatriyo vāhanāyudham |**

**	vaiśyaḥ pratodaṃ raśmīn vā yaṣṭiṃ śūdraḥ kṛtakriyaḥ || 5.98 ||**

daśāhādīnāṃ kalpānāṃ paripūrṇa āśaucakāla idam aparaṃ kartavyam | **apaḥ spṛṣṭveti** snānam upadiśyata iti prāg vyākhyātam | **kṛtakriya** iti kṣatriyādibhir abhisaṃbadhyate | kriyā ca snānam eva, anyasyāśrutatvāt | snātvā vahanādīni spṛśeyuḥ |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> śrāddhakriyām āhuḥ | śrāddhādi kṛtvā sarva eva viśudhyati | tatrāpi brāhmaṇa udakaṃ hastena spṛṣṭvā kṣatriyādayas tu vāhanādibhiḥ || 5.98 ||

	**etad vo 'bhihitaṃ śaucaṃ sapiṇḍeṣu dvijottamāḥ |**

**	asapiṇḍeṣu sarveṣu pretaśuddhiṃ nibodhata || 5.99 ||**

pūrvottaravastūpasaṃhāropatattyupanyāsārthau pūrvottarāv ardhaślokau || 5.99 ||

	**asapiṇḍaṃ dvijaṃ pretaṃ vipro nirhṛtya bandhuvat |**

**	viśudhyati trirātreṇa mātur āptāṃś ca bāndhavān || 5.100 ||**

**bandhuvad** iti dharmeṇa, na mūlyena | **mātur āptāṃś ca** | āptagrahaṇaṃ pratyāsannabāndavamātulādigrahaṇārtham | asmāc cānumīyate **asapiṇḍaḥ** asamānodako na sarvasapiṇḍād anyaḥ || 5.100 ||

	**yady annam atti teṣāṃ tu daśāhenaiva śuddhyati |**

**	anadann annam ahnaiva na cet tasmin gṛhe vaset || 5.101 ||**

anaśnato nivasataś ca pūrvoktas trirātra eva | anaśnato na nivasataś ca ekāha eva | aśnataḥ nivasataś ca daśāha eva || 5.101 ||

	**anugamyecchayā pretaṃ jñātim ajñātim eva ca |**

**	snātvā sacailaṃ spṛṣṭvāgniṃ ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśuddhyati || 5.102 ||**

anugamanaṃ buddhipūvam anuvrajanam | yathākathaṃcid adhigamane na ca sacailam | snānam agnisparśo ghṛtaprāśanaṃ ca smucchitaṃ śuddhihetuḥ || 5.102 ||

	**na vipraṃ sveṣu tiṣṭhatsu mṛtaṃ śūdreṇa nāyayet |**

**	asvargyā hy āhutiḥ sā syāc chūdrasaṃsparśadūṣitā || 5.103 ||**

**na nāyayen** na nirhārayet | **sveṣu tiṣṭhatsu** samānajātīyeṣu satsu | āhutigrahaṇān na dāhayed iti | vipragrahaṇam atantram | kṣatriyavaiśyayor api śūdrasaṃsparśo doṣa evety arthavādāt pratiṣedhaḥ pratīyate || 5.103 ||

	**jñānaṃ tapo 'gnir āhāro mṛn mano vāryupāñjanam |**

**	vāyuḥ karmārkakālau ca śuddheḥ kartṝṇi dehinām || 5.104 ||**

**jñānā**dīni kālaśuddheḥ dṛṣṭāntatayopādīyante | tathaitāni svaviṣaye śuddhikāraṇāni | evaṃ kālo 'pi nātrātiśaṅkitavyaḥ | eteṣāṃ yasya yatra śuddhihetutvaṃ tad ihaiva prakaraṇe teṣāṃ vakṣyate | anyeṣāṃ tatra tatra deśe |

	tatra **jñānam** ādhyātmikaṃ sāṃkhyayogopadiṣṭam | tena hi avidyāvāsanāpāsanena rāgādikṣaye nirdoṣajñānam upaiti | vakṣyati ca "buddhir jñānena śudhyati" iti (MDh 5.108) | **tapaḥ** kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādi | tat pātakopapātakānāṃ śuddhihetuḥ | **agnir** mṛnmayādiṣu "punaḥ pākena" (MDh 5.121) iti | **āhāraḥ** pavitrāṇāṃ payomūlānām | so 'pi tapa iva śodhayati | mṛdvāriṇāṃ śuddhihetutā prasiddhaiva | **manaso** vakṣyate "manaḥ satyena" iti (MDh 5.108) | **upāñjanaṃ** maṭhādeḥ sudhāgomayādinā saṃmārjanānulepane | **vāyuś** caṇḍālādispṛṣṭe tṛṇakāṣṭhādau rathāpatite | **karmāṇi** saṃdhyopāsanādīni | uktaṃ ca "pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ japaṃs tiṣṭhen naiśam eno vyapohati" iti (MDh 2.102) | etac ca dvitīye vyākhyātam | 

	saty api tapasaḥ karmatve prādhānyakhyāpanārthaṃ pṛthag upadeśaḥ | prāyeṇa ca śāstre bhedenaiva karmaṇas tapo nirdiśyate "karmaniṣṭhās taponiṣṭhāḥ" iti (YDh 1.219) || 5.104 || 

	**sarveṣām eva śaucānām arthaśaucaṃ paraṃ smṛtam |**

**	yo 'rthe śucir hi sa śucir na mṛdvāriśuciḥ śuciḥ || 5.105 ||**

<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ko 'sya</span> prasaṅgaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yathā</span> mṛdvāriśucāv avilambaṃ kṛtotsargaḥ pravartate tathā pramādaskhalite paradravyāpaharaṇādāv avilambitaṃ prāyaścittaṃ śuddhaye samāśrayaṇīyam | ekādaśe vakṣyati[^226] || 5.105 ||

	**kṣāntyā śuddhyanti vidvāṃso dānenākāryakāriṇaḥ |**

**	pracchannapāpā japyena tapasā vedavittamāḥ || 5.106 ||**

ye **vidvāṃsas** te **kṣāntyaiva** **śudhyanti** | te hi dveṣerṣyāmatsarair nopahanyante | tato duṣkṛteṣu pravṛtteṣu nityaśuddhā bhavanti | **kṣāntir** nāma cittadharmaḥ, sarvatra sāmyam | **dānasy**āpy **akāryakṛc**chiddhir uktā "dānena vadhanirṇekam" (MDh 11.138) ityādinā | **pracchannapāpānām** api rahasyādhikāre **japa** ukta eva | **tapo** vedavidāṃ vedābhyāsa eva, jñānaṃ ca | yathoktam "brāhmaṇasya tapo jñānam" iti (MDh 11.234) | kṛcchrādi tu sarveṣāṃ śuddhihetur na vedavidām eva || 5.106 ||

	**mṛttoyaiḥ śudhyate śodhyaṃ nadī vegena śudhyati |**

**	rajasā strī manoduṣṭā saṃnyāsena dvijottamāḥ || 5.107 ||**

**nadyaḥ** pārāvāre kṣīṇodakāyā aśuddhyupahate, tasyā eva vegaṃ gatāyāḥ[^227] kūlaṃkaṣāyā udakaṃ **vegena śudhyati** | na[^228] yathānyāsyā bhūmeḥ "bhūmiḥ śudhyati pañcabhiḥ" iti (MDh 5.122) śuddhaye pratītir naivaṃ nadītīreṣu | 

	atha vā vegavatyā aśucipravāhasaṃsargeṇāśucyāśaṅkāyām idam ucyate **nadī vegeneti** | naivaṃ mantavyaṃ itaś cāmutaś cāśucipravāhaiḥ saṃspṛṣṭā na śudhyati | 

	śārīre vyabhicāre 'nupalabhyamāne parapuruṣarūpaguṇānucintanena **manoduṣṭā rajasā** ṛtau śoṇitena srutena **śudhyati strī** | 

	**saṃnyāsaḥ** ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyate | tena **dvijottamāḥ** śuddhā bhavanti | na kathaṃcin mānasāpacāre | yad aviduṣā cintitaṃ[^229] sūkṣmaprāṇivadhādi tad eṣām apanīyate || 5.107 ||

	**adbhir gātrāṇi śudhyanti manaḥ satyena śudhyati |**

**	vidyātapobhyāṃ bhūtātmā budhir jñānena śudhyati || 5.108 ||**

iyān evādhikārī: kartā ca puruṣo, yad āntarātmā; antaḥkaraṇaṃ **manaḥ**; **buddhiḥ;** śarīraṃ bhogāyatanam | indriyāṇāṃ bhautikatvān na pṛthaktvam | atra kiṃcit kenacic chodhyate | "kālena tu sarvam" iti stutiparam | 

	**gatrāṇīty** avayavair avayavinaṇ lakṣayati | **adbhiḥ** snānena śrīraṃ **śudhyati** | **manas** tu sadasadātmakam, tasyāsatsaṃkalpād aśuddhiḥ **satyena** sādhusaṃkalpena nivartate | pūrvaṃ (MDh 5.104) manasaḥ śuddhihetutvam uktam, tadadhyāhāreṇa nedaṃ vāco manaḥśuddhikaraṇam | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "manasā vā iṣitā vāg vadati, yā hy anyamanā vācaṃ vadaty asuryā vai sā vāg avedajuṣṭā" (AitB 9.4) iti | 

	**vidyayā** sāṅkhyavedāntābhyāsajanyayā, **tapasā** ca kṛcchrādinābhyupetaḥ śudhyati **bhūtātmā** | bhūtaśabdas tattvavacanaḥ | pāramārthiko 'yam ātmānupacitāhaṃpratyayavedyaḥ, na tu bhūtamaya ātmā śarīrātmeti mantavyam | **buddhir** avidyamānārthākāradarśanīyā svapnādiṣv asatsiddhāntaprakalpitārthābhiniveśatayā vastvātmārthākārayor asadbhedādhyavasāyena duṣyantī | yā vānupabhuktajanmāntarakṛtāśubhakarmajā ekaikaduṣkṛtajā vā buddhir ātmano yāvat sahajā avidyātmakābhedagrahaṇalakṣaṇā guṇātmavivekābhāvalakṣaṇā vā dhanaputrādyabhiṣaṅgarūpā tṛṣṇātiśayahetuḥ,  sā tu **jñānena** svaprakāśāśrayayā pramāṇavyutpattyā **śudhyati** | buddhyarthayor bhedād ākāravatvād arthasya viṣayākāreṇa ca pariṇāmāsiddhir nirvikāratvaniścayād buddhiśuddhiḥ | 

	pūrvatra ca vidyā vedārthavedanam eva | tasyāś ca hetutvam "yathaidhas tejasā vahniḥ" (MDh 11.245) itivad iti | 

	evaṃ śuddhaḥ pūto brahmalokam avāpnotīty eṣā sā caturvidhā śuddhiḥ | yathaitā śuddhayaḥ parapuruṣārthahetavas tajjananādiṣv iyam iti praśaṃsā || 5.108 ||

	**eṣa śaucasya vaḥ proktaḥ śārīrasya vinirṇayaḥ |**

**	nānāvidhānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ śuddheḥ śṛṇuta nirṇayam || 5.109 ||**

**nānāvidhānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ** bahuprakārāṇāṃ taijasamārtikadravakaṭhinavyastasaṃhatakāryadravyādibhedair dravyāṇām upakaraṇabhūtānām| pūrvasyāḥ śuddher bhedam etenāha | tatra buddhyātmanaḥ pradhānatā śuddhiḥ | dravyāṇāṃ tu tatsaṃparigrahāt | iha tu viparītam | **śṛṇuta nirṇayam** | pūrveṇārthasyāsāṃkāryārthaḥ ślokaḥ || 5.109 ||

	**taijasānāṃ maṇīnāṃ ca sarvasyāśmamayasya ca |**

**	bhasmanādbhir mṛdā caiva śuddhir uktā manīṣibhiḥ || 5.110 ||**

**taijasāny** ucyante yāny agnisaṃyogād dravībhavanti, rajatasuvarṇatāmrāyasatrapusīsādīni | **maṇayaḥ** sphaṭikakalpāḥ | **aśmā** pāṣāṇaḥ | tadvikāraḥ pātram aśmamayam | **sarvasyeti** pādapūraṇārtham | parvatagrāvṇo nadīsthasya cety ālaṃbanam | bhasmanet[^230] ekakāryatvān mṛdbhasmanī vikalpyete | āpaḥ samuccīyante | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kiṃ</span> punar atra kāryam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">lepa</span>gandhāpamārjanam | uktam "lepagandhāpakarṣaṇe śaucam amedhyasya" (GDh 1.42), ihāpi "yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktāt" (MD 5. 124) iti | tatra rūpataḥ pāruṣyaṃ[^231] samānaṃ mṛdbhasmanoḥ, snehanimittakāryabhede śuddhiḥ | aśuceḥ śucitvāpādanaṃ[^232] pratyavāyāpanayena saṃvyavahārayogyatā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">yady</span> evam āśuddhir vācyā: idam anena saṃpṛktam aśucīti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> laukikāḥ padārthās tatraloka eva jñāsyante |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">naivam</span>[^233] | sāmānyamātraṃ lokāj jñāyate[^234] | yaj jugupsitaṃ mūtrapurīṣaśoṇitasaṃsargeṇa tādṛśaṃ loke 'śucīty āha | yad ayogyaṃ sparśanādikriyāsu tad aśuci | kathaṃ ca tasyāyogyatety etac chāstrād eva vivektavyam | kiṃ ca paradravyādau yo na skhalati sa śucir ucyate | ato nānayā[^235] padārthaprasiddhyeha kiṃcit sidhyati | apahatam aśucīti siddhe 'pi idam anenāpahanyata iti nāntareṇa śāstraviśeṣaṃ[^236] siddhyati |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punaḥ śāstrāt padārthaviśeṣāvasāyaḥ, yāvatā kartavyatāparatvena śāstraṃ pramāṇam, na padārthaprasiddhau, pāṇinivat, vedamūlatvābhyupagamān manvādismṛtīnām | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | anena dravyeṇa yad duṣṭaṃ tena na vyavahartavyam ity asty eva vidhyanumānam | yat saṃsargeṇa vyavahārapratiṣedhaḥ sa upaghātahetur ity avagamo na virudhyate | evaṃ śuddhāv api yad upahataṃ dravyaṃ tena yathāvihitaṃ kṛtaprakṣālanādikriyeṇa vyavahartavyam iti śakyate vidhimūlatā pratipattum | na ca śuddhiḥ kartavyeti vidhyarthaḥ | tathā saty akurvan pratyaveyāt | kiṃ tu dṛṣṭārthe vyavahāre yena kenacit pātreṇa śucinānyena vā kartavye 'rthitvāt prāpte niyamaḥ śāstrīyaḥ: itthaṃbhūtena vyavahartavyaṃ saty arthitve, nānitthaṃbhūtena |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca niyamapakṣe 'bhyudayārthino 'dhikāraḥ | anyasya tu kāmaprasaṅgaḥ | yathā kusādhutvacintāyāṃ "vācakatvāviśeṣe 'pi niyamaḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ" (VākP 3.3.30) iti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>,yady aśuddhapātrasya[^237] pratiṣedho na syāt | pratiṣedhe tu sati kuto 'kṛtaśuddhinā vyavahāraḥ | śuddhividhis tu pratiprasavamātram | pratiprasave kuto 'bhyudayaḥ | kevalaṃ pratiṣedhātikramo na bhavati | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">bhavatu</span> vā padārthādhigamaparaiva smṛtir iyam, sādhvasādhuvivekavat svalpasmṛtivac ca | yat tu kāryamūlatvaṃ manvādivākyānām iti kenaitad uktam | yatra yādṛśyam mūlatvena śakyate 'vagantuṃ tatra tad evābhyupagamyate | aṣṭakādau kāryarūpe tādṛśam eva vākyaṃ mūlam, siddhe tv arthe siddhārthaviṣayam eva[^238] | padārthavyavasthāyām idaṃ prathamatā vyavahāramūleti na kadācit kṛtiḥ | iha tu na kathaṃcid vyavahāramūlaṃ saṃbhavati | vaidikamantrasādhyāyāṃ ca śuddhau kā vyavahāramūlatā śakyā | vidhiś cānarthakaḥ syāt |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca pāṇiner api vidhir asti "sādhubhir bhāṣitavyaṃ nāsādhubhir" iti | naiṣā pāṇineḥ smṛtiḥ | sā hy etāvati paryavasitā sādhur ayam ayaṃ neti | etat tu dharmasūtrakāriṇāṃ smaraṇaṃ yady apy asti | abhidhānasārāc caitan nipuṇato 'vagantavyam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> tatsmṛtāv api vidhiḥ śrūyate | dāyādā evaṃ vibhajeran, "caturo 'ṃśān harc jyeṣṭhaḥ" (MDh 9.153), "jyeṣṭha eva tu gṛhṇīyāt" (MDh 9.105) iti | kiṃ vidhyartha eva liṅgāntare praiṣādau smaryate | padārthā vidhirūpāḥ, vidhiseṣāḥ praiṣdayaḥ sarvatra pravartanāpratipatter iti cet, hetuhetumator āśiṣi prāptakālādiṣu kā pravartanā | na ca grahaṇaṃ vidheyam, arthitayā prāptatvāt |

	svaparāṃśayor aviśiṣṭāyām arthitāyāṃ niyamārtho vidhir iti cet, adṛṣṭakalpena vihitāṃśātirekeṇa vidhiniyamānupapatteḥ | pratiṣedhākhyāparisaṃkhyeti cet, yuktam etat | kiṃ tu[^239] vibhāgakāla eva yaḥ kaścid adhikam aṃśaṃ bhrātṛbhir anujātam ādadīta sa pratyaveyāt satyām apy anujñāyām, na caikavastvaṃśe[^240] svatvaṃ[^241] jñāpyeta | grahaṇavidhau hi svatvāpattir upāttā | tasya yad anyat tad asvam iti vijñāyate pratiṣedhaḥ | punas tadatikrameṇāpi parigrahe syād eva svāmyam | ataś ca cauryādināpīṣyate | na tadā idam asya svam idaṃ neti parigṛhād ṛte niścīyate |

	tasmād vidhiniyamaparisaṃkhyānām asaṃbhāvād iyaty aṃśe 'yaṃ svāmīyaty aṃśe 'yam iti etāvān vibhāgārthaḥ | ato 'yam arthāntare liṅ bhajerann iti prāptakālatāyām | hareyur ityādiṣu laukikapravṛttyanuvādaḥ, yathā "kṣudhito bhuñjīta" "yogakṣemārtham īśvaram abhigacchet" (GDh 9.63) iti | gautamaś ca spaṣṭam evāha: "rikthakrayaḥ" ityādi (GDh 10.39) | 

	tasmād aṣṭakādismṛteḥ śuddhyaśuddhivacanasya saṃskāravidhitaiva śiṣyate, vidhimūlatvād vidhiśiṣṭaiva | ataḥ śuddhyaśuddhī ubhe api śāstrāvaseye | tataḥ śuddhir api vācyā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | uktaiva tarhi "vasā śukram" (MDh 5.133) iti | nṛgrahaṇaṃ ca tatra smṛtyantaradarśanena pradarśanārtham | śvamārjārakharoṣṭrakapikākaviḍvarāhagrāmya-kukkuṭākhuśṛgālakravyādamṛgaśakuntanakhinakulānāṃ | vasādigrahaṇaṃ ca romamāṃsānāṃ | 

	śuddhivacanāc cāsuddhānāṃ mūtrādyupahātānām ayaṃ saṃskāraḥ kartavyaḥ, na punar evam eva prayujyamānānām | na hi suvarṇādayo bhāvāḥ svarūpeṇāśuddhāḥ, yena prayogakāle śuddhim apekṣeran | 

	atha vādṛṣṭārtho dṛṣṭaprayogāśrayaḥ saṃskāro vidhīyate | prāṅmukheneva bhojane | tatra śuddhivacanaṃ virudhyate | 

	ye tu pātrāṇāṃ bhojanārambhe saṃmārjanaprakṣālane, te samācārataḥ, na punar asyāḥ śuddhismṛteḥ | yad apy anyad aspṛśyaṃ puruṣasya patitacāṇḍālādi tathā laśunapalāṇḍusurāmāṃsādi, tad api dravyāṇām upaghātakam | tatra kasminn upaghāte kā śuddhir iti smṛtyantarasamācārāv anveṣaṇīyau | uktaś ca viśeṣo hārītāpastambaparāśaramunibhiḥ | tāni tu vacanāny asmābhir iha sarvāṇi na parivartitāni | lekhakaviśeṣaprasaṅgāc candragomitantrakāravat[^242] || 5.110 ||

	**nirlepaṃ kāṃcanaṃ bhāṇḍam adbhir eva viśuddhyati |**

**	abjam aśmamayaṃ caiva rājataṃ cānupaskṛtam || 5.111||**

taijasaviśeṣayoḥ kāñcanarājatayor nirlepayor ayaṃ vidhiḥ | anyeṣāṃ tu tāmrādīnāṃ yathocchiṣṭasparśe dhāvanād iṣṭakādibhiḥ | yatra[^243] kṣīraṃ vā pānīyaṃ vā pītaṃ tatra na bhavati lepaḥ | yatra māsaghṛtakṣīrādibhir ucchiṣṭaiḥ saṃśliṣyanty avayavās tatra vakṣyati "tasmāt tayoḥ svayonyaiva" (MDh 5.112) iti | lepagandhāpakarṣaṇavacanāc ca (GDh 1.42) yo lepo yenaivāpakraṣṭuṃ śakyate tatra tad evopādeyam, na bhasmavāriṇī eva | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "godhūmakuṣṭhakakalāyayavamudgamasūracūrṇaiḥ[^244]" ityādi paṭhati | evaṃ "śvacāṇḍālodakyādisparśe tu nirlepayor api bhasmanā triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ parimārjanam" iti  hārītaḥ | śaṅkhas tu "taijasānāṃ kuṇaparudhiraretomūtrapurīṣopahatānām āvartanam ullekhanaṃ bhasmanā vā triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ parimārjanam" iti | tatra cirakālamūtrādivāsitānām āvartanam | nāmākṛtim upamṛdyecchātas tadākṛtisaṃpādanam āvartanam | ullekhanaṃ tīkṣṇena śastreṇāśmanā vā nigharṣaḥ | 

	smṛtyantare tv ākaradāhāvacūlanāny[^245] āmnātāni | tatra suvarṇakārair varṇīkṛtasya śuddhiḥ ākaraḥ[^246] | dāhaḥ agnau suvarṇakārair niṣṭhāpanam | avacūlanaṃ dāhonnotānāṃ[^247] suvarṇakārāṇāṃ suvarṇaghanabhāṇḍe tena sarvata ahananaṃ tasmin varṇākare[^248] | tathā coktam "ākarāḥ śucayaḥ sarve" (BDh 1.9.3) iti | 

	**abjaṃ** śaṅkhasphaṭikādi[^249] | śaṅkhasya tu salepasya gaurasarṣapakalkena gomūtrodakābhyāṃ kṣīreṇa ca | smṛtyantare hi paṭhyate "adbhiḥ śaṅkhasya" iti, "kṣīrodakābhyāṃ gaurasarṣapakalkenocchiṣṭasnehayuktasya" iti | 

	**anupaskṛtam** akhātapūritam, atha vātyantānupahatam | sarvaśeṣaś cāyam | tena śuṣkāmedhyacaṇḍālādisparśe saty api nirlepatve prākpradarśitaiva śākhāntarīyā śuddhiḥ || 5.111 ||

	**apām agneś ca saṃyogād dhaimaṃ raupyam ca nirbabhau |**

**	tasmāt tayoḥ svayonyaiva nirṇeko guṇavattaraḥ || 5.112 ||**

arthavādo 'yam | "agnir vai vāruṇāni" ityārabhya, "akāmayata" ityādyarthavādeṣu hemnaḥ suvarṇasya rūpyasya cotpattiḥ śrutā | puruṣadharmeṇāgnir varuṇānīr apo 'kāmayata maithunadharmeṇa samayujyata tata etad dvayaṃ **nirbabhau** udbhūtam | atas **tayoḥ svayonyā** svenotpattikāraṇenāgninā atyantopaghāta udakena ca | "sayonyā" iti pāṭhe samānotpattinā bhasmaneti vyākhyeyam | taddarśanāc ca mṛdo 'pi kadācid anujñāyante | **nirṇekaḥ** śodhanaṃ **guṇavattaraḥ** || 5.112 ||

	**tāmrāyaḥkāṃsyaraityānāṃ trapuṇaḥ sīsakasya ca |**

**	śaucaṃ yathārhaṃ kartavyaṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ || 5.113 ||**

**yathārham** | yasya yad arhati, yena yasya malam apakraṣṭuṃ śakyata ity arthaḥ | ata eva smṛtyantaroktam api labhyate: "vāhanīyāś trapusīsakavikārā gomayatuṣaiḥ" iti | yathā: 

	gavāghrātāni kāṃsyāni śūdrocchiṣṭāni yāni ca |

	śuddhyanti daśabhiḥ kṣāraiḥ śvapakopahatāni ca || iti |

ata eva kṣārabhedāś ca kāñjikadāḍimādiyojitāḥ siddhā bhavanti || 5.113 ||

	**dravāṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śuddhir utpavanaṃ smṛtam |**

**	prokṣaṇaṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca dāravāṇāṃ ca takṣaṇam || 5.114 ||**

kṣaraṇadharmāṇo **dravāḥ** ghṛtatailodaśvitprabhṛtayaḥ | teṣāṃ ca kākādyucchiṣṭānāṃ prasthamātraparimāṇānām **utpavanaṃ** kasyacid aṃśasyāpanayanaṃ pūrvabhāgasthitasya | smṛtyantare tv evam āmnātam: "kuśāgrābhyāṃ pavamānaḥ suvarjanaḥ" ityanuvākena (MS 3.11.10) | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tu</span> plāvanam utpavanam āhuḥ: anyat samānajātīyaṃ tāvad āsicyate yāvat pūrṇe bhāṇḍe kāścin mātrā avasravanti | 

	sākṣād upaghāta etat | alpānāṃ tyāga eva | bhāṇḍopaghāte tu pātrāntaranayanam | ucchiṣṭasaṃsparśe tu tailasarpiṣī udake 'vadhāya japed ity uktam | tatrārthāt pātrotkṣepaḥ | na hi tailasya udake kṣiptasya pātrarahitasyopayogaḥ saṃbhavati | sāhacaryāt ghṛtasyāpi | etac cotpavanaṃ dravāṇām | yatra[^250] madyāmedhyasaṃsargakṛtau gandhavarṇau na dṛśyete | tayos tu satyos tyāga eva | sarvaṃ caitad baudhāyanasmṛtau parigṛhītam (BDh 1.8.32–53) | pakvānāṃ tu dravyāṇāṃ punaḥpāko 'pi śaṅkhenāmnātaḥ | sarveṣāṃ ye 'py amedhyā madyādayas teṣām apy eṣaiva śūdrādīn prati śuddhiḥ | atra tūtpavanaṃ plāvanam eva | yathā vasiṣṭhenoktam "bhūmiṣṭhānāṃ tūdakavat" |

	**saṃhatā** kaṭhināḥ, śītaṃ ghṛtaṃ āmikṣāguḍaparpaṭakādayaḥ | teṣāṃ yaḥ pradeśa upahatas tam apanīya śeṣasya śuddhiḥ | uktaṃ ca śaṅkhena: "śuṣkāṇām uddhṛtadoṣāṇām" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">atha vā</span> samudāyād avayavinaḥ saṃhatāḥ, śayanāsanasaraṇādayaḥ sajātīyavijātīyadravyasaṃghātātmakāḥ | "uddhṛtadoṣāṇām" iti sarvatra draṣṭavyam | śavaśuṣkāmedhyasaṃsargeṣu yaḥ pradeśo vṛttasaṃsargas tasya prakṣālanam avaśiṣṭasya prokṣaṇam |

	**dāravāṇāṃ** kevaladārukṛtānāṃ bṛsīphalakādīnāṃ kāṣṭhamayānāṃ ca śavacaṇḍālapurīṣasaṃsarge **takṣaṇam** | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu purīṣasaṃsarga evecchanti | takṣaṇena gandhalepādyapanetavyam | avaśiṣṭasya mṛdvāribhyāṃ prakṣālanaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ vā | śvādyupaghāte tu prakṣālanam eva purīṣavat | khaṭvāśayyādīnāṃ ca dārucarmasūtraghaṭitānāṃ saṃhatatvena śuddhiḥ || 5.114 ||

	**mārjanaṃ yajñapātrāṇāṃ pāṇinā yajñakarmaṇi |**

**	camasānāṃ grahāṇāṃ ca śuddhiḥ prakṣālanena tu || 5.115 ||**

**	carūṇām sruksruvāṇāṃ ca śuddhir uṣṇena vāriṇā |**

**	sphyaśūrpaśakaṭānāṃ ca musalolūkhalasya ca || 5.116 ||**

ślokadvayaṃ śrutisiddhārthānuvādena dṛṣṭāntatayā neyam | grahacamasādīnāṃ yajñapātrāṇāṃ prayogāntare prayujyamānānāṃ pūrvaprayogalagnājyahavirlepādisaṃsargaparihārārtham **uṣṇena vāriṇā** lepādyapakarṣaḥ kartavyaḥ | tato yathāśruti kvacit pāṇinā kvacid darbhaiḥ kvacid daśāpavitreṇa saṃmārgaḥ kartavyaḥ | iyaṃ prāyogikī śuddhiḥ | ucchiṣṭādyupaghāte tu laukikapātravat | "na somenocchiṣṭā bhavanti" (ĀśŚ 5.6.3) iti viśeṣaśruter anyatropaghāte sāmānyaśuddhir astīti jñāyate | grahacamasasphyā yājñikebhya ākāraviśeṣeṇāvasātavyāḥ || 5.115–116 ||

**	adbhis tu prokṣaṇaṃ śaucaṃ bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām |**

**	prakṣālanena tv alpānām adbhiḥ śaucaṃ vidhīyate || 5.117 ||**

bahutvaṃ dhānyānāṃ droṇādhikye smaryate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye</span> tu puruṣāpekṣayā deśakālāpekṣayā ca varṇayanti | kasyacid durgatasya kuḍavārdham api bahu bhavati | tathā kasyāṃcid avasthāyāṃ vardhitakośo bahutām eti | tathāha baudhāyanaḥ: 

	deśaṃ kālaṃ tathātmānaṃ dravyaṃ dravyaprayojanam | 

	upapattim avasthāṃ tu jñātvā śuddhiṃ prayojayet || (BDh 1.8.53) 

evaṃ vāsaḥsv api kecid āhuḥ: "tribhya ūrdhvaṃ bahūni" | yady api triprabhṛtiṣu bahutvam, yataḥ "**alpānām**" iti bahuvacanaṃ śrutam, atas triparyantāny alpāni | 

	**adbhir** ity upalakṣaṇam | tena yasya vāsaso yenaiva doṣasaṃsargo vyapaiti tad api draṣṭavyam | tac ca prāg darśitam | prokṣaṇasaṃbandho 'bgrahaṇaniyamārthaḥ | udakenaiva prokṣaṇaṃ kartavyam | etenaiva ca bhedena dviḥpāṭhaḥ | 

	etac ca mahaty upaghāte śavapurīṣacāṇḍālādisparśe | anyathā <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tv alpānām</span> iti prokṣaṇam eva | 

	yadi prakṣālitasyāpi[^251] lepādi vāsaso nāpaiti tadā tanmātracchedanam "utsargo vā" (GDh 1.34) iti gautamenoktam || 5.117 ||

	**cailavac carmaṇāṃ śuddhir vaidalānāṃ tathaiva ca |**

**	śākamūlaphalānāṃ tu dhānyavac chuddhir iṣyate || 5.118 ||**

**carmaṇām** vardhrāṇāṃ spṛśyānām, na tu śvaśṛgālādisamanvitānāṃ svabhāvāśucīnām | upānatkavacādīnām api tadvikārāṇām eṣa eva vidhiḥ | atra hi prakaraṇe prakṛtyāpi vikṛtir gṛhyate, vikṛtyāpi prakṛtiḥ | tathā ca dāravāṇām ity atra dārūṇām apy eṣaiva śuddhiḥ | vasiṣṭhena hi dāravāṇāṃ śuddhim abhidhāya, "dārvasthibhūmyāni" ity uktam (cf, VaDh 3.52) | yadi ca vikṛtyā prakṛtir na gṛhyeta tadanuktakśuddhividhānena dārūṇāṃ katham atideśaḥ kriyeta | prakṛtes tu vikāragrahaṇaṃ tadbuddhyanapāyād yuktam eva | 

	**vaidalāni** vārkṣatvagādīni | smṛtyantare pakṣapavitracarmacāmaratṛṇavetrabālavalkalānām eṣaiva[^252] śuddhir vihitā | tatra mayūrādipakṣās tannirvṛttāś ca chatrapicchikādayo gṛhyante | pavitraṃ darbhas teṣāṃ darbhamayānāṃ ca vāsasām | tṛṇaśabdena tālapatrāṇy ucyante | "tṛṇarājaṃ vidus tālam" iti smaryate | tatraikadeśāt samudāyapratipattir dattaśabdādivad devadatte | bālā gavāśvājānāṃ na manuṣyāṇām, teṣāṃ cyutānām apṛśyatvāt | 

	sarvā ceyaṃ dravyāntaropaghāte śuddhir ucyate na svabhāvopahatau, celadhānyayor ekarūptvāc chuddeḥ | **śākāder** dhānyavad vacanam | yathā dhānyānām avaghātādisaṃskārāntararahitānāṃ dhānyāvasthānām eva prokṣaṇaprakṣālane śuddhihetū tadvac chākādīnām api | tenāpakavānām ayaṃ vidhiḥ | pakvānāṃ tu saty api śākādiśabdavācyatve śuddhyantaram anveṣaṇīyam | yathoktam "suvarṇavāriṇā pāvakajvālayā ca" ityādi | ākarād āhṛtānāṃ tu śākādīnām udaśviddadhikṣīrādīnāṃ prokṣaṇaparyagnikaraṇe viśeṣato hārītenāmnāte | tathā śimbīdhānyānām udgharṣaṇadalanapeṣaṇādi | etac ca pādasparśe śaṅkānivṛttyartham | tad uktam "ākarāḥ śucayaḥ sarve" (BDh 1.9.3) iti || 5.118 ||

	**kauśeyāvikayor ūṣaiḥ kutapānām ariṣṭakaiḥ |**

**	śrīphalair aṃśupaṭṭānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ || 5.119 ||**

**ūṣāḥ** kāñcanamṛdaḥ | **ariṣṭakā**dayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | snehādilepe saty udakena teṣāṃ dravyāṇāṃ cūrṇasaṃmiśreṇa[^253] lepanocchedanādi kartavyam | **kauśeyaḥ** paṭṭaviśeṣaḥ | evam **aṃśupaṭṭam** āvikam ūrṇāmayaṃ tasya hārītenoktam "ādityenorṇāmayānām" | tan nityaṃ pradhriyamāṇānām anekapuruṣasya śarīrasaṃsparśe draṣṭavyam, nānyasminn upaghāte | vāsastvādeḥ teṣāṃ kevalayoḥ prokṣaṇaprakṣālanayoḥ prāptayoḥ snehādilepāpakarṣaṇe atidiśyete | **kṣauma**grahaṇaṃ śāṇādīnām api pradarśanārtham || 5.119 ||

	**kṣaumavac chaṅkhaśṛṅgāṇām asthidantamayasya ca |**

**	śuddhir vijānatā kāryā gomūtreṇodakena vā || 5.120 ||**

asthiśṛṅgadantāḥ spṛśyānāṃ gomeṣahastyādīnām, na śvagardabhādīnām | **gomūtrodakayor** vikalpaḥ | gaurasarṣapakalkas tu samuccīyate || 5.120 ||

	**prokṣaṇāt tṛṇakāṣṭhaṃ ca palālaṃ caiva śudhyati |**

**	mārjanopāñjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam || 5.121 ||**

vrīhyādikāṇḍaṃ srastarādiprayojanaṃ **palālam** | **tṛṇāni** kuśaśādvalādīni |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca dāravāṇām ity atra vikṛtiḥ prakṛter grāhikety uktam | kimarthaṃ kāṣṭhagrahaṇam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">niyamārtham</span>, prokṣaṇam eva | tena yāvan na mahān upaghātas tāvad dārūṇi na[^254] takṣyante | caṇḍālādisparśe tu "somasūryāṃśumārutaiḥ" (YDh 1.193) ity anenaiva śuddhiḥ | tadvikāraṇāṃ tu darvyādīnāṃ prakṣālanatakṣaṇe svalpopaghāte 'nnādyupayogināṃ kartavye | 

	**mārjanaṃ** śodhanaṃ gṛhasya dūmāṃdhakārādyapanayanam | **upāñjanaṃ** sudhāgomayādibhir bhūmivilepanam | etac ca śavacaṇḍālodakyādibhir bhittisaṃsparśe vyāpini draṣṭavyam | avyāptau tu tāvanmātrasyaiva | ūrdhvaṃ śavopaghāte tu bhittitakṣaṇaṃ sūryaraśmyanupraveśo 'gnijvālābhimarśanam | kvacit punar navīkaraṇam ityādipaṭhitaṃ saṃmārjanam | 

	**mṛnmayānāṃ punaḥpākaḥ** | paryagnikaraṇam ucchiṣṭapuruṣasaṃsparśādau draṣṭavyam | punaḥpākas tu madyabhāṇḍādisaṃsparśe draṣṭavyaḥ | sākṣātsparśe tu tyāga eva | yathoktam 

	madyair mūtrapurīṣair vā ṣṭhīvanaiḥ pūyaśoṇitaiḥ |

	saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śudhyeta punaḥpākena mṛnmayam || iti | (VaDh 3.59)

	**saṃmārjanopāñjanena sekenollekhanena ca |**

**	gavāṃ ca parivāsena bhūmiḥ śuddhyati pañcabhiḥ || 5.122 ||**

**seko** gomūtreṇodakena vā | kṣīreṇāpi kvacid uktaḥ | **ullekhanaṃ** śastrādinā lekhākaraṇam āvāpanaṃ ca | "āvāpanaṃ ca bhūmeḥ" (GDh 1.32) iti gautamanirdeśād eva | **pañcabhir** iti punarvacanam abhighātāpekṣayā vyastasamastaprayogadarśanārtham | tatra **saṃmārjana**śūnyaṃ śodhanam **upāñjanaṃ** tv avakararahitāyāḥ kevalam api | mūtrapūrīṣādilepe ullekhanasaṃmārjane | seko nadīpulinavanādiṣu | **gavāṃ parivāsaḥ** ekāhamātraṃ goṣṭhīkaraṇam | etac ca śmaśānabhuvaḥ sarvaṃ kartavyam | āvapanaṃ tu yatra pūrvam asthikapālikādy asti tad uddhṛtya mṛdām anyāsāṃ prkṣepaḥ, yatra cāntarhitam evamādikālāntareṇāśaṅkyamānasadbhāvam ityādivat tatrāpi || 5.122 ||

	**pakṣijagdhaṃ gavā ghrātam avadhūtam avakṣutam |**

**	dūṣitaṃ keśakīṭaiś ca mṛtprakṣepeṇa śudhyati || 5.123 ||**

atra jagdhipadāl liṅgād annaviṣayatāsya ślokasya pratīyate | 

	pakṣibhis tu śukādibhir anyaiś ca bhakṣyair yad annam ucchiṣṭīkṛtam, na tu kākakaṅkagṛdhrādibhiḥ | tatra hi mahat prāyaścittam "patatriṇāvalīḍham" (MDh 4.209) iti tad etad uktaṃ prakṛtaśuddhe bhojanaprāyaścittam | tathā ca tattulyaprāyaścittasya gavā ghrātasya naiva śuddhiḥ | bhaved ayaṃ nyāyaḥ | tathāpi smṛtyantarasamācārāv anveṣyau | evaṃ hi śiṣṭā daśaśarāvādhikaṃ kākādikravyādopahataṃ tāvanmātram apanīyāvaśiṣṭaṃ śodhayitvopayuñjate arvāk tu tat[^255] tyajanti | atrāpy avasthāviśeṣo 'pekṣyaḥ | smṛtyantare tu kṛṣṇaśakuninopahatam api niṣiddham | 

	**avadhūtaṃ** mukhaśvāsenāvakampitam | vāsaso vā yasyopari rajo'panayanārtham utkṣepaṇādi kriyate ākāśadeśāt | **avakṣutaṃ** yasyopari kṣutaṃ tad eva | **keśā** manuṣyāṇāṃ cyutāḥ | **kīṭāḥ** kṣudrajantavaḥ kṛmayaḥ | te kecid gṛhasvedānnādyajāś te jīvanto makṣikāvan nopaghnanti | mṛtānāṃ teṣām annasaṃsparśe śuddhir iyam | ye tv amedhysaṃsargajās te viḍbhojinaś ca, teṣāṃ jīvatām api | gautamīyam: "nityam abhojyaṃ keśakīṭāvapannam" iti (GDh 17.8-9) | bahuvyāptau sarvatra tyāgaḥ | mahārāśāv aśucikīṭasaṃsarge 'pi svalpe tanmātrāpanayanam avaśiṣṭasya śuddhiḥ | kāñcanarajatadarbhamaṇīnāṃ vārisahitānāṃ sparśaḥ smṛtyantare keśādyavapanne vihitaḥ | avajvalanam api kvacit | 

	ye tu bhūmer imāṃ śuddhim āhus taiḥ smṛtyantarasamācāro vākyārthaś ca tyaktaḥ || 5.123 ||

	**yāvan nāpaity amedhyāktād gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ |**

**	tāvan mṛd vāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu || 5.124 ||**

**amedhyam** aspṛśyam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">tac ca</span> yad yasya yad abhojyaṃ tasya tad aśuddhihetuḥ, yathā brāhmaṇasya surāmadye, na śūdrasya | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam</span> | prāg ghomād dhavīṃṣy abhojyāni, na ca tāny apṛśyāni | surāmadyādīni tu sparśe 'pi pratiṣiddhāni brāhmaṇasya | tasmād yasyaiva sparśaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ sa eva saṃsargeṇāśucitvam āpādayati | ato nāyaṃ niyamaḥ: yad abhojyaṃ tad apṛśyaṃ yat tv apṛśyaṃ tad abhojyam iti | 

	**āktaṃ** liptam upadigdham | **tāvad** ity āvṛttividhānam | mṛd vāri, sati prayojane | prayojanaṃ ca gandhalepāpanayanam | śuṣkāmedhyasaṃsarge ciravṛttasaṃsarge vā kālenāpi tayor gandhalepayoḥ sakṛd eva mṛdvāribhyāṃ mārjanam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> mṛdvāryādīnāṃ śuddhyartham ādānaṃ dṛṣṭārthaṃ tatraiva śuddhyaty apagate lepa iti kim anena "yāvan nāpaiti" iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> | "ekā liṅge" (MDh 5.134) ityādau saṃkhyātikramārtham | uktayā saṃkhyayā aśakye purīṣādilepāpanaye anādṛtyāśrutasaṃkhyādhikāpy āśrayaṇīyā | saṃkhyāvacanaṃ tu tato nyūnatayāpy apanīte lepe saṃkhyā pūrayitavyety evamartham | 

	mṛdvārigrahaṇaṃ śuddhisādhanopalakṣaṇārthaṃ varṇayanti | ataś ca yady apy aśuddhihetubhūtaṃ vāriṇā kṣālitam api kṣārādinā saṃmārṣṭavyam anyathā na dṛśyeta | **apaiti** apagacchati nivartata iti yāvat | **tatkṛtaḥ,** tenāmedhyena kṛtaḥ | ataś ca kastūrikādivastragandho nāpaiti naiva duṣyeta | kuṃkumādyanuliptasya yaḥ pradeśo 'medhena saṃsṛjyet tatra kuṃkumādy apy apamārjitavyam | amedhyasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ hi tat, tatrāpi gandhalepagrahaṇāt | yadi gātrarūḍhaḥ kuṃkumavarṇo nighṛṣyamāṇo na śakyetāpakraṣṭuṃ syād eva śuddhiḥ || 5.124 ||

	**trīṇi devāḥ pavitrāṇi brāhmaṇānām akalpayan |**

**	adṛṣṭam adbhir nirṇiktaṃ yac ca vācā praśasyate || 5.125 ||**

**pavitrāṇi** śuddhāni | **deva**grahaṇaṃ stutiḥ | **brāhmaṇa**grahaṇam api samācārāt[^256] sarvavarṇārtham | **adṛṣṭaṃ** yad anārakṣapradeśasthaṃ dravyam adṛṣṭaśvakākādisaṃsargaṃ[^257] | na ca sadbhāvamātreṇa tadupaghātāśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikā kartavyā | evaṃ mahānasādau sūdādibhir akṛtaśaucair vyavahardbhiḥ pākyaṃ dravyam adṛṣṭaṃ paribhoktuṃ na duṣyati | 

	na punar iyam āśaṅkā kartavyā: uttarakāle tat prāg avijñātopaghāte na doṣaḥ | tathā hi "amatayaitāni ca" (MDh 5.20) ityādi virudhyeta | evaṃ tāvad yatra doṣasaṃbandho na kenacit pramāṇenāvagamyeta tac chuddham | yatra punar asaty api niścāyake pramāṇe kutarkeṇa saṃbhavyate tatrādbhir nirṇektavyam | yathā samānadeśasthālīpīṭharādi śvakākādibhir upahanyamānaṃ dṛṣṭam, anyad adṛṣṭam apy adbhir nirṇektavyam | 

	tathaivaṃvidham eva **vācā praśaṃsanīyam** | śuddham etad astv iti śiṣṭā vācayitavyāḥ | brāhmaṇavacanāc chuddhir bhavtīty āhuḥ | **praśasyata** iti laḍ ayaṃ vidhau draṣṭavyaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">ye tv āhur</span> dṛṣṭopaghātaṃ yat tasya vyavahartrā sākṣāc chuddhau kriyamāṇāyām adṛṣṭāyām śiṣṭāś ced āhuḥ: "kṛtam asya śaucam" iti, tatra pratyetavyam iti vākpraśastasyārthaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad ayuktam</span> | āptavacanasya sarvatraivāprāmānyasyānaṅgīkṛtatvāt paunaruktyaprasaṅgaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye tv</span> **adbhir nirṇiktam** iti dṛṣṭāntatayā vyākhyānayanti | adṛṣṭavākpraśaste vidhīyete | yathādbhir nirṇiktaṃ śuddham evam adṛṣṭaṃ vākpraśastaṃ vidhīyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yady adṛṣṭadoṣaṃ pratyakṣānumānāgamaiḥ śuddhaṃ, tat kathaṃ "saṃvatsarasyaikam api" (MDh 5.21) iti |

	bhakṣyaviṣayaṃ tat | spṛśyaviṣayā śuddhir iyam | gurulaghutayā vā, āpadanāpadbhedena vā vyavasthā || 5.125 ||

	**āpaḥ śuddhā bhūmigatā vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yāsu gor bhavet |**

**	avyāptāś ced amedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitāḥ || 5.126 ||**

**bhūmi**grahaṇam upalakṣaṇārtham | tena praṇālikāgatā api śucaya eva | svabhāvaśucayo hy āpo **bhūmigatā** ākāśagatāś ca | kiṃ tu bhūmer amedhyadravyasaṃsargāt kiṃcid aśucitvam | tatra gatānāṃ sargato 'śucitvaprāptau yāvatīnāṃ ca śuddhis tadartham idaṃ **vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yāsu gor bhaved** iti | vaitṛṣṇyaṃ pipāsāvicchedaḥ | parimāṇopalakṣaṇārthaṃ caitat | tatra cirantanair vyākhyātaṃ liṅgadarśanena "yathā vai goḥ sasnāmbhasi plāvya" iti | yatra goḥ sāsnādi majjati tṛṣṇā ca vicchidyate tāvatyaḥ | yās tu medhyabhūmigatās tāḥ svalpā api śuddhāḥ | kathaṃ punar amedhyavyāptir avaseyā: **gandhavarṇarasānvitāḥ** | **amedhyene**ti tṛtīyāntaṃ ṣaṣṭhyā vipariṇamyate | amedhyasaṃbandhibhir gandhādibhir yady anvitāḥ saṃyuktā bhavanti, tato **vyāptā** ucyante | evaṃ ca kṛtvā pānīyaṃ taḍāgādiṣu yady ekasmin pradeśe 'medhyaṃ dṛśyate pradeśāntare gandhādiśūnyaṃ śuddhyed eva || 5.126 ||

	**nityaṃ śuddhaḥ kāruhastaḥ paṇye yac ca prasāritam |**

**	brahmacārigataṃ bhaikṣyaṃ nityaṃ medhyam iti sthitiḥ || 5.127 ||**

**kāravaḥ** śilpinaḥ śūdarañjakatantuvāyādayas teṣāṃ **hasto nityaṃ śuddhaḥ** | ataś ca jananamaraṇāśaucayos tatspṛśyatāsti | na tu purīṣādilepe dṛśyamāne śuddhatā vijñeyā | yad uktam "sadyaḥ śaucāḥ prakīrtitāḥ" iti tad evedam | atra cāpaunaruktyam, manuśāstre 'syānupadeśāt | viṣayāntaram apy asti | "anācāntās tantuvāyā vayanti" tantūnāṃ stambhaviśleṣaṇārthaṃ yat piṣṭamaṇḍādi dīyate, tadbhājanaṃ ca yatra tatra bhūmau vidhīyate, tāvatī yāśuddhiḥ sānena nivartyate | na tu svabhāvāśucīnāṃ sparśas tais tasya śuddhatā vijñeyā, na hi teṣāṃ tatkārukarmavihitam | 

	evaṃ caiṣaivopapattir iti mlecchasaṃsṛṣṭānām api nāśucitvam, tatra śaṅkhavacanāt prokṣaṇābhyukṣaṇe | tatra hi paṭhitam "kāruhastaḥ śucis tathākaradravyāṇi" iti | 

	**paṇyaṃ** vyavahārāya yad dravyaṃ rūpakair vikrīyate 'nyena vā dravyeṇa mīyate, tat paṇyaṃ tac ca **prasāritam** āpaṇabhūmau śuci | anekakretṛsaṃsparśād bhūmau ca lepanādirahitāyāṃ sthāpanādyupaghātas tena nāśuci punaḥ punar dṛśyamānopaghātam | prasāritagrahaṇād gṛhāvasthitasya buddhau sthite 'pi paṇye na śuddhiḥ | siddhānnānāṃ tu saktvapūpādīnāṃ saty api śucitve 'bhakṣyatā śaṅkhavacanād eva "āpaṇīyāny abhakṣyāṇi" iti | 

	**brahmacārigatam** asmād eva sāhacaryāt pūrvoktā śuddhir īdṛśa upaghāte vijñāyate | bhikṣamāṇasya rathyākramaṇam aśucidarśanaṃ kṣavathuniṣṭhīvanam anekahastasaṃpāto bhikṣāyā ityādyupaghātaḥ saṃbhāvyate | medhyatayāśucitvam āha[^258] || 5.127 ||

	**nityam āsyaṃ śuci strīṇāṃ śakuniḥ phalapātane |**

**	prasrave ca śucir vatsaḥ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ || 5.128 ||**

sarva**strīṇām** **āsyaṃ śuci** paricuṃbanādau | "striyaś ca ratisaṃsarge" (VaDh 28.8) iti smṛtyantaram | ratisaṃbandhinīṣv eva na mātṛbhagiṇyādiṣu | atra ucchiṣṭapratiṣedho 'yaṃ na mantavyo yoṣitaḥ | saty api ratisaṃbandhitve "nāśnīyād bhāryayā sārdham" (MDh 4.43) iti vacanān na bhujyeteti siddhaṃ caturthādhyāye | nityagrahaṇān na saṃyogavelāyām eva, kiṃ tarhi tadarthāyām eva apravṛttau[^259] |

	**śakuniḥ phalapātane** | pakṣimātravacane 'pi śakuniśabdaḥ kākakaṅkādīnāṃ viṭbhujā neṣyate samācārāt | pātanagrahaṇād vṛkṣasthasya phalasyāyaṃ vidhiḥ | 

	**prasrave** duhyamānāyā gor **vatsaḥ** payaḥprakṣaraṇārthaṃ staneṣu saṃśliṣyate | atha vocyate "gāvo medhyā mukhād ṛte"[^260] iti vacanād aśucitve prāpte, tannivṛttyarthaṃ vacanam atas tadīyāsyasaṃsparśasya | na tu **śvā** śuciḥ | **mṛgaṃ** tu yadākheṭakādau gṛhṇāti hantuṃ tadā **śuciḥ** || 5.128 ||

	**śvabhir hatasya yan māṃsaṃ śuci tan manur abravīt |**

**	kravyādbhiś ca hatasyānyaiś caṇḍālādyaiś ca dasyubhiḥ || 5.129 ||**

pūrvaṃ "śvā mrgagrahaṇe" (MDh 5.128) iti mrgavadhe śvā śucir ity etāvad eva vivakṣitam | iha tu tena gṛhīto 'nyair vā daṇḍādighāteneti viśeṣaḥ |

	uttarārdhaślokārtho vidhīyate | **kravyādbhiḥ** śyenajambūkaprabhṛtibhiḥ | **caṇḍālādyaiḥ** ādigrahaṇaṃ śvāpadādīnām abādhāya | **dasyavo** niṣādavyādhādayaḥ prāṇivadhanīvinaḥ || 5.129 ||

	**ūrdhvaṃ nābher yāni khāni tāni medhyāni sarvaśaḥ |**

**	yāny adhastāny amedhyāni dehāc caiva malāś cyutāḥ || 5.130 ||**

**kha**śabdo 'yam indriyavacanaḥ | tena pādayor grahaṇe[^261] karmendriyāṇi[^262] **yāny adhastāny amedhyāni** iti[^263] bahuvacanam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">etad ayuktam</span> ūrdhvaṃ nābher ity anena virodhāt | tatra nābher ūrdhvaṃ medhyataratvam uktam, prakarśaś ca | yady adhastān medhyatvaṃ bhavati tata upapadyate | na hi bhavati śuklaḥ kṛṣṇatara iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">na cāyam</span> indriyavacanaḥ, kiṃ tarhi chidrārtho 'yam | tad uktam "sapta śīrṣaṇyāḥ prāṇāḥ" (ŚB 13.1.7.2) iti | 

	adho dve chidre | strīpuṃsopasthabhedād bahuvacanam | evaṃ saty antarāsyasparśe[^264] 'pi hastādeḥ śuddhatā, yadi tadgataśleṣmasaṃbandho na bhavati | tathā dūṣikāduṣṭena punaś cāsaṃsparśanāya[^265] || 5.130 ||

	**makṣikā vipruṣaś chāyā gaur aśvaḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ |**

**	rajo bhūr vāyur agniś ca sparśe medhyāni nirdiśet || 5.131 ||**

**makṣikā**grahaṇaṃ[^266] svedajānām | **go**grahaṇam ajaiḍakasya | **aśva**grahaṇaṃ hastyaśvatarāṇām | **sūrya**grahaṇaṃ jyotiṣām | **vipruṣa** udabindavaḥ sparśamātrānubhavena yā adṛśyamānarūpaviśeṣāḥ | **chāyā** caṇḍālādīnām | **bhūś** caṇḍālādispṛṣṭā padbhyām ākramyamāṇā śuddhā | anyasyās tu saṃmārjanādi vihitam | ete makṣikādayaḥ purīṣādi spṛśanto na dūṣayanti | 

	ajāśvaṃ mukhato medhyaṃ gāvo medhyā mukhād ṛte |

	mārjāranakulau spṛśyau subhāś ca mṛgapakṣiṇaḥ ||

iti smṛtyantare || 5.131 ||

	**viṇmūtrotsargaśuddhyarthaṃ mṛdvāry ādeyam arthavat |**

**	daihikānāṃ malānāṃ ca śuddhiṣu dvādaśasv api || 5.132 ||**

"dehāc caiva malāḥ cyutāḥ" (MDh 5.130) ity aśuddhatāyām idam ucyate | viṇmūtre utsṛjyete yena sa **viṇmūtrotsargaḥ** pāyvādiḥ, tasya śuddhyarthaṃ **mṛdvāry ādeyam arthavat** | anādṛtya saṃkhyāṃ yāvatībhir gandhalepāv apasarpatas tāvatīr apo mṛdaś ca gṛhṇīyāt | dehe bhavā **daihikā** **malā** aśucitvāpādakāḥ | tadarthāsv api **śuddhiṣu** mṛdvāriṇī ubhe apy **arthvatī** **ādeye** | smṛtyantare paṭhyate |

	ādadīta mrdo 'paś ca ṣaṭsu pūrveṣu śuddhaye |

	uttareṣu tu ṣaṭsv adbhiḥ kevalābhis tu śudhyati ||

viśuddheṣu śleṣamādiṣu smṛtyantare paṭhitam: "snehavisraṃsanaṃ nāsikyaṃ śleṣmāvakṣate" | teṣām eva saty apy uttaraṣaṭkatayā na mṛda ādātavyā eva || 5.132 ||

	**vasā śukram asṛṅ majjā mutraviṭ ghrāṇakarṇaviṭ |**

**	śleṣmāśru dūṣikā svedo dvādaśaite nṛṇāṃ malāḥ || 5.133 ||**

yāny etāni dvādaśamalāni darśitāni | **nṛ**grahaṇaṃ pañcanakhānāṃ pradarśanārtham | śvaśṛgālādīnāṃ tv aspṛśyatvād eva siddham | viṇmūtre tu sarvasyājāvikagavāśvebhyo 'nyatra || 5.133 ||

	**ekā liṅge gude tisras tathaikatra kare daśa |**

**	ubhayoḥ spata dātavyā mṛdaḥ śuddhim abhīpsatā || 5.134 ||**

viṇmūtrotsargānantaraṃ meḍhrasya śuddhyartham **ekā** **mṛd** dātavyā vāmena | smṛtyantare śuddhividhānād yāvatī tasmin haste yāti tāvatī sodakā grahītavyā | ahaṃ tu brave, "arthavat" (MDh 5.132) iti vacanenoktam eva parimāṇam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> paṭhanti |

	prathamā prasṛtir jñeyā dvitīyā tu tadardhikā |

	tṛtīyā mṛttikā jñeyā tribhāgakarapūraṇe ||

etac ca parimāṇaṃ pāyāv eva | anyatra tv "arthavat" iti | ekotsarge 'pīyaty eva saṃkhyā | āvṛttividhānaṃ cedam | mṛdāṃ bhedo[^267] gavādivat | tathā cātrocyate "valmīkād dūratarād aśvasthānāc cānyetyādi" | evam iha sitā kṛṣṇā lohitetyādy api nādaraṇīyam | **abhīpsatā** icchateti || 5.134 ||

	**etac chaucaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ dviguṇaṃ brahmacāriṇām |**

**	triguṇaṃ syād vanasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ tu caturguṇam || 5.135 ||**

śaucavidhir āśramaviśeṣeṇa | anāśramiṇas tu mṛdvāry ādeyam arthavad ity etad eva | śūdrasyāpi gārhasthye 'dhikāro 'sty evety eṣā saṃkhyā || 5.135 ||

	**kṛtvā mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā khāny ācānta upaspṛśet |**

**	vedam adhyeṣyamāṇaś ca annam aśnaṃś ca sarvadā || 5.136 ||**

mūtrotsargadeśān mūtrādisaṃbandhān[^268] **kṛtvā** śodhayitvā yathoktena vidhinā | **ācāntaḥ** **khāni** indriyāṇi **upaspṛśet** | **vedam adhyeṣyamāṇaś ca** dvitīye svādhyāyavidhau | prāthamikārthatvāt karoteḥ kṛtvā utsṛjyeti pratīyate | unmṛjya mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca pāyūpasthaṃ kṣalayitvā ācāmet | **vedam adheṣyamāṇaś ca** svādhyāyavidher dharmatayoktam "adhyeṣyamāṇas tv ācāntaḥ" (MDh 2.70) iti | idaṃ tv adhyāpayato 'dhyeṣyato[^269] vā[^270] | anyathā vedam udāharanta ucyante | laukikāni kriyāntarāṇi kṛtvā nānācānto vedākṣarāṇy uccārayet | **annam aśnaṃś ca** || 5.136 ||

	**trir ācāmed apaḥ pūrvaṃ dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham |**

**	śārīraṃ śaucam icchan hi strī śūdras tu sakṛt sakṛt || 5.137 ||**

ayam anuvādaḥ strīśūdrārthaḥ | uktam apy etat strīśūdrārtham ucyate | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> vyācakṣate "śudraḥ spṛṣṭābhir adbhiḥ" (MDh 2.62) iti sparśamātram apāṃ śūdreṇa kartavyam | ataḥ parimārjanaṃ śrotrādisparśanaṃ vā prāptaṃ sacchūdraviṣayatayā vidhīyate | strīṇāṃ tu "hṛdgābhiḥ pūyate vipraḥ" (MDh 2.62) iti jātinirdeśāt puṃvat prāptāv idam ucyate | 

	**śārīraṃ śaucam anvicchann** iti vacanasāmarthyād yady adhyayanabhojanayoḥ śuddhaḥ pravarteta tadā nāvaśyaṃ trir āvṛttiḥ syāt | nāpi pramārjanam | kiṃ tarhi ācamanaṃ yāvatīnāṃ tāvatīnām apām indriyasparśanaṃ ca | nānyo brahmacāridharmokta ācamanavidhiḥ || 5.137 ||

	**śūdrāṇāṃ māsikaṃ kāryaṃ vapanaṃ nyāyavartinām |**

**	vaiśyavac chaucakalpaś ca dvijocchiṣṭaṃ ca bhojanam || 5.138 ||**

sāmānyoktaḥ sacchūdrāṇāṃ prasaṅgenāyaṃ dharma ucyate | **nyāyavartino** dvijaśuśrūṣavo mahāyajñānuṣṭhāyinaś ca | tair **vapanaṃ** muṇḍanaṃ **māṃsikaṃ** kartavyam | tṛtīyārthe ṣaṣṭhī | atha vā brāhmaṇāśritās tatparatantrāḥ | brāhmaṇaiḥ **kāryam** | anekārthatvāt karoter upadeṣṭavyam iti pratipattiḥ | **vaiśyavat** **śaucakalpa**viśeṣāḥ, sūtakādāv ācamane ca | **dvijocchiṣṭaṃ ca bhojanaṃ** etat prāgvyākhyātam || 5.138 ||

	**nocchiṣṭaṃ kurvate mukhyā vipruṣo 'ṅgaṃ na yanti yāḥ |**

**	na śmaśrūṇi gatāny āsyaṃ na dantāntaradhiṣṭhitam || 5.139 ||**

"niṣṭhīvyoktvānṛtāni[^271] ca" (MDh 5.143) iti niṣṭhīvane[^272] ācamanavidhānād anācāntasyāśuddhitā jñāpitā | vipruṣām api mukhān niṣkramaṇaṃ niṣṭhīvanam eva | ato **vipruṣāṃ** śleṣmanirasanarūpaniṣṭhīvanād ācamanaprāptāv idam āha | mukhe bhavā mukhanirgatā vā **mukhyāḥ** | **vipruṣa** ity anucchiṣṭaṃ kurvanti "na ced aṅge nipatanti" (GDh 1.41) iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca vipruṣaḥ śuddhā ity uktam "mukhajā vipruṣaḥ" ity atra[^273] | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">daihika</span>malavyatirekeṇānyatra | idam eva jñāpakam | na sarvo viṣayaḥ saṃdarśitaḥ | 

	**śmaśrūṇi** dāḍikālomāni | **āsyagatāni** praviṣṭāni | nocchiṣṭaṃ kurvantīty anuṣaṅgaḥ | ataś cānyat pūgaphalādi janayaty eva | tathā **dantāntaradhiṣṭhitaṃ** lagnam | smṛtyantare viśeṣaḥ: "dantaśliṣṭe tu dantavad anyatra jihvāvimarśanāt | prākcyuter iti eke | cyuteṣv āsrāvavad vidyān nigirann eva tacchuciḥ" (GDh 1.38–40) iti | cyuteṣv ajihvayeti vidyāt, jihvāsaṃsparśe śucitvaniṣedhāt || 5.139 ||

	**spṛśanti bindavaḥ pādau ya ācāmayataḥ parān |**

**	bhaumikais te samā jñeyā na tair aprayato bhavet || 5.140 ||**

**parān ācamayataḥ** parebhya ācamanaṃ dadata ity arthaḥ | etad uktaṃ bhavati | yaḥ parasmā ācamanaṃ dadāti tasyācamayitṛhastād adho 'ṅgulivivarebhyaḥ patadbhir uda**bindubhir **bhūmyabhighātotthair yad ācāmanasya dātuḥ **pādau** **spṛśyete** tadā na tair aśucir bhavati | **bhaumikair** yathānupahatāyāṃ bhumau sthitāḥ kāścid udakamātrāḥ śuddhā evaṃ te 'py ucchiṣṭā hastāt patanta udabindavaḥ | **na taiḥ** spṛṣṭaḥ **aprayataḥ** aśuciḥ | **para**grahaṇād ya ācāmati tena tatsaṃsargo rakṣitavyaḥ anyena ca samipasthena | **pāda**grahaṇāc ca jaṅghādyantasparśo duṣṭa eva || 5.140 ||

	**ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravyahastaḥ kathaṃcana |**

**	anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt || 5.141 ||**

ācamanārheṇa prāyaścittena yuktaḥ puruṣa **ucchiṣṭa** ucyate | tad yathā: kṛtamūtrādyutsargaś cākṛtaśaucācamanādiś ca yaś cāmedhyādisaṃsparśadūṣito yadi puruṣo **dravyahastaḥ,** hastena ca gṛhītaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādi dravyavastrādi vā yena sa ucyate **dravyahastaḥ** | vajrahastādivat prayogavavyavasthā | sa cet **spṛṣṭo** bhavati, tadā **anidhāyaiva tad dravyam** anapanīya, hastagṛhītadravya evācāmet | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kathaṃ</span> punar hastasthe dravya ācamanasaṃbhavaḥ | "ā maṇibandhanāt pāṇī prakṣālayet" (GDh 1.36) iti tatra vidhiḥ |
