	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> āhuḥ | śarīrasaṃsparśamātraṃ dravyasya vivakṣitam, na hastasyaiva, evam aśuddhāv api skandhādyāropite 'pi dravye ucchiṣṭasyāśuddhataiva, tathaivācānte śuddhiḥ | ato hastāt pradeśāntare prakoṣṭhotsaṅgādike tu dravyaṃ gṛhītvācāmet | abhiprāyo yathaiva puruṣāśaucasaṃbandhād aśucy evaṃ tacchaucāc chuddhiḥ[^274] |

	gautamena tu "dravyahasta ucchiṣṭo nidhāyācāmet" (GDh 1.28) ity uktam | atra vyākhyānayanti | saty api tulyasahitatve 'tra nidhānam evābhipretam | itarathā dravyahastasyobhayoḥ śuddhau kartavyāyāṃ kaḥ prasaṅgo dravyanidhānasya | ato 'ntareṇa vacanaṃ nidhānāprāpter vacanaṃ nidhānārtham eva | kathaṃ tarhi dravyasya śuddhiḥ | prayatena puruṣeṇa grahaṇāt, smṛtyantaravihitena vā prokṣaṇena |

	pracarann annapāneṣu ucchiṣṭaṃ saṃspṛśed yadi |

	ācāmed dravyam abhyukṣya evaṃ caiva na duṣyati || iti |

yady antareṇa vacanam atra nidhānaṃ labhyate, apy **anidhāyaiveti** vacanam anarthakam | ekavākyatvāt smṛtīnām iha niścitena vidhānena tathāpy evaṃ vijñāyate | adya punar matabhedo gamyate | tataś ca vikalpaḥ | 

	tasya ca vyavasthā | garīyo dravyaṃ nidhīyate, anyad aṅgasthaṃ kṛtvāvagamyate | yadāpi svayam annam aśnāti, bhūyiṣṭaṃ vā ucchiṣṭaṃ spṛśati, ācamanārhena vākṛtācamanena spṛśyate, sarvo 'pi dravyasyocchiṣṭaṃ saṃsparśaḥ || 5.141 ||

	**vānto viriktaḥ snātvā tu ghṛtaprāśanam ācaret |**

**	ācāmed eva bhuktvānnaṃ snānaṃ maithuninaḥ smṛtam || 5.142 ||**

vamanavirecane prasiddhe | aśitam annaṃ yena mukhenodgīrṇaṃ sa **vāntaḥ** puruṣaḥ | yasyoccāravegā aṣṭasaṃkhyāyā ūrdhvaṃ jātāḥ, harītakyādibhakṣaṇena vyādhinā vā, sa **viriktaḥ** | tau snānaṃ prathamaṃ kuryātām | tato 'nte **ghṛtaprāśanaṃ** kṛtvaitad anyad annam adyatām | na cānena ghṛtaprāśanena bhojanāntaranivṛttiḥ | prāyaścitteṣu dravyaśuddhir iyaṃ bhasmodakamārjanavad **ghṛtaprāśanam** | **ācamed eva bhuktvānnam** | annaṃ bhuktvā tad ahar eva yadi vamanavirecane syātāṃ tadācamanam eva kevalam, na snānaghṛtaprāśane | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">aparais tu</span> svatantraṃ vyākhyāyate | bhuktvācāmed eva | bhojanānantaram ācamanaṃ vihitaṃ tasyaivāyam apavādaḥ | 

	**maithuninaḥ** | striyāṃ kṛtaśukrotsargaḥ snānena śudhyati || 5.142 ||

	**suptvā kṣutvā ca bhuktvā ca niṣṭhīvyoktvānṛtāni ca |**

**	pītvāpo 'dhyeṣyamāṇaś ca ācāmet prayato 'pi san || 5.143 ||**

**kṣutvā** anicchato vāyupreryamāṇasya yo nāsikācchidrād upajāyate śabdaḥ sa kṣavathuḥ, taṃ kṛtvā | **prayato 'pi san** | etad adhyeṣyamāṇapadenaiva saṃbadhyate[^275] | prayato 'py **adhyeṣyamāṇa** ācamyādhīyīta, adhyayanavidhyaṅgatayācamanaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | snānādibhyas tv anantaraṃ sakṛd eva | yat punar uktam:

	suptvā kṣutvā ca bhuktvā ca pītvāpo vai munis tathā |

	ācāntaḥ punar ācāmen niṣṭhīvyoktvānṛtaṃ vacaḥ || iti |

evam abhisaṃbandho 'tra kartavyaḥ: ācānto bhuktvāpunar ācāmet | yatra punar dvir ācāmed iti paṭhyate tatrānantaryeṇaikakriyāvṛttiḥ || 5.143 ||

	**eṣa śaucavidhiḥ kṛtsno dravyaśuddhis tathaiva ca |**

**	ukto vaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ strīṇāṃ dharmān nibodhata || 5.144 ||**

ādyena padatrayeṇa śuddhiprakaraṇopasaṃhāraś caturthena vakṣyamāṇasaṃkṣepavacanam | **śaucavidhi**śabdaḥ sāmānyaśabdo 'pi dravyaśuddhisaṃnidhānād gobalīvardavad itaraviśeṣaparaḥ saṃpadyate | **strīṇāṃ dharmā** asādhāraṇastrīkartṛkā eva | yas tu sādhāraṇo yāgādiḥ sa iha nocyate || 5.144 ||

	**bālayā vā yuvatyā vā vṛddhayā vāpi yoṣitā |**

**	na svātantryeṇa kartavyaṃ kiṃcit kāryaṃ gṛheṣv api || 5.145 ||**

**svātantryaṃ** strīṣu kasyāṃcid avasthāyāṃ nāstīty upadeśārthaḥ | vayovibhāgavacanaṃ tu yatrāsyāḥ pārtantryaṃ tatpradarśanārtham avivakṣitasvarūpam || 5.145|

	**bālye putur vaśe tiṣṭhet pāṇigrāhasya yauvane |**

**	putrāṇāṃ bhartari prete na bhajet strī svatantratām || 5.146 ||**

tathā coktam:

	tatsapiṇḍeṣu vā satsu pitṛpakṣe prabhuḥ striyāḥ |

	pakṣadvayāvasāne tu rājā bhartā striyā mataḥ ||

tatsapiṇeṣv ityādinā cāsati svāmini kartavyam || 5.146 ||

**	pitrā bhartrā sutair vāpi necched viraham ātmanaḥ |**

**	eṣām hi viraheṇa strī garhye kuryād ubhe kule || 5.147 ||**

avyavasthānaṃ vacanīyatāhetuḥ kathito **garhye kuryād** iti | **eṣāṃ hi viraheṇa** nivasantī gacchantī vā grāmāntaram ity adhyāhāryam || 5.147 ||

	**sadā prahṛṣṭayā bhāvyaṃ gṛhakārye ca dakṣayā |**

**	susaṃskṛtopaskarayā vyaye cāmuktahastayā || 5.148 ||**

ābhikṣṇavacanaḥ **sadā**śabdo nityaśabdavat | nityaprahasitayā[^276] iti | saty apy anyatra krodhaśokavege bhartur darśane mukhaprasādasmitanarmavacanādinā praharṣo darśanīyaḥ | kumāryā bhartṛmatyāś cāyam upadeśaḥ | **gṛhakārye ca dakṣayā** | arthasaṃgrahavyayayoḥ dharmkārye snānādau ca | "arthasya saṃgrahe cainām" (MDh 9.11) ityādinā gṛhakāryam uktam | tatra **dakṣayā** caturayā bhavitavyam | atra saṃskārādi śīghraṃ niṣpādyam | **susaṃskṛtopaskarayā** | upaskaraṃ gṛhopayogi bhāṇḍaṃ kuṇḍaghaṭikādi, tat susaṃskṛtaṃ susaṃmṛṣṭaṃ śobhāvat kartavyam | **vyaye ca** mitrajñātyātithyabhojanārthe dhane **amuktahastayā** udārayā na bhavitavyam | na bahuvyayitavyam ity arthaḥ | susaṃskṛtāny upaskarāṇi yasyā iti bahuvrīhiḥ | evaṃ mukto hasto yasyā iti vigrahaḥ | paścān nañsamāsaḥ | rūḍhyā udāravacano muktahastaśabdaḥ || 5.148 ||

	**yasmai dadyāt pitā tv enāṃ bhrātā vānumate pituḥ |**

**	taṃ śuśrūṣeta jīvantaṃ saṃsthitaṃ ca na laṅghayet || 5.149 ||**

**bhrātā vānumate pituḥ** | yathaiva pitrānujñātasya bhrātur dātṛtvam, evaṃ pitur nirapekṣasyāpi dātṛtvaśrutau bhāryāyā anumate sati dānaṃ boddhavyam | sarvatra sahādhikārād ubhayoś ca duhitari svāmyāt | asati pitari mātrāpi deyeti navame darśitam | mātrāpitror apatyaṃ tannimittaṃ ca svāmyam iti yuktā itaretarāpekṣā | **śuśrūṣeta** ārādhayet | **saṃsthitaṃ ca** mṛtaṃ ca, **na laṅghayet** | laṅghanam atikramaṇam | na svātantryeṇāsītety arthaḥ | yathā jīvati bhartari tatparavatī evaṃ mṛte 'pi tadaiva tatparatantrayā bhavitavyam | yata āha: "pradānaṃ svāmyakārakam[^277]" (MDh 5.150) | yadaiva pitrā dattā tadaiva pituḥ svāmyaṃ nivartate. yasmai dīyate tasyotpadyate | ataś ca na vivāhakāla eva dānaṃ prāg api vivāhād varaṇakāle asti dānaṃ || 5.149 ||

_kimarthas tarhi vivāhaḥ |_

	**maṅgalārthaṃ svastyayanaṃ yajñaś cāsāṃ prajāpateḥ |**

**	prayujyate vivāhe tu pradānaṃ svāmyakāraṇam || 5.150 ||**

abhilaṣitārthaniṣpattir **maṅgalam,** tatsādhanaṃ tad**arthaṃ** prayujyate | tatra **prajāpater yajñaḥ** iti kriyāviśeṣaṇatvān napuṃsakam | svasti īyate prāpyate yena tat **svastyayanam** | yad asya priyaṃ vastu vidyate tan na naśyatīty arthaḥ | **āsāṃ** strīṇām | teṣu vivāheṣu | **yajñaḥ prajāpater**[^278] devatāyāḥ kriyate "prajāpate na tvad etāni" (RV 10.121.10) iti vivāhe ājyahomāḥ keṣāṃcid āmnātāḥ | upalakṣaṇaṃ caitad anyāsām api devatānāṃ pūṣavaruṇāryamṇām | tathāhi tatra mantravarṇāḥ | "pūṣaṇaṃ nu devam, varuṇaṃ nu devam" (ĀśG 1.7.13) ityādayo devatāntaraprakāśanaparāḥ | pradānād evāsaty api vivāhe svāmyam utpadyata ity etad atra jñāpyate | vivāhayajñas tu maṅgalārtha ityādy avivakṣitam | dārakaraṇaṃ vivāha iti smaryate | saty api svāmye naivāntareṇa vivāhaṃ bhāryā bhavatīti || 5.150 ||

	**anṛtāv ṛtukāle ca mantrasaṃskārakṛt patiḥ |**

**	sukhasya nityaṃ dāteha paraloke ca yoṣitaḥ || 5.151 ||**

"sarvatraiva pratiṣiddhavarjam"[^279] (GDh 5.2) iti **anṛtāv** api **sukhasya dātā** | mantrasaṃskāro vivāhavidhis tasya kartā **mantrasaṃskārakṛt** | **paraloke ca** | patyā saha dharme 'dhikārāc ca tatphalāvāpteḥ paralokasukhasya dātety ucyate || 5.151 ||

	**viśīlaḥ kāmavṛtto vā guṇair vā parivarjitaḥ |**

**	upacāryaḥ striyā sādhvyā satataṃ devavat patiḥ || 5.152 ||**

dyūtātisakto **viśīlaḥ** | kāmapradhānaṃ vṛttam asyeti **kāmavṛttaḥ** | **guṇair vā parivarjitaḥ** | śrutadhanādiguṇavihīnaḥ | **upacāryaḥ** ārādhanīyaḥ || 5.152 ||

	**nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthag yajño na vrataṃ nāpy upoṣitam |**

**	patiṃ śuśrūṣate yena tena svarge mahīyate || 5.153 ||**

bhartrā vinā kṛtānāṃ yajñādhikāro nāstity etad asakṛt pratipāditam | tena vratopavāsāv api kurvatī tadanujñāṃ gṛhṇīyāt | **vrataṃ** madyamāṃsādinivṛttisaṃkalpaḥ, na tu kṛcchāṇi | tatra japahomayor aṅgatvāt tadabhāvāc ca striyāḥ | na ca vaktuṃ yuktam "japahomavikalaṃ kṛcchrānuṣṭhānam asyā bhaviṣyati" | na hi svecchayāṅgatyāgo yuktaḥ | sarvāṅgakalpayuktasya karmaṇo 'bhyudayasādhanatvenāvagatatvāt | na hi puruṣaśaktibhedāpekṣayāṅgānām upacayāpacayau bhavataḥ | santi ca sarvāṅgopasaṃhāreṇa savarṇās traivarṇikāḥ prayogam anuṣṭhātum | ato na striśūdrasyābhyudayakāmasya kṛcchreṣv adhikāraḥ | prāyaścitteṣu viśeṣaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ | **upoṣitam** upavāsaḥ āhāraviccheda ekarātradvirātrādiṣu | **śuśrūṣate** paricarati || 5.153 ||

	**pāṇigrāhasya sādhvī strī jīvato vā mṛtasya vā |**

**	patilokam abhipsantī nācaret kiṃcid apriyam || 5.154 ||**

patyur lokaḥ patyā saha dharmānuṣṭhānena yo 'rjitaḥ svargādiḥ sa **patilokaḥ**, tam **abhīpsantī** prāptukāmā **nācaret kiṃcid apriyaṃ** parapuruṣasaṃsargādi śāstrapratiṣiddham | na hi mṛtasya kiṃ priyam apriyaṃ cāśakyam avasātum | na ca jīvato yat priyaṃ tad eva mṛtasya, bhavāntaropapannānāṃ tu prītibhedāt | tasmād yat pratiṣiddhaṃ svātantryaṃ tad evāpriyam | tan nācaret || 5.154 ||

	**kāmaṃ tu kṣapayed dehaṃ puṣpamūlaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ |**

**	na tu nāmāpi gṛhṇīyāt patyau prete parasya tu || 5.155 ||**

tad eva saviśeṣaṃ darśayati | puṃvat strīṇām api pratiṣiddha ātmatyāgaḥ | yad apy āṅgirase "patim anumriyeran" ity uktam, tad api nityavad avaśyaṃ kartavyam | phalastutis tatrāsti | phalakāmāyāś cādhikāre śyenatulyatā | tathaiva "śyenena hiṃsyād bhūtāni" ity adhikārasyātipravṛddhataradveṣāndhatayā satyām api pravṛttau na dharmatvam | evam ihāpy atipravṛddhaphalābhilāṣāyāḥ saty api pratiṣedhe tadatikrameṇa maraṇe pravṛttyupapatter na śāstrīyatvam | ato 'sty eva patim anumaraṇe 'pi striyāḥ pratiṣedhaḥ | kiṃ ca "tasmād u ha na purāyuṣaḥ preyāt" (ŚB 10.2.6.7) iti pratyakṣaśrutivirodhe[^280] 'yaṃ smṛtir apy eṣā śakyate kalpayitum | yathā "vedam adhītya snāyāt" (BauG 2.5.6) ity adhyayanānantaram akṛtārthāvabodhasya snānasmaraṇam | ato mṛtapatikāyā anapatyāyā asati bhartṛdhanādau dāyike ca kartanādinā ca kenacid upāyena jīvantyā jīvitasyātipriyatvāt tadupekṣaṇasyāśāstratvāt pratiṣiddhatvād āpadi sarvavyabhicārāṇāṃ "viśvāmitrajāghanīm" ityādinānujñātatvād vyabhicāropajīvitāprāptāv idam ucyate | **kāmam** asyām avasthāyāṃ **śarīraṃ kṣapayet** kṣayaṃ nayet **puṣpamūlaphalair** yathopapādaṃ vṛttiṃ vidadhīta | **na tu nāmāpi gṛhṇīyāt** patir me tvam evādyety anyasya | yat tu,

	naṣṭe mṛte pravrajite klībe 'tha patite patau |

	pañcasv āpatsu nārīṇāṃ patir anyo vidhīyate || iti | (NSm 12.97)

tatra pālanāt patim anyam āśrayeta, sairandhrakarmādinātmavṛttyartham | navame ca nipuṇaṃ nirṇeṣyate | proṣitabhartṛkāyāś ca sa vidhiḥ | kāmaśabdaprayogo 'rucisaṃsūcanārtham | dehakṣapaṇam apy akāryam idaṃ tv anyad akāryataraṃ yad anyena puruṣeṇa saṃproyogaḥ || 5.155 ||

	**āsītāmaraṇāt kṣāntā niyatā brahmacāriṇī |**

**	yo dharma ekapatnīnāṃ kāṃkṣantī tam anuttamam || 5.156 ||**

eṣa evārtho vispaṣṭīkriyate | **ā maraṇād brahmacāriṇy āsīta** | asyām āpadi na vyabhicāreṇātmānaṃ jīvayet | **kṣāntā** | tatkṛtaṃ duḥkham avadhīrayantī | na brahmacaryaṃ kṣudutkṛtaṃ yena cittaṃ kallolena khaṇḍayet | ekaḥ patir yāsāṃ tāḥ, ekasya vā patnya **ekapatnyaḥ**, tāsāṃ sāvitrīprabhṛtīnāṃ **yo dharmo** yasya phalaṃ varadānābhiśāpādiṣu śaktatā. **taṃ kāṃkṣantī** kāmayamānā brahmacaryaṃ na jahyāt | asyām avasthāyāṃ mūlaphalāśinyā yadi bhavati maraṇaṃ tato na doṣaḥ || 5.156 ||

	**anekāni sahasrāṇi kumārabrahmacāriṇām |**

**	divaṃ gatāni viprāṇām akṛtvā kulasaṃtatim || 5.157 ||**

pūrveṇāpadi jīvikārthaḥ parapuruṣasaṃsargo niṣiddho 'nena putrārthā pravṛttir niṣidhyate | evaṃ kila śrūyate "nāputrasya loko 'sti" (AitB 33.1) iti | liṅgaṃ ca tatrāvivakṣitam ataḥ putrārthe prasaṅga idam ucyate | bahūni **sahasrāṇi** **kumārā** eva **brahmacāriṇo** 'kṛtadārā naiṣṭhikās teṣām **anekāni sahasrāṇi** **divaṃ gatāni** svargaṃ prāpnuvanti | niyogas tu navame (MDh 9.59) gurvicchayā[^281] vihitaḥ, nātmatantratayā putrārthinyāḥ | akṛtvā kulasaṃtatiṃ kulavṛddhyarthā saṃtatis tām akṛtvā putrān ajanayitvety arthaḥ | **anekānīti** nañsamāsasyottarapadārthaprādhānyena bahuvacanaṃ cintyam | saty apy ekatvapratiṣedhe dvyādisaṃkhyāvacanaṃ durlabham | tathā hy ayaṃ svadharmāveśena parityaktasvagatikatvenācchāditatadrūpo 'py atidīrghasaṃkhyāviśeṣān ācaṣṭe | yathā modo grāma iti | uktaṃ ca cūrṇikākāreṇa "anekasmād iti sidhyati" iti | ekavacanaprayogaśiṣṭisiddhiḥ darśitavān | asahāyavacano vāyam anekaśabdaḥ | asahāyāni gatāni, bhāryā sahāyabhūtā eṣāṃ nāsīd ity arthaḥ || 5.157 ||

	**mṛte bhartari sādhvī strī brahmacarye vyavasthitā |**

**	svargaṃ gacchaty aputrāpi yathā te brahmacāriṇaḥ || 5.158 ||**

eṣa evārtho bhūya ucyate pratipattidārḍhyārtham || 5.158 ||

	**apatyalobhād yā tu strī bhartāram ativartate |**

**	seha nindām avāpnoti paralokāc ca hīyate || 5.159 ||**

putro me jāyatām ity abhilāṣaḥ | so **'patyalobhaḥ**, tato hetor **yā bhartāram** **ati**kramya **vartate** 'nyena saṃprayujyeta | **sā iha** loke **nindāṃ** garhāṃ prāpnoti svargaṃ na prāpnoti || 5.159 ||

	**nānyotpannā prajāstīha na cānyasya parigrahe |**

**	na dvitīyaś ca sādhvīnāṃ kvacid bhartopadiśyate || 5.160 ||**

anyena bhartrā yā utpāditā **prajā** sā naiva tasyāḥ prajā | anyadāreṣu ca yā puṃsotpāditā sāpi tasya na bhavati || 5.160 ||

	**patiṃ hitvāvakṛṣṭaṃ svam utkṛṣṭaṃ yā niṣevate |**

**	nindyaiva sā bhavel loke parapūrveti cocyate || 5.161 ||**

_na kevalaṃ nindām eva yena, _

	**vyabhicāre tu bhartuḥ strī loke prāpnoti nindyatām |**

**	śṛgālayoniṃ prāpnoti pāparogaiś ca pīḍyate || 5.162 ||**

ato nāticared bhartāraṃ dṛṣṭādṛṣṭaphalalobena || 5.162|

**	patiṃ yā nābhicarati manovāgdehasaṃyatā |**

**	sā bhartṛlokam āpnoti sadbhiḥ sādhvīti cocyate || 5.163 ||**

**	anena nārī vṛttena manovāgdehasaṃyatā |**

**	ihāgryāṃ kīrtim āpnoti patilokaṃ paratra ca || 5.164 ||**

strīdharmopasaṃhāraślokā ṛjavaś ca strīdharmā ity ato mayātra vyākhyānādaraḥ kṛtaḥ | etāvat tatropadeśārthaḥ | yathā puṃso 'nyayā saha punaḥpravṛttikarma neha “saṃsthitaṃ ca na laṅghayet" (MDh 5.149) ity anena nyāyena punaḥ sahapravṛttir iti, tathā "svargaṃ gacchaty aputrāpi" (MDh 5.158) ity anenāpatyajananam āpadi pratiṣidhyate — niyogasmṛtyā tu tat punar abhyanujñāsyate — tad etad apatyotpādanam uktapratiṣiddhatvād vikalpyate | anayos tu smṛtyoḥ katamā smṛtir jyāyasīti na śakyaṃ kartum atiśayāvadhāraṇaṃ yenaikatrāpatyam anyatrāsyāḥ saṃyamaḥ | ubhayor api vastu nirvahati || 5.163–164 ||

**	evaṃ vṛttāṃ savarṇāṃ strīṃ dvijātiḥ pūrvamāriṇīm |**

**	dāhayed agnihotreṇa yajñapātraiś ca dharmavit || 5.165 ||**

nyāyaprāptāptānuvādaḥ ślokaḥ | evaṃ tasyāḥ sādhvītyādyukta evātrāgnihotiṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ | "na vāgnayo ha vā ete patnyāṃ pramītāyāṃ dhāryante" iti || 5.165 ||

	**bhāryāyai pūrvamāriṇyai datvāgnīn antyakarmaṇi |**

**	punar dārakriyāṃ kuryāt punar ādhānam eva ca || 5.166 ||**

tad etat punar adhikārārtham udāhriyate | idam apy anyayā sahādhikārapratiprasavaḥ | yadā tv arthe prayojane dharmakarmānuṣṭḥāne vā tadāpy asahāyabhāvād vānaprathe[^282] pārivrājye vādhikārasyāpratiṣedhaḥ | tathā ca śrutiḥ "jarasā ha vā etasmād vimucyate" iti | arthalopena vā | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">apare tv</span> āhuḥ | atra "yadā" iti kalpayiṣyate | etena yāvajjīvahomīyaśruter avirodhaḥ siddho bhaviṣyati || 5.166 ||

	**anena vidhinā nityaṃ pañcayajñān na hāpayet |**

**	dvitīyam āyuṣo bhāgaṃ kṛtadāro gṛhe vaset || 5.167 ||**

upasaṃhāraślokaḥ | **pañcayajña**grahaṇaṃ ca sarvaprasiddhyartham iti || 5.167 ||

**iti mānave dharmaśāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ **

**pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ ||**

**iti śrībhaṭṭavīrasvāmisūnor bhaṭṭamedhātithisvāminaḥ kṛtau**

**manubhāṣye pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ samāptaḥ ||**

[^242]:
     M G: candragopa-; This may be the Buddhist author Candragomin who is said to have authored a large number of texts, according to Tāranātha: "in all he composed four hundred and thirty-two separate works, of which ... one hundred and eight were treatises on secular knowledge" including "fine arts, grammar, logic, medicine, prosody, dramaturgy, dictionary, poetics, astronomy, etc." (trans. Chimpa & Chattopadhyaya, pp. 206-7). Possibly Medhātithi is noting that he did not want to follow the example of Candragomin to be too prolix.
